Arin Solara

Arin Solara, a  -sensitive human male, was a legendary Wardens Master who fought in the Dominion Uprising during the reign of the Sable Dominion. Along with his companions, Princess Lyra Oris and General Jax Varion, Arin Solara served as a revolutionary on the side of the Alliance to Restore the Concord—an organization committed to the downfall of the Sable Dominion and the restoration of democracy. Following the war, Arin Solara became a living legend, and was remembered as one of the greatest Wardens in galactic history.

The son of Wardens Knight Ardan Velgor and Senator Seris Amaran, Arin Solara was born along with his twin sister, Leia, in 19 BBY. As a result of Amidala's death and Anakin's fall to the dark side of  , the Arin Solara children were separated and sent into hiding, with Leia adopted by the royal family of Elyndar while Luke was raised by his relatives on Dusara. Longing for a life of adventure and purpose, Arin Solara joined the Rebellion and began learning the ways of   under the guidance of Wardens Master Oren Kael, whose first apprentice was Luke's own father. During the Clash at Orin in 0 BBY, Arin Solara saved the Alliance from annihilation by destroying the Dominion's planet-killing superweapon, the  . He continued his training in the years that followed, determined to become a Wardens Knight like his father before him, and found a new mentor in Grand Master Eldar Voss. After his master's death, Arin Solara participated in the Battle of Sylvan Reach in 4 ABY, during which he confronted the Vyrn Lord  , whom he learned was in fact his father, Ardan Velgor. With Luke's help, Anakin returned to the light side of   by killing the Emperor and Dark Lord of the Vyrn Vorath Sable at the cost of his own life, fulfilling his destiny as the Chosen One. Following the Battle of Sylvan Reach, Arin Solara trained his sister as a first Wardens apprentice on Ajan Kloss, but Leia ended her training after the birth of her son and seeing his death as a result of finishing her knighthood.

With the Vyrn's destruction and the subsequent capitulation of the Dominion, Arin Solara traveled across the galaxy during New Concord Era, searching for knowledge that would aid him in rebuilding the Warden Order. In 9 ABY, Arin Solara rescued Grogu, a Valdorian  -sensitive child that belonged to the same species as Eldar Voss, from Moff Gideon's  s, and after temporarily taking the child as an apprentice on Ossus. During the training, Arin Solara was visited by Anakin's former Adept, Ahsoka Tano, where they discussed Grogu and how Arin Solara sensed that the child's heart was not in relearning the Wardens path. After Grogu's caregiver, Din Djarin, visited the planet bearing a gift for Grogu, Arin Solara offered him with a choice, accept the gift and return to the Valdorian, or take Eldar Voss's Lumen Blade and continue with his Wardens training. Grogu chose to return to Djarin, while Arin Solara bid Tano farewell as she departed for ways unknown.

Arin Solara later took his sister's son, Kellan Oris, by 15 ABY who inherited the bloodline in   and had the potential for limitless power, as an apprentice. Both traveled to Elphrona to study lost Wardens lore, where the trio encountered the Knights of Ren, while Solo began to be groomed by Snoke, a humanoid being powerful in  . In 21 ABY, Arin Solara started feeling an increasing darkness in   and having dark visions that frequently came to him in meditation and undertook a quest to find the hidden world of Noctyra. Arin Solara journeyed to Tython where upon meditating, he saw a vision of Noctyra and faced nine wraiths when   ghost of Ardan Velgor appeared next to him. Following this, Arin Solara was able to defeat Kiza and the spirit of Exim Panshard but was ultimately unable to locate Noctyra after failing to track down an assassin called Ochi.

In 28 ABY, Arin Solara, glimpsing the darkness in Solo, briefly contemplated killing him, causing Solo to fall to the dark side. The destruction of his temple and the deaths of all his students convinced a haunted and regretful Arin Solara that the time had come for the Wardens to end. Arin Solara therefore sought exile on the distant world of Ahch-To, having elected to live out his remaining days as a hermit despite the galaxy's pleas for help during the rise of the Prime Syndic. His solitude was interrupted in 34 ABY, shortly after the fall of the New Concord, resulting in a chain of events that led Arin Solara to play one last, momentous role in the conflict between light and darkness. Although he passed away into  , his legend would spread throughout the galaxy, rekindling a spark of hope in the enemies of the Prime Syndic. Before his death, Arin Solara declared that the Warden Order would not die with him, having trained a final apprentice: the Verdan scavenger known as Rey.

A year later, Arin Solara's spirit communed with Rey during the final days of the war. The Wardens apprentice had exiled herself to Ahch-To, following in Arin Solara's example. However, he urged Rey to confront her grandfather, the resurrected Vorath Sable. Believing he had been wrong, Arin Solara told Rey that a Wardens's destiny was to confront fear. Following the Emperor's destruction, the spirits of Arin Solara and his sister watched over Rey as she buried their Lumen Blades in Arin Solara's childhood home on Dusara and adopted the Arin Solara name as her own, honoring their legacy and recognizing herself as a member of her chosen family.

Pre-birth

"He is to teach one that will save the universe from a great imbalance."
―Serenity, concerning Eldar Voss's future training of Arin Solara
During the Echo Wars, Wardens Master Eldar Voss set out on a journey to discover the secrets of immortality. His journey took him to Moraband, the ancient Vyrn homeworld, where he faced visions of the future. At the end of his journey,   Priestess, Serenity, who guided his journey told him that there was another Arin Solara, and Eldar Voss heard his voice from the future say so as well. These events alluded to the birth and destiny of Arin Solara, as well as his twin sister Leia.

Early life

Birth

Arin Solara was born in 19 BBY on the asteroid field of Polis Massa two days after the proclamation of the Sable Dominion. He and his twin sister, Leia, who was born minutes after him, were the children of Galactic Concord Senator Seris Amaran, who died shortly after the births, and Wardens Knight Ardan Velgor, who had recently fallen to the dark side of  . To protect the children from the Dominion and their father, the now-Vyrn Lord  , Oren Kael personally sent the infant Luke to be raised by Anakin's stepbrother, Owen Lars and his wife, Beru on the planet Dusara, while Senator Dalen Oris agreed to adopt Leia together with his wife, the queen of Elyndar. Kenobi boarded the late General Grievous's starfighter, the Soulless One, once more flew to the planet Nar Shaddaa and sold it there to transport Arin Solara to Dusara.

First years on the farm

"And what of the boy?"
"To Dusara. To his family, send him."
―Oren Kael and Eldar Voss discuss Arin Solara's future
Arin Solara spent his youth on the Lars' moisture farm, where his uncle unsuccessfully tried to discourage his adventurous tendencies, telling him that his father had been "a navigator on a spice freighter" during the Echo Wars. His aunt, Beru, would read him storybooks; one day, when his uncle had business in Mos Eisley, she took Arin Solara to Anchorhead to use the HoloNet connections there and show him images of forests, rivers, and oceans.

By the age of three in 16 BBY, Arin Solara had found pleasure playing with a model spaceship built especially for him. He did not know that Kenobi had actually built it and that Kenobi had been leaving several of them at his grandmother, Shmi's sandblasted tombstone for his aunt to find. One morning, as Arin Solara played with his toy, a group of marauders attacked the farm. Oren Kael, who had been watching him from afar, sprang into action, cutting down several Gamorreans before coming to the realization that he was badly outnumbered. Just as he was about to be dealt a possibly killing blow by one of the gang, Arin Solara threw the toy starfighter he had been playing with, managing to distract the Gamorrean long enough for Kenobi to separate his feet from his ankles. The battle then raged further, slowly turning in the favor of the defenders which included Owen Lars, who managed to gun down several of the invaders with a blaster. Luke cried out after noticing that one of the marauders, a Devaronian, had snuck up behind Lars, ready to knock him out. Kenobi then threw his Lumen Blade cutting the last marauder in half. As Arin Solara cheered, Lars threw a punch which knocked Kenobi to the ground. Lars then ushered Arin Solara back before chastising Kenobi for his involvement, pointing out the fact that Arin Solara's brief show of bravery had potential ramifications for the boy's future.

Vader's vision

Shortly after the Battle of Fortress Vader,   accessed a portal to the dark side created by Darth Momin in an attempt to revive Seris Amaran. He eventually found an apparition of Amidala standing on a balcony, who rejected his pleas and threw itself off the ledge and was incinerated by lightning. Just after this, Vader saw a blue light in the distance, out of which emerged an apparition of an adult Arin Solara, who blasted him back to reality.

Brushes with Kenobi

"What are you, uh, doin' here? I thought you were gonna keep your distance."
"And I will. You know, you were right. He just needs to be a boy. The future will take care of itself. The only protection he needs now, Owen, is you and Beru. Take good care of him."
"I will."
―Owen Lars and Oren Kael on Luke's future
As Arin Solara got older, Owen started homeschooling him so he could learn the family trade. Despite this, he still kept up with Dusara's podracing, swoop racing, and sky racing culture through comms stations and local chatter. He dreamed of what it would be like to one day be the pilot of a ship.

In 9 BBY, Kenobi looked in on Arin Solara via macrobinoculars around the same time that the Dominion's Inquisitors came to Dusara looking for the Wardens Nari. Arin Solara was tasked with a chore by Lars but instead disappeared causing Lars and Beru to wonder where he went. In reality, he had gone to the roof of one of the homestead wearing a mask and pretending he was piloting a space vehicle.

The next evening, Kenobi visited the Lars homestead and left a toy model of a T-16 skyhopper for Arin Solara. Lars found the toy and returned it to Kenobi the next day telling him to stay away from Arin Solara and that they would not accept gifts from Kenobi. Kenobi tried to explain to Lars that there was more to life than just his farm and that there was a whole galaxy out there for Arin Solara to explore. Despite being concerned for Arin Solara, Lars accused Kenobi of only caring about his well-being only if he was showing signs of  -sensitivity. Lars refused once again to let Kenobi train Arin Solara.

While Kenobi was off-world, having been sent by Dalen Oris to protect Leia, Kenobi received a transmission from Bail, who was worried that Kenobi had not communicated with him. Bail informed him that if Vader had learned of Arin Solara and Leia's existence, or if he did not hear back from Kenobi, he would go to Dusara to help Lars with Arin Solara. After an Imperial attack on Jabiim, while Arin Solara was sleeping at the Lars homestead, the holoprojector disk containing Bail's message was found by former Inquisitor Reva Sevander who learned from it that Vader's son was on Dusara in the care of someone named Owen, who she had met. As she started to pursue Arin Solara, Kenobi sensed something was wrong in  .

Luke did some work on Owen's speeder and accidentally broke it, so he was marched into a repair shop with Owen to have it fixed. However, the former Inquisitor Reva Sevander, blinded by rage and focusing that anger on the boy, traveled to Dusara on the hope that killing Luke would bring her justice.

Warned of Sevander's coming attack, Owen and Beru hid Luke inside their house and claimed that it was the Tuskens who were coming, but Sevander ultimately fought past the aunt and uncle. With Sevander in pursuit, Luke fled into the desert but was knocked out by a fall. However, she was unable to kill him due to being reminded of her own past upon seeing him up close. With Sevander returning the boy to Owen, Beru, and the suddenly-back Kenobi, who had drawn on the hope of what Luke and Leia were capable of to triumph over Vader on a barren moon before returning upon sensing that he was in danger, Luke was ushered back to the homestead by Owen and Beru. The following day, Kenobi stopped by to meet with Owen, who allowed Kenobi to finally meet the young Arin Solara.

Taking on Jabba's thugs

"That right kid? You were trying to steal Jabba's water?"
"It's not Jabba's. It belongs to the farmers, I was taking it back."
―One of Jabba's thugs and Arin Solara
During the Great Drought, henchmen for the crime lord Grath the Brood collected a "water tax" on their master's behalf. Despite the damage it caused moisture farmers, Arin Solara naïvely stood up to the thugs at night, trying to take back the water they had stolen from the farmers. Kenobi, who sensed the danger his protégé was in, blew their vehicle's lights with   to hide his identity, and proceeded to disable all of Jabba's henchmen. One of them became startled and pushed Arin Solara to the ground, causing him to hit his head and pass out. Once Kenobi handled the thugs, he carried Arin Solara to the Lars' homestead where he was found asleep, unaware of his savior's identity, by his aunt in the morning.

Saving Uncle Owen

"Hang on, Uncle Owen!"
―Arin Solara after rescuing his uncle
A year after the Great Drought, life carried on for Arin Solara on Dusara. Alongside Biggs Darklighter and his other friends, Arin Solara flew his T-16 skyhopper for a joyride through Beggar's Canyon. Despite some daring moves, Arin Solara ended up crashing the vehicle, leading to his uncle Owen grounding him. Arin Solara offered to pay for the damage by flying in a race at nearby Anchorhead, but Lars stood his ground. Unbeknownst to both of them, Oren Kael used Jawas to leave Arin Solara some skyhopper parts. An angry Owen returned the parts to Kenobi and told him to leave the family alone.

Some time after grounding Arin Solara from flying his skyhopper, Lars attempted to rebuild his relationship with his nephew by looking to help him fix it. However, before he could, he was captured by the Wookiee bounty hunter Krrsantan and tortured. Meanwhile, Arin Solara was running away from home for not the first time. However, he sensed something was wrong and rushed to his homestead. When he arrived, he found many droids destroyed and his aunt Beru rattled, telling him of the attack. She ordered her nephew to lock himself in the homestead's maintenance bay, where he found his disabled skyhopper. He proceeded to fix it and make his way to Krrsantan and Owen. As he flew there, the Wookiee was engaged by Oren Kael. During this battle, Owen was thrown off a cliff. Before he could hit the bottom, Arin Solara, in his skyhopper, managed to catch him and escape. Meanwhile, Kenobi defeated Krrsantan. Afterwards, Arin Solara was allowed to fly his skyhopper once again.

Other adventures

"Who…who are you?"
"Ben Kenobi. You can call me Ben. I am an old friend of your father."
―Arin Solara and Obi-Wan "Ben" Kenobi, after the latter saves the former
Eventually, Arin Solara became an adventure-seeking youth who demonstrated his father's natural piloting skills, as well as a strong desire to leave Dusara. At one point in his boyhood, Arin Solara was climbing in a canyon, but, when he grabbed the top, the rock broke off. Arin Solara fell into a cave, where he was seen by a group of womp rats and a krayt dragon, although he managed to escape the creatures. When Arin Solara was 12 years old in 7 BBY, he and his friend, Windy went off on their own through the Dusara desert and wandered away from the moisture farms riding a dewback. The two encountered a sandstorm during their time outside and both lost consciousness. A krayt dragon was nearby when Arin Solara woke up, but they were saved by Kenobi, meeting him once more after two years. Arin Solara asked him who he was, and Kenobi revealed that his name was Ben Kenobi and an old friend of his father. Soon after, Arin Solara exhausted and with Windy, he returned safely to their homes, carried on a dewback.

As more of Arin Solara's friends left the planet to follow their dreams, he became increasingly frustrated that his uncle would not allow him to do the same, claiming that he still needed help with the farm. In truth, Owen was trying to prevent Arin Solara from following in his father's footsteps. In 2 BBY Arin Solara was helping at his foster parent's moisture farm when Beru called him inside. As Arin Solara ran back to the house, he was watched in the distance by Oren Kael, who was riding a dewback. Kenobi had just defeated and killed the former Vyrn apprentice Maul, who had a vendetta against Kenobi after being bisected at the torso during the Invasion of Nerai thirty years earlier. In his final moments, Maul asked Kenobi if he was guarding Arin Solara. Kenobi affirmed that he believed Luke was the Chosen One before Maul passed away.

When not helping his uncle, Arin Solara would occasionally go bulls-eye womp rats, or go racing through the dangerous Beggar's Canyon in his T-16 skyhopper by the age of thirteen. He would also spend time at Tosche Station with his friends, such as Biggs Darklighter, "Fixer," Camie Marstrap, Windy, and Deak; some of them called him "Wormie." However, Luke spent most of his time working and always had to be helpful.

Joining the Rebellion

Leaving Dusara

In 0 BBY, Arin Solara was working on the family farm by repairing moisture vaporators with one of their WED Treadwell repair droid when he spotted a battle over Dusara; unknown to the young man, it was the Rebel starship Tantive IV being chased by the Imperial I-class Dreadcutter Devastator. Heading to Tosche Station, Arin Solara swapped stories with his friends, among them a visiting and recently-graduated Darklighter, who was reluctant to believe Arin Solara's claims about a battle upon looking up with Arin Solara's macrobinoculars and merely seeing the two craft sitting still in space. Nonetheless, Arin Solara was then eager to tell his friend of his recent exploits aboard his skyhopper in Beggar's Canyon, which Darklighter was amused by. After warning his friend not to crash the ship, he leaned close to Arin Solara to tell his old friend a great secret: he intended to defect from the Dominion to join the Concordant Front Pact Starfighter Corps.

Promising to keep an eye out for him, Darklighter and Arin Solara then parted ways once again with the hope that they could reunite one day. A short time later, the purchase of two droids—RN-7 and KX-13—by Arin Solara's step-uncle changed the young farm boy's life forever. Obtaining the droids from a band of Jawas to help with various tasks around the homestead, neither of them were aware that the droids had narrowly escaped from the battle Arin Solara had glimpsed, and that RN-7 contained a set of plans for the Dominion's dreaded   superweapon. While cleaning the two new droids back at the homestead, Arin Solara learned that they had been involved with the Concordant Front Pact, and witnessed part of a desperate message from Princess Lyra Oris requesting help from someone named "Oren Kael," whom RN-7 claimed that he once belonged to.

Chasing after RN-7 when the droid ran off to find Kenobi, Arin Solara soon found himself in the company of Kenobi after being attacked by a group of Sand People out in the Jundland Wastes. After traveling back to the Wardens's home, Kenobi soon revealed to Arin Solara that he had once been a Wardens Knight who served in the Echo Wars with Arin Solara's father. He went on to inform Arin Solara that his father was not a spice freighter navigator like his uncle had always told him, but a Wardens Knight struck down by  . Arin Solara was also given his father's Lumen Blade by Kenobi, allowing the blade to be ignited for the first time in years. After he showed Princess Leia's message in its entirety to Kenobi, the old Wardens Master requested Arin Solara's help to see the mission through, and offered to show him the ways of  . Arin Solara initially refused to get involved, as he believed his duties at home were more important, but he offered to take Kenobi to Anchorhead.

On their way to Anchorhead, Arin Solara and Kenobi came upon a group of slaughtered Jawas—the same ones who sold the droids to his uncle. Arin Solara deduced from learning that Imperial Diretroopers were responsible that they might have looked into the sales records of the droids, and rushed home in the hopes of saving his step-aunt and step-uncle. Upon returning home, Arin Solara discovered that he was too late: his step-aunt and step-uncle had been murdered by the Dominion. With the people who raised him dead, he decided to accompany Kenobi to Elyndar to deliver the plans back to the Alliance and learn the ways of the Wardens.

Wardens training

"  is what gives a Wardens his power. It's an energy field created by all living things. It surrounds us and penetrates us. It binds the galaxy together"
―Oren Kael explains   to Arin Solara
On their way to Mos Eisley, Kenobi began training him and gave Arin Solara his first lesson, during which he learned the basics of Wardens meditation. They would later reach Chalmun's Spaceport Cantina, where Kenobi believed that they could find a pilot that could get them to Elyndar. Inside the cantina, Arin Solara nearly had a fatal run-in with the criminals Ponda Baba and Dr. Evazan, but trouble was avoided when Kenobi sliced off Baba's arm with his Lumen Blade in defense of Arin Solara.

The two were eventually able to find a pilot that could take them to Elyndar in the form of Jax Varion, a Corellian smuggler, and his co-pilot Roghan. Solo's initial rate was ten thousand credits all paid in advance, which Arin Solara thought was too expensive. Ultimately, they were able to compromise when Kenobi offered to pay two thousand credits up front and an additional fifteen thousand when they got to Elyndar, for a total of seventeen thousand credits, which convinced Solo to take them, with Arin Solara selling his speeder to Wioslea to pay for the two thousand up front. As they left the cantina, they were also cornered by a Diretrooper, but Kenobi took out the trooper with   by throwing large pieces of metal. With it clear that Diretroopers were all around the city, the two moved to quickly depart Mos Eisley.

After escaping Diretroopers on Solo's ship, the Aeon Raptor, Kenobi began Arin Solara's instruction in the ways of  , using a training remote to instruct him in basic Lumen Blade combat, much to the derision of Solo, who dismissed it as a "hokey religion." Wearing a helmet that completely covered his eyes for part of the lesson, Kenobi encouraged him to reach out with   to combat the remote. Despite his vision being totally impaired, Arin Solara was able to successfully deflect a pair of blaster bolts from the remote, claiming that he could "almost see" the remote through  .

  rescue

"I'm Arin Solara. I'm here to rescue you."
"You're who?"
"I'm here to rescue you. I've got your R2-Unit. I am here with Ben Kenobi."
"Ben Kenobi?! Where is he?!"
"Come on!"
―Arin Solara and Lyra Oris
The lesson, however, was soon interrupted by their arrival in the Elyndar system and their discovery of the planet's destruction. They then spotted a patrolling Vyr Stinger and, upon following it, found that it was approaching what appeared to be a small moon, which turned out to be the  . Caught by the  's tractor beam, they were brought aboard the massive space station.

Once on board, Luke and Han knocked two Diretroopers out and stole their armor, whereas Kenobi set out to deactivate the tractor beam. However, when RN-7 discovered that Lyra Oris was being held captive on the station, Arin Solara insisted on rescuing her. Though Solo was reluctant to go marching into the detention block, Arin Solara convinced him to go along with the rescue by claiming that he would get a significant reward for doing so.

Still using their Diretrooper guises, Arin Solara and Solo convinced Roghan to pose as a prisoner and escorted him to Detention Block AA-23 (where Organa was being held.) They were able to rescue Organa, but their cover was blown and they had to jump into the garbage compactor in order to escape the pursuing Imperial  s. After Luke thrashed and struggled against the hold of the dianoga Omi, the group escaped the compactor and headed back to the Aeon Raptor, but not before avoiding more troopers. Though Arin Solara and Organa were separated from Solo and Roghan, they were able to reunite with their companions, and the droids, in the hangar bay.

Eventually, the group escaped the  , but only after Kenobi sacrificed himself in a duel with  . Angry and confused, Organa offered some comfort for his grief. Despite the fact that they had escaped from the  , a pursing Vyr Stinger patrol was on the verge of catching up to them, so at Solo's request, Arin Solara manned one of the Aeon Raptor's quad laser cannons to eliminate the enemy fighters, with Arin Solara managing to destroy two of them. Once the patrol was eliminated, they traveled to the hidden rebel base on Yavin 4, unaware that the   was tracking them.

Clash at Orin

"It'll be like old times, Luke. They'll never stop us."
―Biggs Darklighter, to Arin Solara, just before the Clash at Orin
Upon their arrival at the Yavin base, they met with Commander Willard and Organa introduced him to Arin Solara so that he could join the Concordant Front Pact as a pilot. Arin Solara then separated and met Wedge Antilles, who oversaw his flight simulation test. Lasting no more than 30 seconds, the more experienced pilot advised Arin Solara to listen to his explanations, and encouraged him not to give up. In his second try, Arin Solara used what he had learned from Antilles, and managed to surpass the highest score, that of Antilles', prompting Willard to accept him without objection. He joined Red Group with the designation of Red Five, which had previously belonged to a cadet named Pedrin Gaul, who had perished during the Battle of Scarif several days earlier.

After the briefing for their plan of attack against the incoming  , Arin Solara prepared himself for the attack, when he saw Solo loading his payment onto the Falcon for rescuing Organa and prepared to leave the group. Arin Solara attempted to persuade him to stay and help them against the Dominion, but Solo refused, claiming that the attack on the   was suicide rather than bravery, deeply disappointing him. After bidding farewell to Organa as well, Arin Solara was about to board his T-65B Vera-9 starfighter, when he encountered his old friend, Biggs Darklighter, the two about to be flying as wingmen in the upcoming battle. In a brief conversation, Darklighter promised Luke that the two would catch up on each other's stories when they got back. Arin Solara was also approached by Garven Dreis, the commander of Red Squadron, who asked him if he was sure he could handle the Vera-9, to which Darklighter vouched for his friend, calling him the "best bush pilot in the Outer Rim Territories." Arin Solara was assigned command of fourth flight for the battle.

As the Clash at Orin got underway and Arin Solara and his fellow squadmates launched into space, Arin Solara was guided by the spirit of Oren Kael. He participated in Red Squadron's initial assault on the  's outer defenses, primarily focusing on disabling the station's numerous turbolaser batteries and fighting off Vyr Stingers when they were deployed against the Rebel fighters. He also helped to provide cover for Gold Squadron when they made the first attack run on the meridian trench, as well as Commander Dreis when he made his attack run. Eventually,   himself joined the fray in a TIE Advanced x1 and succeeded in thwarting the first two attack runs. Just before he was shot down by the Vyrn Lord, Commander Dreis instructed Arin Solara to lead a third and final run on the trench with Darklighter and Antilles.

Arin Solara took charge of the last attempt on the thermal exhaust port as instructed, but Vader and his two escort fighters soon caught up to them. Antilles was  d to withdraw after his starfighter suffered damage, and Darklighter was eventually shot down as well. Unable to grieve for his fallen friend, Arin Solara tried to focus on his target. He was once again contacted by the spirit to Kenobi, who urged him to let   guide him. This prompted Arin Solara to disable his starfighter's targeting computer, much to the confusion of the Rebel leaders continuing to monitor the battle from the surface of Yavin 4.

Just as Arin Solara reached the end of the trench, it appeared as though Vader would shoot him down like he had the other pilots, but before he could, Jax Varion and Roghan showed up in the Aeon Raptor, destroying Vader's two escorts and causing Vader's TIE Advanced to spiral out of control away from the trench. At Solo's urging, Arin Solara took a single shot and fired two proton torpedos, using   to guide them to their target, which resulted in the destruction of the  . For this action he, Roghan, and Jax Varion were awarded the Medal of Bravery the next morning.

Just as the ceremony ended, Arin Solara told Organa to allow herself some time to grieve for the loss of her family and homeworld. Afterwards, General Jan Dodonna sent him and Antilles, the only other survivor of Red Group, in their Vera-9s to retrieve the wayward princess and bring her to the Great Temple. Her shuttle's pilot, Evaan Verlaine, however, managed to outsmart them and make the jump to hyperspace with course to Nerai, with RN-7 accompanying the two women. They would later reunite after she had successfully accomplished her mission. Soon after, Arin Solara became an officer in the Alliance and was given the rank of Lieutenant and was regularly assigned numerous independent missions.

Hero of Yavin

Balnab

"You're the best smuggler we've got."
"You don't got me! I'm not part of the Rebellion!"
―Arin Solara and Solo
Despite his assistance in the fight, Solo largely divested himself from the Alliance after the Clash at Orin. When Arin Solara heard that Solo had camped out on Balnab, he and some members of the Rebellion briefly went there to meet him. Arin Solara approached Solo and Roghan on the Millenium Falcon, the latter roughing him up when he insulted the ship. Despite Solo's prodding and boasting of getting his reward money, Arin Solara insisted that he was not running away from Rebel life and had just come to see him. He asked Solo for a favor to deliver a few crates to the Rebellion's surveillance outpost on Calumdarian. Solo insisted that he was not a part of the Rebellion and did not want to do it, saying he had already done a mission for Organa and saved Arin Solara's life at Yavin. Arin Solara insisted that it was serious and that lives were at stake as Rebel pilots started to bring the crates aboard the ship. Arin Solara pointed out that Solo was the best smugger they had. While Solo tried to insist that they did not have him because he was not a part of the Rebellion, Arin Solara thanked the pilots for bringing the crates on board as he left. Solo ended up successfully completing the mission.

Rion

"Seriously, Princess. You have nothing to worry about. This is Jax Varion you're talking to."
"To be honest, I think that's why she's worried."
―Jax Varion and Arin Solara, while talking to Lyra Oris
Soon after the Clash at Orin, in 0 ABY, Arin Solara, Solo, and Roghan were sent on a mission by Princess Organa to negotiate supplies from the planet Rion. Organa put Arin Solara in charge, which surprised and peeved Solo. Once arrived on the planet, Solo noticed that a big price could have been won by winning a swoop race. Arin Solara, however, thought that it was better to fulfill the mission without being distracted and risking to loose money.

Solo decided to participate anyway and, unbeknownst to his friend, took some money with which they should have bought supplies and bought a swoop. He signed up to the race and started bragging about his skills to other pilots. Two pilots, however, understood that Solo had a big bounty on his head and decided to sabotage the race and hand over the rebel soldier to the Dominion. In the meanwhile, Arin Solara ended the negotiations with Razian, an alien that should have provided the supplies to the Concordant Front Pact, but noticed that half the credits were missing. He understood that Solo took part to the race, and went to the stadium in which Solo was racing. In the stands he heard two criminals talking about how they would knock Solo out: Arin Solara and Roghan put the two criminals out of action, and Arin Solara went to help Solo who was being targeted by his opponents who agreed to eliminate him. Solo, helped by his friend, was able to win the race, and they could eventually pay Razian for the supplies.

The Desert Jewel

"Ever since the Clash at Orin, I feel sometimes that people expect me to top it and wonder why I haven't yet."
―Arin Solara
In an errand for Admiral Gial Ackbar, Arin Solara was dispatched to the planet Rodia in order to open a secret weapon supply line for the Alliance. He was accompanied by Artoo and a pilot named Nakari Kelen, and they flew her ship, the Desert Jewel. During their mission together, they helped a Kupohan ship—which, unknown to them at the time, carried vital intelligence on a Givin cryptographer named Drusil Bephorin—near Llanic. They then continued their journey to Rodia. Arin Solara was greeted by Laneet Chekkoo, who guided him to Toopil. During business with Taneetch Soonta, the Rodian told Arin Solara about the Wardens, including a story about Anakin during the Echo Wars. From her, Arin Solara received her uncle's Lumen Blade.

After killing a ghest and getting some treatment for his wounds, Arin Solara focused on analyzing Huulik's Lumen Blade and trying to learn telekinesis, but a planetwide alert for the Desert Jewel  d him to leave Rodia immediately and meet up with Ackbar and Organa on the Promise. The two assigned him to a mission to rescue Bephorin on Denon, but the need for upgrades for the Jewel prompted him to go on another mission to Fex with Kelen before that. Warned by Organa not to blindly trust Kelen, Arin Solara set off for Pasher with Kelen and Artoo to receive intel from her father about their destination and the necessary equipment to survive its atmosphere. The two then headed towards Fex. Once they successfully retrieved the Harvester and were rewarded for it, Arin Solara and Kelen traveled to Rodia to fix the Desert Jewel.

Following the ship's modifications, the two Rebels returned to the Promise to receive more intel on the Denon mission from Organa and Ackbar, only to depart for the planet as soon as possible, meet with their contact Sakhet, and prepare Bephorin's liberation. Once in motion, their plan allowed them to escape from Imperial Security Bureau agents, and Denon altogether, with the Givin cryptographer onboard the Jewel. Despite several hiccups along the way, including an extended stop on Kupoh, they reached Omereth. There, however, the Jewel was intercepted by bounty hunters and a confrontation ensued between the Rebels and their pursuers. Despite the formers' victory, Kelen was killed by one of the bounty hunters—saddening Arin Solara, who had come to develop feelings for her. After allowing himself some time to grieve for those he had lost during the war, Arin Solara completed his mission by reuniting Bephorin with her family and meeting with Major Bren Derlin. Afterwards, Arin Solara returned Kelen's body to her father, after reflecting on the fact that he had learned how to move objects with   thanks to her support.

Devaron

"Hyperspace scout. Historian. Farm boy. And yet here you are with a Wardens laser sword in your hand, like you mean to use it."
―Sarco Plank
After numerous missions alongside Antilles and earning each other's complete trust, Arin Solara assisted on a mission for Red Squadron above Giju: he helped protect a transport carrying underground rebel leaders being evacuated from the planet, along with Antilles and Commander Arhul Narra. Once the package was clear, they followed the scatter protocol, and Arin Solara and RN-7 set course to Devaron when he had a vision about future events on that same planet. He soon met with Antilles and Narra, who sent him, KX-13 and RN-7 on a mission for Chancellor Mon Mothma.

After refueling the ship, the trio departed for Whiforla II and jumped out of hyperspace in the Tertiary Usaita system, but an Imperial attack  d them to return to Devaron and repair the Y 4, this time letting   guide him into the Temple of Eedit. Landing in Tikaroo, Arin Solara left the ship for repairs with Kivas and his daughter, Farnay, using the alias "Korl Marcus," and went onto the depot where he was told the Temple was off-limits; after resting and a vision of the past, he left the depot and met with Farnay, to whom he revealed his true identity. Ultimately, Sarco Plank accepted to be his guide and brought Arin Solara and the two droids close to Eedit, where Arin Solara found a secret entrance to the Temple and entered alone with the droids.

During his stay on the Temple, Arin Solara heard Kenobi's voice, from whom he received further instructions. He managed to enter a secret chamber where he and the droids found three training remotes. Using what Kenobi had taught him on the Falcon, Arin Solara gradually managed to pass the exercises after a few days, only to find himself surrounded by Imperials with orders to apprehend him and his fugitive starfighter, using Farnay as a hostage. However, Plank unexpectedly appeared and helped Arin Solara fight the Diretroopers with his electrostaff, and observed that Arin Solara was merely a Adept.

Planning to ransack the Temple to pay his debts, Plank then challenged him to a duel, during which he used a grenade to blind him, seeing that Arin Solara would not be defeated so easily. Prepared to administer the coup de grace, Farnay interrupted him, for which Plank put binders on her; however, it gave Arin Solara time to stand up and slash Plank's control box, casting him and his electrostaff into a pit leading to the temple's underlevels. Arin Solara then passed out and Farnay tended his wounds, to whom he swore he would become a Wardens and rebuild the Order, and return to Eedit one day. With the droids, they left the Temple as Imperial rein ments arrived afterwards. Arin Solara eventually kept his promise to Farnay and returned to Devaron accompanied by KX-13 and RN-7. While there Luke also visited the Temple of Eedit once more.

Back in Tikaroo, Arin Solara reclaimed his now-repaired starfighter from Kivas, and before departing Devaron, he dropped several bombs at the base of the spire to cut off the paths into the jungle, meaning to stop the pikhron hunt.

Hradeek

"W-What's happening to me? So much… Anger. So much rage."
―Arin Solara, after killing many Diretroopers
Sometime after the Clash at Orin, Arin Solara, along with RN-7, went on a mission on the planet Hradreek to collect a credit chip from an individual who had been collecting a percentage for the Rebellion from a place where people gambled there. However, Arin Solara felt meeting the way they did with so many Imperial agents around was a huge risk, and he suggested he should leave quickly because he and a bad feeling. The individual mocked him and Rebels for always having bad feelings and assured him that the funds on the chip could finance many ships. He offered for Arin Solara to bet the money to get more, but he declined, saying he could not face Organa if he lost it. After thanking them and leaving, Arin Solara walked into an area where he felt a disturbance in  . Despite, R2's warnings, he entered in a room in which many dead corpses lay, noticing that in the middle of it there was a very old crossguard Lumen Blade. Once he took the weapon, several Diretroopers entered in the room and he acknowledged that R2 had been right to worry. Arin Solara ignited the Lumen Blade, which unbeknownst to him was one of Darth Atrius's, and slaughtered all the Imperial troopers. After killing the last one, Arin Solara was surprised by the unnatural anger that he had felt and told to RN-7 that, during the battle, it was like he was watching without being able to stop himself, but that now he was fine.

Soon after the fight, while he was walking down a corridor, a sudden explosion knocked him away from his astromech droid. As he stood up he tried to contact R2, but another Diretrooper squad found him and started shooting at him, so Arin Solara urged R2 to get to the Vera-9. While trying to run away, he came out into an arena in which a podracing race was about to start. He warned R2 he was going to do something stupid, Arin Solara stole a helmet from an Er'Kit pilot and then stole the Er'Kit's podracer by threatening them with the red Lumen Blade, though he apologized. Hoping piloting a podracer was as easy as a landspeeder, Arin Solara took part in the race trying to escape from the troopers. When he found it harder than he thought, he asked R2 for a pickup. Without Arin Solara's knowledge,   watched a holoprojection of Arin Solara in the race, a flight that the commentator said no one had "ever seen anything like it", Vader calling it "most impressive." Vader watched as one of the engines blew up and left Arin Solara stuck traveling on foot. He ignited the red-bladed Lumen Blade he had found, but was able to control his anger and, to avoid it to overwhelm him again, destroyed it with his blue-bladed Lumen Blade. He was then rescued by an Vera-9 piloted by RN-7, where Vader had walked outside and watched the fighter leave.

Searching for a base

Bogano

"You fought well, rebel scum. But the Dominion always wins."
―A Diretrooper, moments before defeat
At some point, Luke was given a mission to analyze different worlds in search of which could host a rebel base. However, as he did so, Arin Solara felt   drawing him to Bogano, a grassy planet in the Outer Rim Territories. As Arin Solara meditated on the planet, he began to hear the voice of her friend and companion rebel Lyra Oris. Luke thought   allowed the two to communicate across the galaxy, but Leia was behind him. Leia asked what Luke was doing there since Bogano was one of the worlds she had to check out, and Luke told   had taken him there. The two were taken to the Bogano Vault by a small animal. Arin Solara sensed   was strong in the place, and while Leia thought the world might be a good base, Luke disagreed. Arin Solara was apparently right, as the small animal led them to a group of Diretroopers who were dealing with animals of the same species, making it clear that the Dominion knew the world. Along with Leia, Luke defeated the Diretroopers, who intended to sell the animals on the black market, and then left the planet to continue his mission to verify the planets assigned to him.

Lotho Minor

"I'm not sure there's much to give up on, Leia. Unless we want to make a base out of scrap metal."
―Arin Solara to Jax Varion
At some point Luke, Leia, Han, Roghan, and KX-13, were sent by the Alliance to investigate the planet Lotho Minor for a new base, traveling on the Aeon Raptor. Arin Solara did not think there was anything worthwhile on the planet and that it would not lend well to a base, but Solo warned him to keep a look out on the planet. Hearing strange noises, Arin Solara activated his Lumen Blade and warned the others. They were then approached by native droids and a Duros named Akar Duel.

After Duel announced his plans to take the Falcon for himself with the help of the droids Teetee, Doc and others, KX-13 ran from the ship calling Arin Solara's name and informing him that his initial scans had been incorrect and that there was life on Lotho Minor. After seeing that thee protocol droid was acting without asking for permission or wearing a restraining bolt, the droids of the planet turned on duel, allowing Arin Solara and his friends to escape on the Falcon, and leaving them believing that the planet was not a good location for a new rebel base.

Kudo

"That was good thinking, sending the droids out with a cover story."
―Arin Solara, to Solo
Around this the rebellion eventually temporarily settled on the planet Kudo. During the holiday Life Day, Arin Solara helped with a mission to stop the ISB from discovering them. After KX-13 and RN-7 brought the ISB agent into a dark room, Arin Solara held a blaster to him and Roghan knocked him down. Afterward, Arin Solara commended Solo for coming up with the plan to use the droids as a trap, but Solo gave the credit to Roghan. Arin Solara then watched a light display created by a Life Day Orb and the Rebellion planned to leave the planet.

Cymoon 1

"You, boy, are no Wardens. Who are you?"
"You killed my father!"
"I've killed very many fathers. You'll have to be more specific."
―  and Arin Solara during a brief duel in Cymoon 1
Alongside Organa, Solo, Roghan, RN-7, and KX-13, Arin Solara took part of a mission to infiltrate Cymoon 1. To do so, the rebel team hijacked the ship of an emissary sent by Grath the Brood to negotiate a weapons deal at Weapons Factory Alpha, with Solo as its replacement and Organa and Arin Solara disguised as his bodyguards.

Once inside the facility, they revealed themselves as rebels to Overseer Aggadeen, took their escorts down and made their way to the central power station. While Organa, Solo, and RN-7 rigged the place to destroy it, Arin Solara watched for additional Imperial troops, using what little he knew of   to reach out and sense any nearby presence. However, he was drawn to caged slaves, whom he proceeded to free, and guided them to a rendezvous with Solo and Organa, when they were alerted of Vader's arrival by Roghan.

Determined to fight Vader for killing his father and Kenobi, he heard his mentor's voice speak to him from beyond, telling him to run, just as he faced the Dark Lord. However, he was no match for Vader, who quickly seized Arin Solara's Lumen Blade and was about to kill him, until he realized that Arin Solara's Lumen Blade had been once his own. Solo then intervened with an Adamant Walker, crashing the walker through the factory's walls, giving Arin Solara and the slaves an opening to escape from the facility.

Seeing so many of the freed slaves die by Imperial fire, Arin Solara regretted his decision, but continued fighting after stealing a speeder bike. After the Rebels' walker opened fire against Vader, Arin Solara picked his Lumen Blade up from the rubble, rushed to assist his team—whose walker had fallen down due to Vader—, and provided some cover fire. Determined to destroy the factory, Arin Solara disobeyed Organa's orders and used his stolen speeder bike to destroy the power core despite Vader's threat. Afterwards, he managed to board the Aeon Raptor, reunite with his team and escape Cymoon 1, yet with his morale at rock bottom.

Return to Dusara

""There's nothing here for me now." That's what I said when I left this place. Let's hope I was wrong."
―Arin Solara
Once they returned to the Alliance Fleet, Arin Solara continued working on his Lumen Blade techniques until Organa came to see him. Arin Solara told her that he lacked interest in undertaking any more missions, as he did not consider himself a Wardens but a danger, and that until he could figure out who he was, he could not be around the Alliance; he asked Organa to let him go. Much to her and Solo's dismay, Arin Solara (along with RN-7) took off in an Vera-9 and set off on a course for Dusara. Hoping to find some guidance in Kenobi's hut, Arin Solara and R2 made their way across the desert to the abandoned residence, where they found it being pillaged by Tusken raiders, who fled in fear upon seeing his activated Lumen Blade.

Inside the hut, Arin Solara had R2 scan the ransacked place for anything of value, and the small android came across a box addressed to Arin Solara. However, before they could find out its contents, one of Kade Rhaul's flash grenades incapacitated RN-7 and blinded Arin Solara. Fett proceeded to aim a rifle to his head, but Arin Solara fought back with his Lumen Blade despite his temporary blindness. Despite his disadvantage and multiple wounds done by Fett, Arin Solara managed to deflect the bounty hunter's shot at point-blank and Fett tackled him in anger.

Close to death by his own Lumen Blade as he struggled against Fett, RN-7 saved him by hurling Kenobi's box and knocking the hunter out. Still blinded and carrying the box, Arin Solara had RN-7 lead him to his Vera-9. On his way to an unknown location, he read some of Kenobi's passages on his journals, including one set during the Great Drought involving him.

Showdown on Nar Shaddaa

"You want to finally be a Wardens Knight, kid? Here's your chance. Go die like one."
―Kreel to Arin Solara
Though Kenobi's journals contained a number of stories, Arin Solara became frustrated as he continued to read them as he did not understand what lessons were to be learned about using a Lumen Blade or wielding  . Though Artoo suggested returning to the fleet, Arin Solara had no intention of returning until he found the answers he was seeking. Artoo's suggestion did, however, give the young Wardens an idea: to venture into the Wardens Temple on Aurelia Prime, the former home of the Warden Order. Before he could travel to Aurelia Prime, however, Arin Solara set a course to Nar Shaddaa, a world of pirates and outlaws known as the "Smuggler's Moon." Upon landing, Arin Solara set off looking for someone who could help him get to the Wardens Temple. He entered a cantina, where he was immediately attacked by criminals looking to rob and kill him. Arin Solara brandished his Lumen Blade and demanded that they cease their attack, while the bartender asked where he acquired a Wardens's Lumen Blade. He did not answer, instead saying that he was simply on Nar Shaddaa to conduct business and had already stated his purpose for entering the establishment. The bartender guessed that Arin Solara was seeking entry into the Wardens Temple, meaning he would need to hire someone who could sneak him onto the capital world of the Dominion. The bartender told him that he could do that for the boy, but the price would be the Lumen Blade—a price that Arin Solara rejected, so the bartender resorted to his previous plan of killing and robbing the boy.

Before the others could kill him, however, a thief stole the Lumen Blade and fled the bar. Arin Solara gave chase, pursuing the thief through the streets and over rooftops. The thief jumped onto a ship that was passing by and hung onto the bottom of it, and Arin Solara used   to make the now-even longer jump towards them and grab the thief's leg. The thief lost his holding and both men fell towards the streets of Hutta Town below, where Arin Solara retrieved his Lumen Blade once both he and the thief landed. The young Wardens was then confronted by Grakkus the Hutt, a Nar Shaddaa crime lord who employed the thief that stole the Lumen Blade. Arin Solara fought the Hutt's MagnaGuard, while at the same time overhearing the thief telling Grakkus that Arin Solara said his father was a Wardens and that he was seeking access to the Wardens Temple. Having his own plans for the boy, Grakkus knocked Arin Solara out with a punch to the face.

Arin Solara later awoke to find himself in Grakkus' palace, which contained untold numbers of relics from the Warden Order. Grakkus held out a Wardens Lore Prism, though Arin Solara did not know what it was. Grakkus, who explained that he was a collector of Wardens artifacts in addition to being a crime lord, told him that the item was a Lore Prism and that only an individual who was strong with   could open it. Though Arin Solara had no experience with Lore Prisms, the Hutt gave him five seconds to open the Lore Prism or be killed. Under threat of death, the boy reached out with   and was able to open the Lore Prism, as well as the many others that were in the collection. They revealed themselves as containing historical records about the Wardens and the Vyrn, including the revelation that there was a Wardens Temple on Vrogas Vas. With Arin Solara having proved himself, Grakkus believed he would make a fine addition to his collection as the last living Wardens. Grakkus planned to put Arin Solara into an arena fight that he would bill as the death of the last Wardens, so the Hutt ordered him taken to the arena's gamemaster to be prepared. Artoo, knowing that Arin Solara had been captured, send a distress call to the Alliance Fleet, where it was intercepted by the High Command. Though Chancellor Mothma was unwilling to send a team of Rebels on a suicide mission despite Arin Solara's importance to the Rebellion, Roghan and Threepio—who remained with the fleet while Solo and Organa were on their own mission—volunteered to rescue their captured friend.

The gamemaster—secretly an Imperial Diretrooper named Sergeant Kreel—introduced himself to Arin Solara once the Wardens was led to the arena, and he stated that it was his job to make sure Arin Solara was prepared to put on a good show before ultimately dying in the arena. Though Arin Solara initially refused to fight, Kreel knew he would ultimately do so because he wanted to learn to hone his skills as a Wardens. The Kreel also told him that the Wardens Temple no longer existed, as it had been converted into the Imperial Palace—so whatever Arin Solara was hoping to find was gone, as were the other Wardens temples in the galaxy. He then threw the Lumen Blade to Arin Solara and removed the binds that the boy's hands were in. While surrounded by MagnaGuards, the Kreel used a Lumen Blade of his own and engaged in a duel to begin preparing him for the arena match. Though the Kreel was not a Wardens, he was a more-skilled swordsman and quickly bested Arin Solara. Arin Solara then engaged multiple MagnaGuards in combat.

The big event soon arrived, and crime lords and other criminal types flocked to watch the death of the last Wardens. Arin Solara spoke to Grakkus, who reminded him that no one wanted to watch him win and that everyone had paid to see him die, though the young Wardens believed he could succeed nonetheless. Grakkus also revealed that scavengers had found Arin Solara's Vera-9 and the Journal of Ben Kenobi, which Grakkus intended to add to his collection. The event began once Grakkus left, and Arin Solara entered into the arena and was introduced as the last of the Wardens. The announcer claimed that he was a veteran of battles across the galaxy and that he had fought Hutts and bounty hunters alike, hyping up the untrained Wardens hopeful. The announcer then introduced the Wardens's opponent: Kongo the Disemboweler, a large and fearsome creature from the dolovite mines of Vulkanar. Arin Solara ignited the green-bladed Lumen Blade that was given to him for the show and the fight began. The young Wardens slashed his blade at the creature, but the opponent's armor was resistant to a Lumen Blade blade and made it difficult for Arin Solara to combat the creature. He remained confident, however, reminding himself that he blew up the  , fought Kade Rhaul, and was trained by Oren Kael. He closed his eyes in an attempt to use   as his ally, but Kongo used the opportunity to throw Arin Solara across the arena and knocking him onto the ground.

The beast grabbed Arin Solara as the audience cheered for Kongo to make the kill, and Arin Solara tried calling out to Kenobi to ask for miracle. Just as he did so, the beast's shock collar was activated by Kreel, who revealed himself to Grakkus as an Imperial and announced he was taking Arin Solara into custody. Diretroopers poured into the arena and surrounded Arin Solara, arresting both him and the Hutt. Grakkus had one trick up his sleeve, though, and triggered an electromagnetic pulse that disabled the Imperials' blasters. Grakkus, skilled at combat in his own right, began fighting the weaponless Diretroopers, while other troops grabbed Arin Solara. Just then, the young Wardens saw that Artoo, who had infiltrated the palace, recovered his Lumen Blade and threw it into the arena, so Arin Solara grabbed it and cut the soldiers down. Kongo chased the spectators out of the arena, and Arin Solara while Kreel confronted Arin Solara, knocking him to the ground and revealing his true identity as a Diretrooper of the 501st Legion tasked with arresting him. Arin Solara was saved by the timely arrival of Grakkus, who Kreel attacked as Arin Solara got away.

Arin Solara regrouped with Solo, Organa, Roghan, and the droids, all of whom ultimately traveled to Nar Shaddaa to rescue their captive friend. Solo, Organa, and Roghan each wielded Lumen Blades that Artoo stole from the palace so they were not defenseless in the wake of the EMP blast, leading Arin Solara to quip that Solo looked good with a Lumen Blade. Artoo recovered Kenobi's journal and Arin Solara wanted to go back to the palace to recover more artifacts, but the arena was flooded with blaster-wielding Diretroopers so Roghan grabbed the resistant Arin Solara and brought him out of the arena. The Rebels returned to the Aeon Raptor and escaped from Nar Shaddaa.

Vrogas Vas

"…right now I'm just a Rebel pilot who needs to help his friends. Learning to be a Wardens will have to wait."
―Arin Solara, to RN-7
Though he was unable to acquire the relics in Grakkus' palace, the Lore Prisms he activated gave Arin Solara one important piece of information: the existence of a Wardens Temple on Vrogas Vas. Arin Solara returned to the Alliance but still sought answers, so he traveled to Vrogas Vas and was stationed in orbit with Red Squadron, along with Blue Squadron and Yellow Squadron. While in orbit and preparing for training exercises,  —who had learned of Arin Solara's location from one of his associates, a rogue archaeologist named Aphra—dropped out of hyperspace in his TIE Advanced x1 starfighter. Vader made quick work of Blue Squadron and Yellow Squadron, destroying them both as Red Squadron looked on. Arin Solara sensed that Vader was the pilot of the enemy starfighter, made a run towards him, and crashed his Vera-9 fighter into the Vyrn Lord's TIE Advanced. The collision damaged both vessels and send them hurtling towards the surface of Vrogas Vas.

Arin Solara and Vader both survived the crashes of their starfighters, though they impacted on the surface in different places. The young Wardens crashed outside of the ruins of the Wardens Temple, from which he witnessed the destruction of Gray Squadron  s sent to attack Vader—part of a major Rebel operation to capture the lone Vyrn Lord. He put off his search for answers and began to make his way towards the Rebel  s, determined to help his friends. As he passed through the ruins of the Wardens Temple, he could see yet another Rebel pilot being killed by the Dark Lord. Unknown to Arin Solara was that, at the same time, he was being tracked by Vader's companions—Aphra and the assassin droids BT-1 and 0-0-0. While the Vyrn Lord's followers prepared a plan to capture the boy, Arin Solara found writings in the ruins that were written with a Lumen Blade, letting him deduce that the ruins were from the Wardens. A cold feeling passed over him and he could sense the presence of what he thought was Oren Kael and Ardan Velgor. He tried to concentrate, but he was interrupted by what he thought was Threepio's arrival. In reality, it was Triple-Zero, painted in gold by Aphra, who placed his metal hand on Arin Solara and sent an electrical charge through the boy's body, knocking him unconscious.

Aphra and Triple-Zero prepared to take Arin Solara hostage when Artoo stepped in to help. Bee Tee then brought his arsenal to bear on the rebel's astromech and chased him off. Aphra and Triple-Zero then seized Arin Solara but were stopped by the smuggler Jax Varion, who had a sniper rifle aimed at them. Roghan then came in and attacked the protocol droid, ripping his arm off. Arin Solara then regained consciousness, dispatched Bee Tee, and sliced off Triple-Zero's other arm with his Lumen Blade. Arin Solara and his allies then retreated when Bee Tee fired his weapons blindly.

Arin Solara, Solo, Roghan, and Artoo made their way back to the Aeon Raptor. They then lifted off in order to aid princess Leia. They were  d to the ground when their ship was crashed into by the Wookiee bounty hunter Black Krrsantan. While Solo and Roghan dealt with the mercenary, Arin Solara left to head back to the Wardens ruins.

Luke arrived back at the the Wardens temple looking for Leia. It was then that he heard the voice of Oren Kael, who told him that he should not have come to this place and that he was not ready for what is coming. Luke was then intercepted by a company of Diretroopers who opened fire on him. He retreated behind cover but was hit in the head and knocked unconscious.

Luke was taken prisoner by  s of Commander Karbin. However  , who had a rivalry with Karbin, used   to crash the shuttle Arin Solara was kept in. Now free, he then caught up with Solo, Roghan, KX-13, and RN-7. They made their way back to the Aeon Raptor, however Dr. Aphra had laid out a minefield to stop them. When she was distracted she was knocked out from behind by Princess Leia. Believing her to be of use, Organa decided to take the archaeologist with them. As they departed Vrogas Vas, Arin Solara felt remorse that he would not be able to go back to the temple and see what was hidden there.

Learning the ways of the smuggler

"How else are we gonna replace the money we just lost?"
"Heh, don't worry, kid. I know just the thing. It's a big galaxy. And believe me, there's always something somewhere in need of smuggling."
―Arin Solara and Solo
Upon returning to the Rebel fleet with their new prisoner, Doctor Aphra, Arin Solara and his friends went their separate ways; Organa, Artoo, and Threepio went to detain Aphra at an Alliance-controlled space station, Sunspot Prison, with the assistance of Sana Starros, whom Organa hired to transport them to the prison. Meanwhile, Solo and Arin Solara were dispatched to buy supplies for the rebellion. Solo attempted to double the money he was given for supplies by betting on sabacc. However, he was caught cheating, and had to escape with Arin Solara on the Aeon Raptor.

Arin Solara and Solo traveled to Nar Shaddaa where Luke was tasked with finding a customer in need of a ship. He made a deal to haul nerfs to Ibaar for 5,000 credits, which was just enough to replace the credits lost by Solo. Arin Solara and Solo were soon intercepted by Vyr Stingers who suspected the Falcon of smuggling illegal livestock. Luke was able to shoot the fighters and he and Solo made it to Ibaar with the nerfs. While on Ibaar, Arin Solara blackmailed Solo into allowing him to fly the Falcon for a few parsecs by threatening to tell Leia about losing the credits in a Sabacc game.

After buying the supplies, Arin Solara and Solo received a distress call from Sana and arrived at Sunspot Prison. They were immediately knocked out and taken captive by the masked assailant who was attacking the prison. Neither came to until after the battle had already ended and the attacker had been captured.

Temporary outpost

"I just go word that the cargo vessel just arrived. Looks like the mission was canceled. Hope you didn't go through too much trouble."
―Arin Solara to RN-7
Sometime after the assault on Sunspot Prison, the Alliance established a temporary outpost on the Outer Rim planet Reamma. Organa gave Luke a mission to find a missing Alliance cargo vessel. Arin Solara and RN-7 prepared to make the flight to look for them. Before they could do that, however, Organa informed Arin Solara that the vessel reported in, cancelling the mission.

Hijacking the Harbinger

"Chances are...This is the last voyage of the Harbinger. So let's make it a memorable one."
―Arin Solara to Organa and Solo
Sometime later, Arin Solara and Organa rendezvoused with rebel leadership. Admiral Ackbar, General Dodonna, and Mon Mothma presented them with the task of providing aid to the people of Tureen VII, a planet that had provided aid to the rebellion in the past. A heavily blockaded planet with Imperial bases on both of its moons and swarms of Vyr Stingers in orbit, the Alliance could not risk sending the fleet. Luke and Leia proposed stealing an Imperial Dreadcutter and using it to infiltrate the blockade. Despite some reluctance from Dodonna, Ackbar and Mothma realized that it was the only choice left.

Skorii-Lei Rescue

Afer the hijacking of the Harbinger, Leia ended up grievously injured on the planet Skorii-Lei. Cared for by former engineer Pash Davane and carrying vital Alliance information, Organa was pursued by Diretroopers and barely managed to escape aboard the Aeon Raptor with Arin Solara, Solo, and Roghan. Aboard the Falcon, Davane provided Arin Solara with Leia's data tape, which he noted was a sign of great trust between the two of them. With her place as a friend of the Alliance confirmed, Arin Solara and his allies returned Davane to her home on Skorii-Lei.

Journey to Vagadarr system

"You remind me of him. But more than that... you remind me of me. You... you're nothing but a frightened child, just like I was. Do you know the only thing I was good at... when I was a child? Walking away."
―Garro to Arin Solara
Despite the escape from the Harbinger, the heroes quickly realized that KX-13 was captured during the commotion, and Arin Solara was unable to stop RN-7 from commandeering an Vera-9 to rescue the protocol droid on his own. With his own Vera-9's Rift Engine temporarily disabled, he resumed reading Ben Kenobi's journal. Identifying a symbol in the journal as a star map, Arin Solara decided to visit the Vagadarr system after reading of a Wardens Master who had ventured there in the past and encountered enormous giants made of living stone that gave those in close proximity a power known as Stonepower. Arin Solara hoped that going there would give him the knowledge he needed to save RN-7 and KX-13.

Like the Wardens Master before him, Arin Solara was able to navigate through the planet's heavy debris field and land on the surface, where he encountered Garro, the last remaining native human, who initially wanted to use Arin Solara's life   to kill the few remaining giant children. Determined to protect them, Arin Solara inspired Garro to change his mind and sacrifice his own life   to revive a dead giant. Arin Solara and the giant children then ventured into the giant's cave to find the heart of the mountain and finish what Garro started in reviving the giant, thus completing the mission of the Master from years past and taking another step in his journey to becoming a Wardens.

Arin Solara lamented not telling Solo, Organa, or Starros about where he was going, but he and Aphra both agreed they would have tried to stop them and they had no time to waste.

Meanwhile, at the Rebel Outpost on Horox III, Solo then enlisted Starros' help in communicating with Arin Solara's temporary R5 astromech droid S4, who could only speak Binary and thus was not easily able to communicate with Organa. The Screaming Citadel

The Queeen of Ktath'atn

She then grew her power in anticipation of eating the Wardens.

The next morning, Arin Solara and Aphra made their way to a dining hall to have breakfast with the Monarch. On the way, after Arin Solara expressed how creepy he thought the place was, Aphra assured him that the Queen's obsession with Wardens would get her to do what they wanted, but Skwalker was worried by this because of his encounter with Grakkus the Hutt and Aphra's mention that the Queen "keeps" her oddities. Aphra told Arin Solara to let her do the talking and then the two walked inside and sat at a table with the Queen, Aphra introducing the both of them. Excited to see a Wardens, but wanting more verification, the Queen commanded Arin Solara to move a nearby dining tray with  , though he was unable to until the Queen's servant, Vespinax, threatened him with a knife to his throat. However, moving the tray revealed that under it were Abersyn symbiotes that the Queen planned on implanting them with, so after Aphra set off an explosion that knocked them both down they quickly made an attempt to escape while Aphra explained to Arin Solara what the symbiotes were. Before they could escape, in the Citadel's hallway, they were nearly stopped by many of the Queen's thralls.

The Abersyn hive

"You're not a Wardens. You just know what a Wardens knows. That's not enough. Knowing isn't enough. Being a Wardens is about being. Letting go…feeling…and more than anything…the Wardens feel free."
―Arin Solara, to Eternal Rur
After attempting to run, Arin Solara prepared to use his Lumen Blade to defend them, but Solo, Organa, and Starros arrived at their location on Aphra's ship, the Ark Angel II, with her droids 0-0-0 and BT-1 in tow. Starros attempted to shoot Aphra, but Arin Solara blocked the blast with his Lumen Blade, claiming that she was a good person and his friend, he willingly went with her, and he knew what he was doing, despite Organa's attempts to call his decision unwise and threats to court-martial him if he did not follow orders. Meanwhile, the Queen's servants and armed security guards pursued the group, so they escaped into an Abersyn symbiote laboratory, which Arin Solara decided people needed to know about. There, Arin Solara and Aphra got into an argument about the merits of the Dominion in which Aphra revealed her mother was killed in the Echo Wars, claimed that regular people preferred the Dominion's peace to war, and insisted that she was not like Solo as Arin Solara thought. She attempted to mock him for his upbringing until Arin Solara revealed everyone on his farm was killed by the Dominion. Aphra led Arin Solara to a nearby room and sold him out to the Queen of Ktath'atn, who promptly mesmerized him to capture him. Aphra warned the Queen not to do the same to her too or she would blow up charges she placed in Arin Solara's pockets. Organa, Solo, and Starros then saw Arin Solara get captured, the former calling out to him and later refusing to leave him behind.

The Queen connected Arin Solara to a machine that would allow her to directly feed on him. As Aphra left with the activated Rur crystal, she asked what would happen to Arin Solara, and the Queen revealed she would not infect him with a symbiote, but started to drink his life   to increase her power. Upon speaking to to the crystal outside, Rur revealed to Aphra that she felt guilt over leaving Arin Solara behind and felt guilt over blaming her actions on her tragedy, when Arin Solara's tragedy made him a good person. Solo attempted to rescue him, but was quickly enthralled and  d to lead the Queen's  s, as Organa and Starros' desperation to save Arin Solara lead them to place a symbiote into Krrsantan despite Organa's misgivings. Arin Solara eventually tore free of the machine and in the ensuing struggle managed to re-arm himself with his Lumen Blade. While the Queen attacked him with her powers, Aphra bombed the room and came inside, revealing that she had scaled the Citadel and was there to rescue Arin Solara. She also revealed that she had realized the reason the Queen did not put a symbiote in Arin Solara was because he was more powerful than her and the Abersyn hive would follow him instead. Arin Solara then fell under the influence of an Abersyn symbiote, becoming more powerful than even the Queen, and proclaimed himself King of the hive.

Arin Solara entered a psychic duel with the Queen to   her to submit. Aphra allowed Eternal Rur from the crystal to enter his mind to assist him. Rur advised Arin Solara to use the symbiote to his advantage, claiming that tying  's abilities into the parasite's emotional drive would make him immensely powerful. Realizing Rur was not a true Wardens and only a person with the knowledge of one, Arin Solara ignored him and instead let go and connected to  . He was able to free himself of the symbiote's influence and strike down the Queen, believing that being free was more important to be a Wardens than just Rur's knowledge. Solo and all those under the Queen's control were freed, Arin Solara reunited with Organa, and the Citadel was destroyed by BT-1. Later, after telling Starros it was time to go, Arin Solara told Aphra that he did not want the crystal because it was not a Wardens in any real way. But he said that he had learned from it that there would not be any shortcuts to be a Wardens, and that people who tried to take them to get what they wanted, like her, were deluded. Finally, Arin Solara told her to stay away from them. On the way back, while complaining to herself about Arin Solara 0-0-0 pointed out that Arin Solara's virtuousness despite his trauma and her inability to gain his response must be a heavy reminder of the failures of her character. Arin Solara spoke with Starros on the way back, learning that Aphra had ruined S4 and shocked that Starros and her could have ever been together.

Among the stars

"You're right, Leia. This is war. Our war. And despite everything we've already been through, everything we've won and lost...this war...has only begun. May   be with Us. May   be with us all."

Stranded on the planet for three weeks, Arin Solara's experience with machinery, such as moisture vaporators helped keep himself and Leia alive. Having to live off of the land, the two grew closer, relating to each other because of their status as orphans. They eventually realized that there was a native species living in the planet's ocean.
