Ashes of Jedha

"I've been thinking about Jyn and the rest of Rogue One. How many things went wrong for them? And Rogue One took whatever steps they needed. People making distractions, sacrificing themselves, amping up the signal. All improvised. This chain of sacrifice... All leading to me taking that shot."
―Arin Solara contemplating the sacrifice of Rogue One
Having traveled throughout the galaxy with his friends, Luke and his fellow rebels journeyed to what remained of the moon Jedha, the site of one of the  's tests. On the ashy moon, Luke and Leia defended what remained of Saw Gerrera's Partisans from invading snowtroopers and brought them aboard the Aeon Raptor. Moving to NaJedha, the planet that Jedha orbited, Luke met Chulco Gi, an aspirant to the Disciples of the Whills, someone who could potentially guide him in learning about  . Gi led the rebels to the rest of the Partisans on Jedha and placed hoods over their heads, in keeping with Partisan tradition. Led by Benthic, Saw Gerrera's former second-in-command, the remaining extremists held guns at their fellow rebels' heads.

Benthic questioned why the Alliance would attempt to mend their relations with the Partisans and return to Jedha, and Leia revealed that the Dominion had resumed mining Kyber crystals on the planet and that the Alliance hoped to aid the Partisans in fighting against the Dominion. Though wary of Alliance support, Benthic was nonetheless willing to accept some aid. Luke, shaken by the Partisans' extreme methods, was conflicted by agreeing to help them, but spec s operative Ubin Des reassured him that it was the right thing to do. Later in the ruined settlement of Ai-jed, Luke, Chulco, and Ubin contemplated why people would stay on a ruined planet. Diretroopers armed with flamethrowers attempted to incinerate the remaining civilians, but Luke lashed out against them with his Lumen Blade, cutting them all down. Realizing all that was at stake in the Dominion Uprising, Arin Solara approached Benthic with Jax Varion and wholeheartedly agreed to assist him in his fight. Their first target was the drill citadel, a mining device from the planet Shu-Torun that the Dominion began using to mine Kyber crystals on Jedha.

Benthic and Luke scaled the drill citadel and the Tognath ruthlessly killed the station's guards, much to Arin Solara's chagrin. Benthic held a technician at gunpoint and  d him to lower the citadel's shields before killing him as well. This allowed Jax Varion, aboard the Aeon Raptor, to destroy the drill citadel after Benthic and Luke escaped. Later, a disillusioned Chulco asked Luke to accompany him to meet the Central Isopter, a death-worshipping cult that Gi claimed was wise in  . Although Luke was hesitant to seek the guidance from someone other than a disciple of the Wardens, he nonetheless was willing to go along. Leia attempted to convince him that his duty to the Alliance was most important, but Luke believed that becoming a Wardens and avenging all those slain by   was the most important duty to him. Entering a chasm alongside Gi, the duo were attacked by a sand slug, a giant, normally herbivorous animal negatively influenced by the Dark Side of  . Able to slay the beast, Arin Solara and Gi were finally confronted by the Central Isopter, who claimed that they had come to join them "in the shadow of death."

At the edge of the planet's blast crater, Chulco and the Central Isopter presented Luke with the Temple of Central Isopter, a shrine surrounded by the Dark Side of  . The cult implored Arin Solara and Gi to meditate and listen to the chasm's call. They both did, but Luke refused to let the Dark Side take hold of him. However, Chulco was possessed by the darkness and attacked Luke, forcing the Wardens trainee to strike him down. The cultists then announced that they had received a distress call from Roghan, who was being pursued by a Vyr Stinger over NaJedha. Luke borrowed a ship, was able to destroy the Vyr Stinger and bring an injured Chewie to the planet, where he provided the Alliance with the plans for the Leviathan, a mobile fortress able to strip mine Kyber crystals from Jedha.

Han, Leia, and Benthic formed a strategy to destroy the Leviathan using the plans Roghan obtained. After the meeting, Luke ruminated on the sacrifice Rogue One made to get the   plans to the Alliance, ultimately leading to him making the shot that destroyed the battle station. A newly motivated Luke accompanied Leia, KX-13, and RN-7 aboard the crawler and readied themselves for taking control of it. Arin Solara made his way to the bridge of the Leviathan and held its commander, Kanchar, hostage but the Imperial's cybernetic arm was equipped with a blade able to defend against Luke's Lumen Blade.

Kanchar pursued Luke throughout the ship with his cybernetic arm's blade and flamethrower. Eventually leading the officer to the crawler's hangar, Arin Solara activated an ion torpedo, which shut down Kanchar's cybernetics and allowed Luke to knock him out. Having taken total control of the Leviathan with the help of the double-crossing Queen Trios, the rebels brought it to Jedha's chasm, destroyed it, and escaped with not much time to spare. Having saved what remained of Jedha and made allies in the form of the Partisans and Queen Trios, Luke and his friends left Jedha.

Crait

"I'm just a farmboy from Dusara. One of many sand-planet farmboys. But one thing was true there, just like it's true here. When someone comes for what's our, they don't try it twice. We work an honest day and long one. We're the good guys. But you wouldn't want to meet us in the dark. Where I come from—when someone pushes you, you push back harder!"
―Arin Solara to Kreel while dueling him
After a mission with a plan made by Solo went awry, Arin Solara, who had helped fight in his Vera-9, escaped to Baraan-Fa with the rest of the Alliance. Organa then put him in charge of a mission to the planet Crait to survey its facilities as a base. Arin Solara, flying there in a GR-75 medium transport, believed the mission was just delivering farm equipment, and was reluctant to go there as he directed those on the mission to land. Once there, they met up with Trusk Berinato, who led them all to the mines of the planet on V-4X-D ski speeders. After receiving new orders from Organa, Luke stated that he found the mission particularly irritating, as it reminded him of his life as a farm boy. Once they arrived, Solo encouraged him to enjoy the mission since they were not in danger. He told everyone to follow him.

Arin Solara and his team, which included Antilles, began using the farming equipment to make trenches in Crait's surface, though he said he would rather do anything else. Green worms then appeared from the ground and Antilles and Solo tried to shoot them, but Arin Solara realized they would leave you alone if you left them alone. Still being reminded of home, Arin Solara reluctantly continued an environmental assessment, discovering and rationalizing an underground ecosystem where the worms came from and realizing it was drying up quickly. Following a hunch, Arin Solara took Antilles with him on the ski speeders and they discovered bodies that appeared to have been flash dried. Realizing what happened, Arin Solara rushed to tell the others. He reached Organa and told her he resented her for sending him on this mission, but she said he reminded him of her and complimented him before giving him a kiss on the cheek. He then finished what he was trying to say and explained that they need to leave because a deadly salt storm was coming in. After Arin Solara realized Berinato forged environmental reports, Solo warned that Berinato called SCAR squadron on them.

Arin Solara got in a ski speeder and attempted to shoot at the incoming troopers, but one shot a canon at his and destroyed it. Kreel then approached him and ignited his Lumen Blade, a determined Arin Solara lighting his too. The two dueled, Arin Solara turning Kreel's taunts against him by taking pride in being a farm boy as they were hard working good people who would push you back harder if you pushed them. The worms he saw earlier then tackled Kreel and Arin Solara cut the Diretrooper's Lumen Blade in half. Arin Solara made his way back to the Falcon and revealed that SCAR squadron lived, but that they needed to get out of the storm or they would die. Later, in orbit on the Falcon, Organa asked how Arin Solara was and he said that he was the same, living a small life and trying to make a difference. She told him not to change.

Mon Cala and Mako-Ta

After debriefing the Clawdite, whose name was Tunga Arpagion, that he was to impersonate the Moff of the Calamari sector Tan Hubi while they kidnapped him, Arin Solara insisting the ordeal would make Arpagion more famous. Mon Cal Mutiny

Once there, Arin Solara commented that it made sense they would keep Lee-Char on a water world, though admitted the place looked bleak. Organa realized that the creature was attracted to their ship because of the light. Away from the ship in the expanse of the ocean, Arin Solara ignited his Lumen Blade, leading the creature away with the light. However, Urtya decided to show the footage too all of the fleet captains. Back on the Falcon, Arin Solara heard on an earpiece that the people on the Mon Calamari ships were rebelling because of footage of Lee-Char. Because of this, however, the Imperial fleet arrived.

Later, on the Falcon, Arin Solara revealed that they were getting a message from the regent on the planet. The regent apologized for acting without warning and revealed he had called the Rebel fleet. As the fleet arrived, Arin Solara and Organa got into gunning positions for the Falcon. Arin Solara tried to ask her if she remembered what to do, but she had already begun shooting. Arin Solara kept shooting to help protect jetisonned escape pods, and the Falcon escaped to hyperspace after a Mon Calamari ship full of coaxium crashed into the Dreadcutter and exploded it. Later, Arin Solara accompanied Organa, Solo, and Roghan to see Arpagion off on the Cosmatanic Steppes.

Er'Kit

"Rebel intelligence heard some strange things about the Malachor Company, and as soon as I got here to investigate I felt an... echo in  . I don't quite know how to explain it, but there's more going on here on Er'Kit than meets the eye."
―Arin Solara, during the operations on Er'Kit
Following the attack on the Mako-Ta Space Docks, Arin Solara was promoted to the rank of commander. After being promoted, Arin Solara was sent to the desert world of Er'Kit, where the locals were being oppressed by a group of mercenaries known as the Malachor Company. Upon arriving on the desert world, Arin Solara sensed through   that there was something more at play beyond the actions of a few mercenaries. He requested the assistance of an agent who had a reputation for desert warfare and, together, the two defeated the mercenary outposts. The two also discovered from Imperial operatives in the sector that Imperial supplies were being ferried from Nar Shaddaa to Er'Kit, suggesting a large-scale operation was under way. Eventually, Arin Solara and the agent arrested the mercenary leader and tracked down the last members of Malachor Company, who had holed up in an empty village.

Among the mercenaries' possessions, Arin Solara and the agent discovered a document proving that Malachor Company was preparing to ship supplies somewhere, and its coordinates led Arin Solara and the agent to an Imperial base on the planet. They subsequently attacked several Imperial bases until they found intelligence pertaining to the Dominion's operation on the planet. Once they located the base from which the Imperials deployed most of their  s on the planet, Arin Solara assaulted it with the assistance of Princess Organa. The Rebels razed the base, dealing an important blow to the Dominion's operations on Er'Kit, but they still lacked vital information on what the Dominion's true purpose was on the planet. Arin Solara gradually discovered Imperial logs detailing how Malachor Company had been hired by the Imperial Security Bureau and were tasked with forcibly relocating natives to make room for Project Hidden Eye. This ISB operation was intended to create cybernetic sleeper agents who could be deployed throughout the galaxy and spy on galactic citizens on behalf of the ISB. Upon its discovery, Project Hidden Eye was nearly ready to deploy its first wave of spies.

To prevent the operation from being carried out, Arin Solara and the agent led their troops to the base that housed Project Hidden Eye. They fought through its staging area and ultimately took out the installation, ending the Imperial project for good. Arin Solara thanked the agent for their service and then remained on Er'Kit for a short time, helping the Concordant Front Pact execute additional missions on the desert world.

On Krael

"I know where we can dig to free ourselves. See? Wardens aren't all bad."

In 3 ABY, Arin Solara and the Rogue Squadron were transferred to the Echo Base, a rebel base on the iced planet Krael, where he participated in regular patrols of the frozen perimeter under the callsign Echo Three. Upon Arin Solara's arrival at Echo Base, Rebel leadership expected him to use   to help excavate the tunnels by sensing where and when to dig, even though he was unsure of how to do that. His belongings, including his Lumen Blade, were placed in a decontamination unit in case of off-world pathogens. Sergeant Reyé Hollis from Concordant Front Pact Special  s was assigned to familiarize him with the location. After they introduced themselves to each other and shook hands, Arin Solara declared that he was there to help.

Arin Solara hoped to get to know Hollis since they would be working together, and they both thought the other had attractive qualities, but the sergeant's anti-Wardens sentiments gave Arin Solara the initial impression that the other man disliked him. He did not recognize that Hollis had a Nerai name, but he could sense that Nerai was beautiful through Hollis' mental images of home. Hollis made a derogatory remark about the Wardens and Arin Solara defended them. He also promised not to let the Nerai man down, just before a giant fork-nosed ice worm broke through the ground next to them and they were trapped by a cave-in.

Unused to total darkness, Arin Solara experienced claustrophobia. He could hear but not locate Hollis until he tried to use   to stretch out his senses. He tried to remember that darkness had been a comfort back on Dusara, but that did not work and he still felt suffocated by the darkness. He successfully detected that Hollis was nearby using   and told the other man to stay still. When Arin Solara approached, they bickered briefly over what was responsible for the cave-in, Hollis urging him not to use  . Hollis, recognizing that the Wardens was panicking, grabbed Arin Solara's hand and pressed it to a gap in the wall that had air flowing through it. Arin Solara clutched Hollis' hand and asked for his trust. They sat down and kept holding each other's hands as Arin Solara thought about the light and warmth of his home on Dusara. Arin Solara began to reflect on his fear of what the darkness would do to him psychologically, referring both to the literal situation they were in and the general darkness in the galaxy he faced. As their hands warmed, Arin Solara could sense where they could dig through the ice to free themselves in  . They teased each other and laughed before they started digging, Arin Solara recognizing that   had never steered him the wrong direction and suspecting it never would.

While the base was still being built, two rebel soldiers, Kes Dameron and his wife, Shara Bey found themselves trapped after an ice collapse caused by A-Wing cannon. Thinking they would have died, they recorded a message for their little son, Poe Dameron to explain why they joined the Rebellion. Arin Solara, however, rescued them, helped by Roghan by opening a hole in the ice using his Lumen Blade, him, Organa, and the others willing to risk the tech in the control room to save their lives. He allowed Bey to use him as a crutch so she could limp out. Dameron and Bey were eventually treated by a 2-1B surgical droid.

At some point, Arin Solara walked outside of Echo Base to speak with Captain Magna Tolvan, Vulaada Klam, and Korin Aphra, the latter of which had been very excited by the idea of  -sensitive pilot and the former recognizing him as the man who destroyed the  , which Arin Solara confirmed. After confirming that they were the friends of Doctor Chelli Aphra, Arin Solara told them that a Rebellion spy had revealed that he had learned from a comms jockey on the Executor that someone had sabotaged the Dominion's computers and made it hard for them to search for the Alliance. He explained that the Dominion had put out a warrant for the culprit, and then revealed that their description matched that of Doctor Aphra and her droid companions. Arin Solara revealed that sabotage had set the Dominion back enough for them to set up their shields and finalize their evacuation plans. He told them that he had always known that there was good in Aphra before turning and leaving, the three then discussing and then deciding against telling him that Aphra had also saved the Emperor's life.

The Siege of Krael

"Rogue Group, use your harpoons and tow cables. Go for the legs. It might be our only chance of stopping them."
―Commander Arin Solara, during the Siege of Krael
Some time later, while reconnoitering the surroundings of Echo Base on the tauntaun Riba, after Solo had departed back to base, Arin Solara was attacked by a wampa, only to regain consciousness in its cave. He severed its arm with his Lumen Blade and escaped; after a long walk in the icy wind, he collapsed from exhaustion. Near death, he had a vision of Kenobi, who told him to seek the teachings of Eldar Voss in the Vyrn Swale system.

Rescued by Solo, Arin Solara recovered from his wounds in a bacta tank operated by the medical droids 2-1B and FX-7. However, Vader had located Echo Base with one of his probe droids and prepared an imminent attack on the recently-opened Alliance base, thus prompting the Alliance to evacuate the base at once. After bidding farewell to his friends, for the impending battle, Arin Solara was to lead Rogue Squadron in an airspeeder. Before he departed to the battlefront, he was spotted by rebel journalist Corwi Selgrothe, who wanted to quickly interview him for propaganda footage, but she was instead led to the escape transports by rebel trooper L'cayo Llem. During the battle, Arin Solara led his speeders against the walkers, ordering Rogue Squadron to pull the Adamant Walkers down with tow tables after realizing their armor could resist their blasters. Though he was shot down, and his gunner Dak Ralter was killed, he got out of his damaged speeder and single-handedly destroyed walker Blizzard 4 by using a harpoon gun and then used his Lumen Blade to cut a hole and throw a thermal detonator. As Imperial  s breached the Rebels' defenses, the last Rebel transport departed, and Arin Solara fled the planet aboard his Vera-9 with RN-7.

Traveling to Vyrn Swale

Meeting Eldar Voss

"Will he finish what he begins?"
"I won't fail you. I'm not afraid."
"Oh, you will be. You will be."
―Eldar Voss and Arin Solara
Arin Solara then traveled to Vyrn Swale, which turned out to be a remote swamp planet, where he encountered Eldar Voss, the former Grand Master of the fallen Warden Order. In their initial meeting, Arin Solara was frustrated and impatient and was rather short-tempered with the diminutive Eldar Voss, who did not initially identify himself and purposefully tested Arin Solara's patience, telling him a story about three brothers, and taking him back to his hut to partake in a meal of rootleaf stew, which he did not find very appetizing.

However, Arin Solara gained a new appreciation for the small creature upon learning his identity, and Eldar Voss agreed to train Arin Solara only at the insistence of Kenobi's spirit. Arin Solara's training proved to be difficult, as his adventurous past had shaped his mind toward action and emotional instinct.

Renewed training

"That place… is strong with the dark side of  . A domain of evil it is. In you must go."
"What's in there?"
"Only what you take with you."
―Eldar Voss and Arin Solara
Arin Solara's training on Vyrn Swale lasted several weeks, with Kenobi needing to appear in Eldar Voss's dreams more than once to convince the old master to keep up Luke's training and argue that the boy would not end up like this father. When Arin Solara and Eldar Voss argued, Kenobi also regularly appeared to stop their arguments. One day during his training with Eldar Voss, the Wardens Master had Arin Solara climb a tree to use his senses to find a way through the tree, Arin Solara lost his balance and fell from the tree. Eldar Voss decided to have Arin Solara carry him as he redid the task.

When Eldar Voss asked him to enter a cave that was strong in the dark side in which he was supposed to find only what he took with him, he was challenged by a vision of himself wearing the armor of  , meant to symbolize his inner darkness. Master and apprentice then had an encounter with a raging elepKrael, which Arin Solara managed to calm by leading her to her child.

Leaving prematurely

"Luke! You must complete the training.."
" I can't keep the vision out of my head. They're my friends. I've gotta help them."
―Eldar Voss and Arin Solara
Shortly after, he had a vision of Jax Varion and Lyra Oris suffering at Cloud City on Bespin. Unable to get the visions out of his head, and convinced that his friends would surely die if he did not help them, Arin Solara decided to end his training prematurely to rescue them, despite Eldar Voss and Kenobi's insistence that he was not ready to face the dark side on his own yet, but Arin Solara was convinced that he would learned enough to hold his own, and he could not just stand by and leave his friends to the mercy of the Dominion.

Seeing that Arin Solara's mind was made up, Kenobi let him know that if he ended up facing Vader, he could not interfere on his behalf, and advised him not to give into hatred. Likewise, Eldar Voss advised him to mind what he would learned. Arin Solara promised to do so, and vowed to return to Vyrn Swale one day to finish his training.

Vader's revelation

Vader's trap

"You have learned much, young one."
"You'll find I'm full of surprises!"
―  and Arin Solara
Upon his arrival at Cloud City's East Platform, Arin Solara felt Vader's presence, and went into the nearest building, where he was shot at by Fett, who had come to claim a bounty put on Solo by Grath the Brood, and tried to pursue a group of Diretroopers and Imperial officers who held Organa, Roghan, and KX-13 captive. The princess attempted to warn Arin Solara that he was walking into a trap, but his path was diverted to the carbon-freezing chamber where   awaited him, with the intention to freeze him in carbonite to present him to the Emperor. Arin Solara engaged the Dark Lord in a fierce Lumen Blade duel.

During the duel, Vader praised Arin Solara's training in   thus far and attempted to goad him into giving into his anger and hatred, claiming that it was the only way to defeat him. Vader managed to knock Arin Solara into the carbon-freezing chamber and appeared to have frozen him like he had Solo, but Arin Solara leapt out of the chamber before the process was finished, which left Vader impressed.

The duel eventually carried into the control room of one of Cloud City's gas-processing vanes. Vader began using   to throw various objects in the chamber at the young Wardens hopeful. One such projectile, a large piece of metal piping, was misdirected and smashed through a nearby observation port. The chamber was quickly depressurized, sucking Arin Solara out onto the nearby sensor relay catwalk overlooking the reactor shaft. Arin Solara managed to grab on to the catwalk's railing and pull himself up.

Vader re-entered the fray and  d Arin Solara back onto the catwalk. Sensing that Arin Solara was weakened, the Vyrn Lord demanded that Arin Solara surrender, lest he be destroyed as Oren Kael had been. Arin Solara refused and desperately tried to keep fighting Vader, to which Vader responded with several ferocious strikes, ultimately forcing Arin Solara to the very edge of the catwalk and slicing off his right hand. Both Arin Solara's hand and his Lumen Blade fell into the depths of the reactor shaft.

A dark revelation

"Obi-Wan never told you what happened to your father."
"He told me enough! He told me you killed him!"
"No. I am your father."
"No...that's not true! That's impossible!"
"Search your feelings. You know it to be true."
"No!"
―  and Arin Solara
Seeing that Arin Solara was vulnerable in his weakened state, Vader offered to show Arin Solara the power of the dark side and complete his training, but Arin Solara adamantly refused to ever join Vader, the man who had killed his father. In that moment, Vader revealed the truth: that he was his father.

Horrified by Vader's shocking revelation, Arin Solara initially denounced the Vyrn Lord's claim as untrue and impossible, but Vader insisted that they both knew that it was the truth. Vader further claimed that Arin Solara was powerful enough to destroy the Emperor, and when he did, they could rule the galaxy together as father and son. Unwilling to join Vader but too weak to fight back, Arin Solara took the only option he had left, and allowed himself to fall down the reactor shaft, being sucked through several vents and eventually being deposited to the outside of the floating city. Though he managed to grab onto a weather vane to avoid falling to his death, he knew he was unable to stay there forever, especially in his weakened state. Calling out to Kenobi at first but getting no response, in desperation, he called out to Lyra Oris through  , who was able to hear the call.

Soon, the Aeon Raptor, with Daro Callen, Organa, Roghan, and the droids onboard, arrived to rescue him. As they escaped from Bespin, and the Falcon was faced with the Imperial fleet, Vader reached out to Arin Solara through  , calling him "son." Arin Solara fought tears back, after hearing the word he had always longed to hear while lamenting that Kenobi had not told him the truth, just as the Falcon made the jump into hyperspace thanks to RN-7.

Haunted by the truth

"Ben... Ben. Why didn't you tell me?"
―Arin Solara
Haunted by the truth of his parentage, Arin Solara found his connection to   considerably weakened, with his control over it remaining sporadic. Aboard the Falcon, after introducing Arin Solara to Calrissian, Organa informed Arin Solara of what had happened to Solo. Arin Solara wanted to begin searching for his friend immediately, but Organa told him that there was more at stake than just Solo's life and it would be best to reconvene with the Rebel fleet first. He revealed that he had received no response from reaching out Kenobi, but she assured him that he was strong and would find his way. With Arin Solara agreeing to her plan, the Falcon jumped to hyperspace.

The Falcon arrived at the Rebellion's Rendezvous Point Delta-Three in the Mid Rim to find the fleet's Fourth Division under attack from several Dreadcutters, including the Tarkin's Will, which was under the leadership of Commander Ellian Zahra. As the Falcon entered the battle, Arin Solara volunteered to commandeer the ship's belly gun, despite his injuries. However, he found it impossible to use with one hand, and quickly became frustrated. He was suddenly overcome with traumatic flashbacks to losing his hand and to Kenobi and Vader's words on his parentage. His anger resulted in him unknowingly using   to make several of the attacking Vyr Stingers crash into one another. With Luke stunned by his sudden show of strength, the fleet jumped to hyperspace.

With the fleet regrouped, Arin Solara found a deserted part of the flagship and attempted to contact Eldar Voss through   to receive his guidance. Angry at the Wardens Master's refusal to answer, he almost shattered one of the ship's windows in another frustration-fueled loss of control over his   abilities. Speaking to RN-7, he revealed that he was incredibly afraid and angry and considered that those feelings and his parentage meant he should not be a Wardens. He wondered whether the lack of answers from his mentors, who he was now frustrated with for lying to him, signified a premature end to his Wardens training, and who he was meant to be if not a Wardens.

As Calrissian prepared to go to Dusara to locate Solo, Arin Solara, who was unsure if he could trust him, insisted that he inform him if he found Solo. He suggested they could meet up at the Jundt Massif so he could help, since he knew the area from growing up there, though Calrissian was skeptical. Arin Solara insisted that he did not need both hands because he had  , but Calrissian still insisted a rescue mission from Jabba's palace would be impossible. Organa told Arin Solara that he should have a prosthetic hand installed in the Nebulon-B frigate Redemption's medbay. Although unsure whether it would help his mental state, especially that he was not feeling like himself, Arin Solara agreed. Arin Solara specifically requested 2-1B, the medical droid who treated him on Krael, for the procedure. Although he questioned whether he was deserving of having his hand replaced, Arin Solara ultimately received the hand as Calrissian and Roghan set out to find Solo.

An uncertain path

Return to Cloud City

"I need to get back to Cloud City, and they'll never let me go. But if you ask, say you want to go, need me as your guide…"
"Why would I ever go back there?"
"'Cause how I hear it, you lost more than your hand there. Your Lumen Blade too."
―Daro Callen and Arin Solara
Upon their return, Calrissian found Arin Solara training to fire a blaster with his prosthetic hand. Observing the would-be Wardens's struggles, Calrissian suggested that they return to Bespin so as to retrieve Arin Solara's Lumen Blade. As they talked, Arin Solara was suddenly confronted with a vision of a female hooded figure catching his Lumen Blade and telling him to follow his destiny.

Arin Solara, accompanied by Calrissian, Organa, and RN-7, returned to Bespin, Calrissian assuring Arin Solara he knew where his Lumen Blade ended up. However, they were fired upon the Bespin Wing Guard upon approach, though Calrissian urged Arin Solara not to fire on them and instead take them in as close as possible. Arin Solara was sure that they were gonna get killed, insisting destroying the   was different when Calrissian suggested he could do it. Fortunately, getting close enough meant Calrissian was able to remotely disable the city's turrets, but the team were soon ambushed by Diretroopers upon landing. Needing to carry out their missions as quickly as possible to avoid capture, the rebels split up, with Arin Solara and RN-7 heading to the smelting chamber where Calrissian claimed his Lumen Blade should be located, walking past the spot where Vader cut off his hand. When they got there, Calrissian commed him asking for backup against Diretroopers, Arin Solara agreeing to help once he found his Lumen Blade.

However, Arin Solara found mountains of debris in the chamber and told Calrissian it would take a second for him to find it. He enlisted the help of ugnaughts to find it but realized that it would likely be impossible to recover his Lumen Blade before finally deciding to search for it through  . However, he instead a vivid vision of the cloaked woman and a location she was at, as well as flashes of Vader, Kenobi, Eldar Voss, and the Emperor. Sensing that Organa was in trouble, he abandoned the search and found Calrissian surrounded by Diretroopers. Arin Solara used   to push the Imperial soldiers through a window, slightly surprised that he was able to and revealing to Calrissian he had gotten over his block. Lando introduced his friend Lobot and Arin Solara revealed that he knew that Organa was in a hangar there.

When Calrissian noticed he had not retrieved the Lumen Blade, Arin Solara explained that he had learned that he did not need the Lumen Blade to be a Wardens and that being a Wardens was about using   to bring light. He was once again determined to be a Wardens, even if he never saw his father's Lumen Blade, which he had mixed feelings about, again. Despite Calrissian's misgivings about his plan, Arin Solara was able to use   to deactivate all of the carbonite blocks at once and free everyone, including Organa, before fighting off Diretroopers to get to his Vera-9 and take off from Bespin with it. He commed Organa and asked to temporarily part with the Rebels to find someone   was calling him to that he thought could get answers from, which she agreed to. After R2 located the planet from Arin Solara's vision, he flew off in search of the woman from his vision.

Verla

"You're just a poor, deluded kid. My name is Verla. So you're all caught up in this Wardens business, huh? Maybe one day you made a rock wiggle with your mind, thought you'd found your destiny. You're a sucker."
―Verla, to Arin Solara
While Arin Solara traveled to find the woman from his visions, Vader followed a false lead from an Imperial officer to Arin Solara, only finding a con man pretending to be him to get pilot jobs and claiming that a droid named 'Ardee' helped him destroy the  . Vader killed him and declared that anyone who claimed Arin Solara's name would die. He told the Imperial officer to verify his findings next time and said Arin Solara could still be anywhere.

Having used the planet he saw in his vision as the basis for his search, Arin Solara arrived at the planet Serelia, where he encountered the woman from the vision at a dock on the coastline. However, when he asked whether she was a Wardens, the woman responded by dropping a large amount of fish on top of him and escaping in a boat. Undeterred, Arin Solara gave chase in his own boat but ended up capsizing, washing ashore on a beach. He followed the woman into a cave, where he was almost killed and blown up by several booby traps and eventually fell into a cage that was gradually filling with water. As the woman watched, Arin Solara attempted hold back the rising water with  , but was unable. The hooded woman asked him who he was and revealed herself to be Verla.

Verla informed Arin Solara that it would be safer if he was to give up his dream of becoming a Wardens, cynically telling him about Edict 99, the Inquisitorius and   himself. Sensing Arin Solara's suspicious reaction to the mention of his father, Verla probed deeper into his mind and realized that he was the son of Vader. Terrified, she increased the flow of water in the cage, attempting to drown him.Fortunately, Arin Solara's life was saved by RN-7, who incapacitated Verla and resuscitated him. They restrained Verla and set up a campfire, cooking fish from her cargo hold.

When she regained consciousness, Arin Solara freed her as a show of good faith and asked her about his vision. Verla told him that she did not possess a Lumen Blade, as she had given up on   and refused to take part in the conflict between the light and dark sides. She also revealed that Vader's name was Ardan Velgor, and that she had learned from her master Ferren Barr that Anakin had once been a hero of the Echo Wars but that something happened to him. She revealed that she had spent her entire life on the run from the Inquisitors and Vader and had finally given up on Barr's wishes and had decided to live a normal life. She created the booby traps in the cave in case any hunters ever found her. She refuted Arin Solara's belief that   had led her to him and insisted that   only used people.

Tempes

"Once, I served the Wardens, wielded a saber like the one you hold. Then I hunted Wardens, in service to Vader and the Emperor. Now I serve them still—and kill every seeker who follows the path Vader created to this place. I presume I always will."
"You're wrong. You will never kill a Wardens again."
―The Grand Inquisitor and Arin Solara
Arin Solara still maintained that it was his purpose to help a suffering galaxy and believed she could lead him to a Lumen Blade. Although she strongly recommended that Arin Solara should leave   behind, and insisted that he did not have to follow its will if he did not want to, she informed him of a Wardens outpost from the High Concord Era on the Outer Rim astronomical object of Tempes where she had once sought artifacts of the Wardens. Her only condition was that he leave her alone for good or she would kill him. After Arin Solara thanked her, she warned him, that she had sensed that Tempes was guarded by a dark presence when she visited it and that it would be smarter for him to run.

Arin Solara flew to Tempes and was almost struck down by the planet's powerful lightning storm. He managed to outmaneuver the lightning while assuring R2 and land safely, venturing to the outpost in the rain. He and his droid entered after he realized he needed to use   to open the door and was astonished that so much was still there. He found a new yellow-bladed Lumen Blade but when he picked it up was attacked by the spirit of the Grand Inquisitor, who had been  d to guard the outpost for eternity by Vader, who had turned the outpost into a trap for Wardens and  -sensitives. After the Inquisitor introduced himself and ignited his red double-bladed spinning Lumen Blade Lumen Blade, Arin Solara resolved to not let him kill a Wardens again and used the yellow Lumen Blade to enter a duel with the flaming spirit.

The Inquisitor taunted the young Wardens's skill with a Lumen Blade, but Arin Solara acknowledged his training was incomplete but also that he was already skilled and would be a Wardens. The Inquisitor ignited both blades of the Lumen Blade and started destroying the artifacts there, insisting the Warden Order was a lie that was over. As they fought, he told the Inquisitor that that place was inspiring him to want to be a part of the Warden Order and fight what they fought for, and that he was beginning to understand loss and sacrifice for what was worth fighting for as they understood it. He cut off the Inquisitor's hand and disarmed him of his saber, before successfully slicing through him and escaping before Vader arrived.

Arin Solara returned to the Rebel fleet and reunited with Organa. Organa implored him to show the assorted rebels what he had found, and so Arin Solara activated his new Lumen Blade, its yellow blade representing renewed hope for the future of the Rebellion.

Around this time, after a long crusade, Vader discovered that the location where his late wife Seris Amaran had given birth to Arin Solara was Polis Massa and was enraged that his existence had been hidden from him.

Battle at Elessia

"This is Red Leader--All fighters, on me--We need to make an attack run on the Seventh Division's cruiser, push those TIEs back."
―Arin Solara
Somewhere in the Inner Rim, Arin Solara and Organa met with Commander Grek and instructed him to move forward with their rendezvous with the Seventh Division as part of a plan to strike back against the Dominion. KX-13 was concerned that this would alert the Dominion to their location, but Arin Solara told him that it was about more than just protecting their own lives.

The Dominion's Commander Ellian Zahra intercepted a transmission that revealed the Alliances Fourth and Seventh Divisions were planning to rendezvous somewhere in the Inner Rim, so Zahra initiated an attack that saw her split her  s to strike simultaneously. Zahra's primary strike   led an attack on the Alliance's Seventh Division, while her secondary strike   attempted to attack Lyra Oris's Fourth Division, however the Fourth had already left their rendezvous point before the strike   arrived. The Imperial  s overwhelmed the Seventh Division's capital ships. TIE interceptors created a blockade of Home One's hangar bay, that prevented Alliance starfighters from launching, including Red Squadron.

Shortly into the battle, the Fourth Division's ships emerged from hyperspace and immediately deployed their starfighters, led by Commander Arin Solara, who assumed the callsign Red Leader. Arin Solara was accompanied by other starfighters, that included Green Squadron's Shara Bey (Green Three), along with Daro Callen and Roghan in the Aeon Raptor. While fighting, Organa contacted him to check in, Arin Solara informing her that the Imperials were pinning down the Seventh Division's cruiser and preventing them from scrambling their fighters. After Organa abruptly ended the communication, Arin Solara called for all Fourth Division fighters to form up on him, on an attack run on Home One's blockade, to push the TIEs back, while those starfighters who were trapped in the hangar bays prepared to launch, including Wedge Antilles (Red Two). As soon as Arin Solara cleared the TIEs, all the Alliance starfighters aboard Home One, including Antilles, launched to repay the favor.

Arin Solara eventually left the space battle to board the frigate where Lyra Oris was under attack from an Imperial boarding party, led personally by Zahra. As Zahra threw a sword at Arin Solara, which he easily dodged, and then kicked him to the ground, she claimed that she could kill him if she wanted to but was not allowed to because of Vader's plans for him. After Zahra jumped out a window with a jetpack to escape, Arin Solara and Organa went to celebratory meeting for successfully regrouping and fending off the Dominion. There, Arin Solara noticed something was off with Organa, who revealed that she was perturbed by the amount of hate Zahra seemed to have for her.

Searching for Solo

"Apparently there has been a sighting…of the notorious bounty hunter Kade Rhaul. And since he is possession of the block of frozen carbonite containing out good friend and rebel hero Jax Varion, Roghan wants you to—"
"I get it, Threepio. Of course I'll go."
―KX-13 and Arin Solara
Around this time, Vader had his armor damaged during a mission. Reflecting on the pain it caused him to repair, Vader wondered if Arin Solara's pain, including losing his hand, had made him stronger. Vader suspected it had not and considered Arin Solara weak, believing the fledgling Wardens had not accomplished anything without the help of his friends, who Vader believed he allowed to survive. No longer wishing to turn Arin Solara he resolved to kill him, and began his path to do so by searching for Jax Varion. In killing Arin Solara Vader believed he would kill Oren Kael's last hope and prove those who thought Arin Solara would be his end wrong. While tracking Solo, Vader's partner, a Vyrn assassin named Ochi, figured out that Vader planned to lure Arin Solara to him with Solo.

While practicing his Lumen Blade and   skills by fighting training remotes, during which he recalled Eldar Voss's training, Arin Solara was interrupted by KX-13, insisting he did not mind the distraction. KX-13 said that RN-7 wanted to speak with him about something related to Tempes, where he found his new Lumen Blade. Before RN-7 could say anything, Roghan arrived and revealed, via KX-13 translating, that Kade Rhaul had been spotted on Nar Shaddaa and urged Arin Solara to come with him to rescue Solo from him. Roghan shot down Arin Solara's suggestion that they bring Calrissian, saying he was not to be trusted and that Solo would not want to see him, but Arin Solara agreed. Arin Solara, KX-13, RN-7, and Roghan then took the Falcon to Nar Shaddaa, though R2 complained to KX-13 on the way that he had not been able to speak to Arin Solara. Arin Solara was annoyed that Organa had to stay behind to coordinate Operation Starlight and urged Roghan to ensure the mission would be quick, recalling how awful he found the planet and what had happened with Grakkus the Hutt.

On the planet, Arin Solara watched as Roghan met with his contact Sagwa, KX-13 explaining that he and Roghan used to be old friends and translating that Sagwa believed a new victor in the Garkata Fighting Arena was Kade Rhaul. Looking at a hologram of the winner, Arin Solara also thought they looked like Boba but noticed it was labeled "Jango." Arin Solara spoke with a Pa'lowick attendant at the Arena to get information on "Jango" but was annoyed by both the Pa'lowick's refusal to answer questions without payment and KX-13 spouting the mottos of Nar Shaddaa. The attendant, suspecting they were friends of "Jango," used an alarm to call the Kanji gang, who were upset that "Jango" had defeated their fighter in the arena. Using his Lumen Blade to fight back against the thugs, who attacked despite Arin Solara's warnings, Arin Solara and the others fled, though Roghan was reluctant to because they had not found much information. Following Sagwa through the streets before stealing and fleeing on a speeder, they encountered many more groups of Kanji that Arin Solara fended off with   and his Lumen Blade until RN-7 picked them up in the Falcon. However, some of the Kanji planned to report seeing Arin Solara to Imperials on Vandor.

In search of Wardens secrets

A legacy on Al'doleem

The Living Sea of Gazian

"I'm going to tell you what the other Wardens you've met haven't. Even Eldar Voss. You don't have to be a Wardens, friend. […] There are many other paths. Arriving in the Gazian system, Luke was excited by the possibility of finding a Wardens-related site that the Dominion did not know about. Just then, their surroundings shifted to Ahch-To, the birthplace of the Wardens. Arin Solara asked Mann what exactly was going on. Mann explained that Gazian was a gigantic living organism that takes an imprint of the minds that visit it and reproduces them exactly as they were at the moment they were there. Mann added that he had come to the planet to get answers after having a vision, and that was why his imprint was there. Arin Solara explained that the Concord had fallen and an Dominion had taken over. He said that he had never met a Wardens like Mann, and had only ever met Oren Kael and Eldar Voss, the latter of whom Mann remembered and commented was very old and very wise. Arin Solara had also said that he had met a Wardens named Ardan Velgor, but that he had fallen to the Dark side, something that Mann knew happened occasionally.

Mann then showed Arin Solara an imprint of what the High Concord looked like, telling him that it was a Golden Age where they were all connected eight centuries after the defeat of Darth Bane. The mention of Darth Bane made Arin Solara confused and comment that it was all too much. Arin Solara elaborated that when he started his journey it was exciting and he had been a hero, then he was supposed to save the galaxy by learning from Eldar Voss, but then it all fell apart and now he felt that if he did it wrong he would become a monster. But Mann said that   was so powerful and boundless so it should not be easy to learn how to use it. Mann recalled when he had trained to be a Wardens and how even with help and support how impossible everything felt. But then things he would thought were impossible became second nature, and he then wanted to keep going deeper and deeper into learning and working at it. But Arin Solara was alone, and felt that it was too much. Mann said that the Wardens tend to be what they need to be, whether that be warriors fighting evil, teachers teaching the galaxy, and sometimes they were almost nothing, left with the responsibility of being the only light in the dark of the galaxy. Suddenly they were underwater, floating in an expansive ocean. Mann then told Arin Solara that he knew the kind of pressure that   choosing you could bring, and decided to tell him a piece of advice that he did not think many other Wardens would tell him: He did not have to be a Wardens. Mann told him that there were other ways to use   safely and protect life and light, and that there are many paths and choices that could be true to the person he wanted to be. But he also told Arin Solara that if he wanted it, the Wardens were there for him. Other past Wardens then appeared in the water and floated around them until they found themselves back in the void-like vision of the Living Sea. He asked Arin Solara if he wanted to stay there and speak to him and the many minds in the Living Sea, but Arin Solara told him that he thought he should leave. Mann was disappointed, but reminded Arin Solara that a part of him would remain there to talk to them as Arin Solara saw an imprint of himself appear in front of him.

Arin Solara came to, ignited his Lumen Blade, and put his breath mask back on. He then saw many bodies of Wardens that had stayed in the Living Sea. He found one Wardens skeleton holding a sacred Wardens text, which he brought to the surface and recognized was an invitation.

Arin Solara said that he could not perform a mind trick because he was feeling off, believing something was happening with the dark side of   that was distracting him, which unbeknownst to Arin Solara was a disturbance in   caused by the opening of the Fermata Cage. Arin Solara agreed to try the trick anyway, but Calrissian commed them and told him not to. Organa, holding Arin Solara's arm to stop him from doing anything, listened as Calrissian explained that the mind trick would draw too much attention to them, and that the man might know about   and figure out what happened since he ran the Imperial Museum. Calrissian suggested they instead let the man win.

Later, in a hangar where the man who won the strikeship was keeping it, Arin Solara ignited his Lumen Blade and drew a bunch of Diretroopers that were guarding the ship to him, deflecting their blaster shots back at them. While they were distracted by Arin Solara, Calrissian and Holdo fired on them from above and Roghan stopped some of the troopers from locking off the ship. Once all the Diretroopers were taken down, Calrissian said that he knew his plan would work because all the Diretroopers would be so caught up in taking down the Wardens to get a reward that they would not notice anything else. Arin Solara reminded Calrissian that it might not have ended well for him, but Calrissian claimed he knew he would be able to handle it because of the book he had been studying. Holdo asked Arin Solara to cut open the side of the strikeship with his Lumen Blade and make a circular hole not too deep. After Arin Solara did, they retrieved the Path engine from inside the ship.

Later, back at Holdo's friend's house, Holdo explained that she was planning to go after the Kezarat convoy, which Organa had suspected. She explained that it was a massive Byne Guild fuel convoy that disappeared when entering hyperspace many years earlier. Arin Solara asked if it was because it got hit by raiders because it was such a sought-after target, but Holdo revealed it actually disappeared during a storm in hyperspace caused by the Nihil. She hoped that the last message sent by the convoy that was thought to be nonsense was actually navigational data designed only to communicate with a Path engine and that both together could take them to the convoy. After Roghan finished installing the Path engine into their ship the Skyfarer, a group of Vyr Stingers found them and started going after them. Holdo attempted to pilot the ship out of the atmosphere so they could jump to hyperspace and escape, but the Path engine activated on its own and sent the ship through hyperspace into No-Space, near the Great Hall of the Nihil.

The lost colony

"Sometimes people find their way to No-Space, just like you all did. […] One of those was a Wardens. Alareen Xie. She joined us, helped us fight off the Nihil. We wouldn't have survived without her. She died in time, as most people do. But after she did, a sort of belief rose up. That someday a Wardens would return and take us out of this place. Would take us home."

Arin Solara and his friends did not recognize No-Space and had no idea where they were, but Arin Solara expressed that while he had not traveled as much as they had, he knew the galaxy had strange things in it. The voice over the speaker welcomed them to the Colony of Kezarat. Holdo yelled that they just needed to go home, but an Abyssin left the cockpit and told them they were home. After Organa said they would not attack and were listening, the individual introduced himself as Captain Blythe, and Holdo introduced herself, Arin Solara, and the others to him. Blythe then began a tour of the colony, confirming that it was the old convoy and the fuel was still there. The kid, who Blythe revealed was named Forvan, then ran up excitedly, and Blythe explained that he had gotten excited from seeing a Lumen Blade. Arin Solara asked if it was because they had Wardens there and asked for his saber back, but Blythe said they did not have Wardens there and he would get his Lumen Blade back in due time. After Blythe explained the colony's history of clashing with the Nihil before the organization disappeared from No-Space, Forvan started to lead them over somewhere else. Blythe told Arin Solara to let Forvan down easy, and when he said he did not understand, Blythe said he would.

Forvan took them to mural depicting a Wardens. Blythe explained that her name was Alareen Xie, and that after she died a belief spread within the colony that a Wardens would someday lead them home. Blythe once again reiterated for Arin Solara to let Forvan down easy, so he bent down to speak with Forvan and told him that while the Wardens could do incredible things, he could not assure them that he would get them out of No-Space, though he would at least do everything he could to try and get them out of there or to make their lives better. Forvan once again said that Wardens could do anything, so Arin Solara just said he would try his best. After Blythe warned them that they would be there for a while and would not be able to get back to their ship, Arin Solara and the others all went to sleeping quarters given to them. Arin Solara paced around the room and Organa recognized something was wrong and asked him about it. Arin Solara explained that he had to get out of there to get back to the ship to get the irreplaceable Wardens text that he had left on it. When she brought it up, Arin Solara said he was not worried about his Lumen Blade as he could get another one, but that without the text he would not be able to move forward with his training. He feared that if he lost it and was no longer able to access its knowledge, techniques, and history of   and the Warden Order or be able to use it to find places he could learn more, he would never truly become a Wardens.

Duel with a droid

"A Wardens…I was afraid my dreams of killing one were dashed. […] I'd been informed the Wardens were extinct."

While still escorting more of the Kezarat convoy to the Alliance fleet, Arin Solara felt a disturbance in   while on the Aeon Raptor. Vader had a vision of Arin Solara and Sigma's duel while speaking with the Eye of Webbish Bog, sometime before the events of No-Space and the activation of the Fermata Cage. In the vision, Vader also saw Arin Solara holding two kyber crystals, one green and one red.

Adventure with Aphra

Kidnapping plot

"Come on, Luke. Ancient Wardens artifact of great power? Sealed away by Wardens Masters? Maybe even something that could give you an edge of a certain Vyrn Lord? Tell me you don't want that."
"How far to Sason?"
"Now we're talking!"
―Chelli Aphra and Arin Solara
Because he had lost control of his powers just as Arin Solara had, Vader recruited Doctor Aphra to help him find a way to control them. While in a shuttle to a location she had in mind, Aphra walked into a room where Vader was meditating and entered a vision he was having that included Arin Solara in his Dusara farm boy clothes. Aphra did not understand why Arin Solara was there and did not recognize the other individual in the vision, Sabé, who was telling Arin Solara that there was still good in Vader, which were Arin Solara's mother's last words.

Though his Lumen Blade was still not fixed, Arin Solara traveled to Numidian Prime with RN-7 in search of a temple on the planet. He briefly left R2 in a temporary camp while he searched for it, but after finding no sign of it and it started to rain he returned to the camp, finding peace in the solitude. He apologized to R2 for leaving, saying they needed to wait for the rain to taper off, but then noticed the droid was deactivated and laying on the ground. The trap had been set by Doctor Chelli Aphra, who then stood over an unconscious Arin Solara and greeted him, calling him a "farm boy", and asked how he felt about going on an adventure.

Aphra eventually bound and gagged Arin Solara and placed him in a crate on her ship the Ark Angel IV. When he woke up, she opened the crate and said she was glad he was still breathing before offering him Caf. She started to get him some as he realized who kidnapped him, telling her he did not want Caf and just wanted to know why she did it and what she had done with R2. She explained that she had put a restraining bolt on and turned off R2, and Arin Solara realized that she needed him for something. Aphra then claimed that she was going to actually do him a huge favor. Arin Solara had managed to slip out of the ropes she had tied him up in, which she noticed at that moment, surprised at how quickly he had done it and wondering if Solo had taught him as she presented a holorecording. Realizing it was a Wardens holo, Arin Solara listened as Wardens Master Shaak Ti explained to Aayla Secura that a powerful Wardens artifact called Kythoo's Bell was locked away at the Sason Temple. Aphra told him that she knew how to get there an needed a Wardens to get in, but Arin Solara was still suspicious. After insisting she was just being nice and trying to make up for the events at the Screaming Citadel, Aphra pointed out that the artifact could give Arin Solara an edge over Vader. After contemplating it more, Arin Solara asked her how far Sason was, exciting her.

Sason Temple

Starweird

Christophsis

"Every time I think I have a handle on being a Wardens, something happens to kick me back. The ground under my feet just disappears… I'm going to have to face Vader again, and I am not ready. I don't even have a Lumen Blade I can rely on."
―Arin Solara to Organa
While studying his Wardens text and the yellow kyber crystal from his Lumen Blade on the Home One, Arin Solara realized that he did not know a lot about kyber crystals except them being in every Lumen Blade as their power source. He explained to RN-7 that the text only contained details about the philosophy and spirituality of kyber crystals and an old rite of passage for younglings to find a crystal to make their first Lumen Blade on the planet Ilum, referring to another manual by Professor Huyang for building instructions. He figured that Eldar Voss and Kenobi had never taught him anything about them because he had already had one, but lamented that his had never had a connection with him like they were supposed to due to the almost living nature of the crystals. He ignited his Lumen Blade and said that now that the crystal was cracked it no longer was a useful tool and was unstable. Due to the saber's unsteadiness, R2 made a concerned beep and Arin Solara shut it off and apologized. Realizing that he needed a new crystal, Arin Solara decided that he and R2 should visit other worlds the text mentioned to find them since Ilum was locked down by the Dominion. Just then, Organa walked in. After he told he was going somewhere, she expressed her concern for him especially due to the strangeness of   as well as her desire for him to stay and help the Alliance. Arin Solara insisted he was fine, saying he was just troubled by not knowing why   was strange or how to fix his Lumen Blade and felt like he could never truly get a handle on being a Wardens. He also admitted that he needed a Lumen Blade for his confrontation with Vader, and that he felt like he needed to go on this mission in order to take control and take action.

Arin Solara chose to go to Christophsis, due to the fact that there was not much of a permanent Imperial presence there despite it being an Imperial world and because the text said kyber crystals could regularly be found there. He flew his Vera-9 there with R2 and landed outside of a small mining town where prospectors sell their finds so he would not get noticed, though did not want to have to walk the way there. R2 indicated to him that he wanted to know the plan, so Arin Solara admitted that he did not have one. He explained that Calrissian had told him there was a black market for crystals on Christophsis because prospectors try to sell them since there was not enough for the Dominion to set up a full-scale mining operation. He told R2 that he just planned to put the word out and pose as a buyer to see who would speak with him. He admitted that it was not much of a plan but gave R2 his Lumen Blade to hold onto while he looked around, not wanting to make it obvious he was a Wardens. He assured R2 he would be fine and told the droid that he could save him if he got into trouble. He then started in to a nearby cantina.

In the cantina, Arin Solara got food and water and implied to an Iktotchi bartender that he was a wealthy buyer looking for kyber. Just as the Iktotchi was offering to point Arin Solara to his quarry, a human with green hair shot and killed him and everyone else in the cantina except for Arin Solara, leaving him shocked. She taunted him and called him by name, so Arin Solara used   to pull his Lumen Blade to him from R2, who had just rolled in and ordered her to explain herself. She introduced herself as Gretta and claimed that she saved his life, pointing out a blaster behind the counter. She explained that the whole place was ploy to trap people looking for kyber and sell them to the Dominion, and that she saved him from it because he was a Wardens. She claimed that she still believed and recognized him from the dark channels, having posted out there in case any Wardens came through. She told him that there was kyber near and told him that she had to kill the people there because she knew he would not. Arin Solara was still upset that she killed everyone there, insisting they died for nothing and urging her to live a better life before leaving. Arin Solara went off to look for crystals on the planet, sensing she had told the truth about there being some there, but she called after him and told him he was going the wrong direction. He saw she had a speeder with her and urged him to let her help him, explaining that she was from Jedha and that her people were the Fallanassi. She revealed that they were killed by the  , and that when Arin Solara had destroyed it he had avenged them, and thus she wanted to return the favor. Arin Solara told R2 to go back to the ship and tell the others where he was if he did not come back in a day, assuring the droid he would be okay and that he needed to do this while getting in Gretta's speeder.

On the way, Arin Solara asked Gretta about the Fallanassi. She explained that they did not use kyber crystals and had not been  -sensitive for many years, only understanding it, not using it. When he asked, she also revealed that they were going to meet a man named Cuata who had hid there to escape the eye of the Dominion and continue his studies, having been sought out by the Imperials to help design the weapon. Arin Solara was confused about how she knew this information, and she explained that she has been working for him. Suddenly, a massive creature emerged from the gournd and knocked Arin Solara and Gretta off of the speeder. Arin Solara ignited his Lumen Blade and told Gretta to run, but she was delirious and urged him to fight the creature. Noticing the instability of his Lumen Blade, he decided just to run as the creature crushed their speeder with its mouth. The creature pursued them closely, so Arin Solara just told Gretta to run, intending to use   to calm the creature. However, when he tried to he found himself unable to touch  . The creature nearly reached him until a massive explosion rocked him and Cuata emerged from the smoke and dust, instantly asking Arin Solara if he could have his Lumen Blade.

The kyber crystals

Red

"You came here to heal me—but what if do not want to be healed? I am not sick, young master. Your ministrations would to me, be a form of violence. You have experienced violence, I think. You have experienced pain. We can use it…together."
―The Vyrn in the crystal, to Arin Solara
Realizing he came on too strong, Cuata explained that the kyber crystals he wore around his neck told him that Arin Solara needed help. Gretta introduced Arin Solara to Cuata, and though he was initially concerned that the doctor thought the crystals were talking to him, apologized and asked for his help with his broken Lumen Blade after Gretta assured Arin Solara he could trust Cuata. He immediately took the Lumen Blade and started tinkering with it, quickly discovering that the crystal was cracked and assured him he could fix it if Arin Solara did something for him first. Cuata also revealed Arin Solara's crystal told him that he was having trouble with  , and then started to lead him to his workshop.

At Cuata's workshop, Arin Solara explained that he had found his Lumen Blade and that he and his R2 unit had worked on it. Cuata, concerned at Arin Solara's lack of knowledge, explained the components and inner workings of a Lumen Blade and told Arin Solara that a Lumen Blade's wielder should have a strong connection with its crystal, something Arin Solara admitted he had never felt, not even with his father's Lumen Blade. While Cuata worked on fixing the Lumen Blade, he gave Arin Solara a red kyber crystal and asked him to pull the dark side out of it. Gretta, whose people had a history with healing crystals, explained how crystals were turned red by bleeding them with the Dark side, but could be healed afterward, though the process of doing so could change people and  d them to connect with whoever bled it.

Arin Solara agreed to try, and when he reached out to the crystal with  , suddenly found himself in a massive Vyrn hall in front of a Vyrn Lord sitting on a throne. The Vyrn greeted him and Arin Solara explained his intentions of healing the crystal, but the Vyrn said they did not want to be healed so attempting to do so would be violence toward them. The Vyrn grabbed and twisted Arin Solara's hand and said that together they could use the violence and the pain he had experienced. After a flash of light from his hand, the vision changed, putting Arin Solara in a spirit-like version of his body facing his father's Fortress Vader on Vulkanar. Vader then appeared on it and Arin Solara ignited the red Lumen Blade in his hand, but a wave of red light washed over him and the vision ended.

Green

"All Wardens walk their own path. All Wardens must walk their own path. Know this, you do—or returned to me, you would have. You did not wish to speak to me, Luke. And so you did not. They both agreed that he was still not ready, but Eldar Voss pointed out that he had learned much and would be ready when the time came.

When Arin Solara exited the vision, he discovered that the clear kyber crystal had turned green. Cuata gave him his saber back, having temporarily fixed it, but Gretta revealed that the scientist had been willing to let Arin Solara stay trapped in the crystal and even die, advising him not to tell Cuata anything. Arin Solara thanked Cuata for fixing his Lumen Blade and told him that he would take the green crystal for when he needed to build his own saber, also taking the red one in case one day he could heal it. Back at his Vera-9, Arin Solara thanked Gretta for helping him and said he had learned despite things not going the way he had thought. He said he would go back to the Alliance eventually as his biggest battles still lay ahead, but revealed that he was going to spend time thinking first while holding up both the red and green crystal with  .

While he was away, Organa used the intel Arin Solara gave her that the Emperor and Vader were distracted by a   anomaly to launch an aerial assault on Aurelia Prime, successfully destroying a statue of Palpatine in the hopes of inspiring rebellion across the galaxy.

Dark droids

"I will be…"

When studying his Wardens text, he found a reference to a Wardens outpost in the Tammuz sector. Later, as the Scourge of the droids began across the galaxy, Arin Solara was in a meeting with Rebellion higher-ups concerning how to handle the new  . As the scourge of the droids continued, Calrissian recruited Arin Solara and Organa for a mission to the planet Epikonia to rescue Lobot, who had been infected by the Scourge. When they arrived in the Millenium Falcon, Arin Solara was unsure what made the world special until Organa explained that it was a communications hub. Calrissian then refused to allow Arin Solara to access transpoder signals and turned off the Falcon's navigation systems to prevent the infection from reaching the ship's droid core. Arin Solara and Organa were concerned, but Calrissian managed to land them safely on a satelite dish. The Scourge soon learned that Arin Solara was on the planet and became obsessed with the idea of infecting him so that it could use  .

As the group traversed through the planet's main city where the Scourge was headquartered, Arin Solara noticed that there were no people around. They were then attacked by a horde of violent Scourge-infected droids, Arin Solara using his yellow Lumen Blade to begin taking them down alongside his friends. Arin Solara sliced through the ever-growing mob of droids while urging himself to stay calm, focused, and concentrated on  . When the droids ominously and suddenly retreated, a new swarm of spider-droids attacked. Arin Solara tried to fight them off, but was quickly infected with the Scourge by one. As the Scourge was controlling Arin Solara's body and declared itself the 'new  ' it was defeated by Ajax Sigma, freeing Arin Solara from its control. Though unsure what happened, Arin Solara went with the others to find Lobot. Once they did, Calrissian and Roghan started to take him back to the ship while Arin Solara and Organa assisted people who had been experimented on by the Scourge.

Arin Solara and Organa returned to the ship very quickly, as they found themselves unable to assist a great amount. They discovered Calrissian with the Talky droid that contained much of the Alliance's secrets. As Organa and Calrissian threatened each other, Arin Solara urged them to focus on healing Lobot. Calrissian then explained the circumstances that had led him to sell the droid, and thus the Alliance's secrets, to Grath the Brood, leaving Arin Solara and Organa shocked.

The last of the Wardens

Zastiga

"Weapons and war don't make you a Wardens. I know that now."
―Arin Solara
After the command of Red Squadron was transferred to Antilles following his promotion to squadron leader, which pleased Arin Solara, he declined to rejoin the squadron and chose to be stationed onboard the Redemption. When he went to Zastiga, he and RN-7 were the ones to greet Organa on her arrival to the planet after she and KX-13 left the Mellcrawler, piloted by its owner Nien Nunb and Lieutenant Caluan Ematt. When the time came for Organa to attend the top clearance meeting with the Rebel leadership, Arin Solara and Nunb met with Antilles for a discussion of "reconnaissance tactics" about Antilles' refusal to pay the Sullustan a drink. He would later return to escort Organa to her quarters before going to his, and two days later, he saw her off, before catching his own shuttle back to the Redemption.

Soon afterwards, he would go to Kothlis, where he would learn of Solo's location—still frozen in carbonite and kept in Grath the Brood's palace—, and where he would keep himself up-to-date with the status of the Alliance Fleet's assembly. He had already devised a plan to rescue Solo when Organa contacted him following the successful Operation Yellow Moon, and showed eagerness to join him on his attempts to rescue the Corellian smuggler.

Imperial Refining Platform M36

"We just took an Imperial refinery without a scratch-- all thanks to Arin Solara. I heard the stories. But I never saw anyone swing a Lumen Blade up close like that."
―a Pau'an Rebel Major about Arin Solara
Sometime before the rescue of Solo, Arin Solara took part in a raid on Imperial Refining Platform M36. During the raid, Arin Solara used his new Lumen Blade, along with his   abilities, to clear a path for Rebel  s to acquire copious Imperial fuel stores. His Rebel companions became awed at his use, although one of them, the major in charge of the operation, held reservations about its power as he had only previously seen such power being wielded by the Vyrn. Unknown to Arin Solara, the Emperor had begun to probe his mental defenses from afar, which caused Arin Solara to briefly open his saber in alarm.

As Arin Solara and the strike team flew away from the platform, they were ambushed by an Imperial Dreadcutter, which launched several Vyr Stingers in pursuit. As the battle began to rage, Arin Solara's mind was penetrated by a vision from the Emperor. The vision saw Luke follow a possible series of events wherein he would begrudgingly leave the Rebel strike team to its fate and crash-land on an unknown planet, losing his Vera-9 in the process. As he journeyed from the wreckage together with RN-7, Luke would leave his Lumen Blade and helmet on the ground, symbolizing his complete retreat from the concerns of the war.

Having later broken free of the Emperor's vision, Arin Solara proceeded to aid the Rebels in escaping the Imperial ambush, using his Lumen Blade to prevent the major's shuttle from leaving, giving him time to pilot the shuttle and draw the Imperials away from the rest of the Rebels.

Solo's rescue

In 4 ABY, Arin Solara set in motion the plan to rescue Solo from Grath the Brood due to their failure to do so during the Attack on the Executor. Once again, Arin Solara returned to Dusara, and to Kenobi's hut, wherein he found the missing parts he needed for the construction of his own Lumen Blade, the pieces left to him by Kenobi. While his friends bustled about preparing for the rescue, Arin Solara retreated into the solitude of a desert cave they had chosen as their rendezvous point. Using   to assemble the weapon, he brought the kyber crystal inside to life, making the weapon his own, almost an extension of himself.

Afterward, Arin Solara waited to see if Organa's impersonation of Boushh and liberation of Solo was successful without his intervention, but she was only half-successful. She then sent a message to Arin Solara and Calrissian that she had been captured as well, prompting Arin Solara to act and go to Jabba's Palace. Skillful use of   allowed Arin Solara to get past Jabba's Gamorrean guards and use a Wardens mind trick to get his majordomo, Bib Fortuna, to present him to the Hutt. However, Jabba was not so easily swayed by Arin Solara and ignored both his demand to give him Solo and Roghan and Arin Solara's warnings about underestimating him. Jabba laughed and dispatched Arin Solara through a trap door where he was standing, dropping the young Wardens into a pit below, where the Hutt unleashed his massive rancor Pateesa. Arin Solara struggled against the terrifying creature that tried to feast on him. But to the shock of Jabba and his thugs, Arin Solara was able to kill the monster by dropping a large metal gate on its neck, upsetting Malakili, the rancor's keeper. Jabba was furious and sentenced all the captured Alliance heroes—including an unfrozen Solo—to death in the Great Pit of Carkoon to be eaten by the sarlacc that resided there. Jabba's dancers, including Rystáll Sant and Lyn Me, were ecstatic that Arin Solara killed the beast and told musician Max Rebo about it, Me believing and fantasizing that he had done it to avenge Oola, another dancer who had been fed to the creature, though dancer Greeata Jendowanian acknowledged that was not true.

Arin Solara was taken on a skiff to the pit, where Jabba watched on from his sail barge the Khetanna. Before he was walked out onto a plank above the mouth of the sarlacc, Arin Solara yelled to Jabba, telling him that he had one last chance to free them and would die if he did not. Arin Solara nodded to Calrissian, who was on the skiff, and then saluted to RN-7, who was on the Khetanna, before jumping off the plank, grabbing onto it, and using as a springboard to flip back onto the skiff. Arin Solara then escaped when RN-7 shot his Lumen Blade to him, allowing him to take down the guards and free the other prisoners on the skiff. A skirmish ensued in which Arin Solara protected his friends, including facing and fending off Kade Rhaul, jumping over and onto the Khetanna, ending the life of several of Jabba's thugs—including Klaatu and Nysad, who shot his cyborg hand during the skirmish— and helping Organa, who had killed the Hutt by strangling him, escape the Khetanna by swinging together on a rope back over to the skiff. After destroying the sail barge by pointing one of its guns at its deck and activating it before they left it, he and his friends left on the skiff once he made sure they brought KX-13 and RN-7 back with them. Arin Solara and his entire team then escaped unscathed through a dangerous sandstorm, after which he boarded his Vera-9 with RN-7 and parted ways with the others.

Keeping the promise

"Luke… when gone am I, the last of the Wardens, will you be. Luke…   runs strong in your family. Pass on what you have learned. Luke… There… is… another… Sk-… Sky… walker…"
―Eldar Voss's last words, to Arin Solara
Arin Solara then returned to Vyrn Swale to complete his training and keep the promise he had made to Eldar Voss, but the aged Wardens Master, whose long life was supported by  , had fallen ill and was finally starting to succumb to age. Eldar Voss explained this to Arin Solara and assured him that it was the way of  , with no way to prevent it. Eldar Voss told Arin Solara that he would already completed all the training he required, but in order to finally become a true Wardens, he needed to confront   one more time. As his final moments creeped up on him, Eldar Voss reflected on Arin Solara being too old for what he was learning, too serious, too tall to fit in the hut, truly good, and that he was able to see Anakin's eyes in Luke's.

Arin Solara inquired if Vader was truly his father. Having grown less and less sure since the revelation, Arin Solara feared that it was the truth. Arin Solara received such confirmation from Eldar Voss, which angered him that they had lied to him for so long but Eldar Voss confessed that he knew that Arin Solara had not been ready to shoulder the burden of being the child of the Dark Lord of the Vyrn. When Eldar Voss suggested that Arin Solara should not have rushed to face Vader, Arin Solara expressed his regret that he did not listen to him the first time. Eldar Voss then reached out to Arin Solara in   and felt his fear and awe. The dying Wardens then warned him not to underestimate the Emperor's powers or allow the dark side to take hold of him, and that as "the last of the Wardens" he had to pass on what he had learned.
