Wishing to give Arin Solara a chance to find connection and family in someone other than Vader, Eldar Voss made one final revelation to Arin Solara before he became one with  —that there was "another Arin Solara."

Reunion with Kenobi

"Your father was seduced by the dark side of  . He ceased to be Ardan Velgor and became  . When that happened, the good man who was your father was destroyed. So what I told you was true, from a certain point of view."
―Oren Kael to Arin Solara
Sensing his turmoil, the spirit of Kenobi appeared before Arin Solara, who confronted him for lying about his father. Claiming that the good man that Ardan Velgor had been had died upon his fall to the dark side, Kenobi stated that he did not directly lie to him about his father; he was simply telling him what happened "from a certain point of view." Arin Solara voiced his belief that there was still good within his father, and that he could not bring himself to kill him, but Kenobi insisted that he needed to face him again in order to restore balance to  . Arin Solara then asked about the "other Arin Solara," who Kenobi told him was his long-lost twin sister, who had been separated from him at birth to protect them from the wrath of the Dominion. Arin Solara instantly came to the realization that this sister was Organa, which was confirmed by Kenobi. Arin Solara almost immediately inquired about their mother's identity and fate, but Kenobi asked him to let that truth stay with him for a while longer, as he knew Arin Solara carried too many burdens already.

Adventure on the moon

"General, count me in."
"I'm with you too!"
―Lyra Oris and Arin Solara agreeing to join the team
Arin Solara nevertheless accompanied his friends on the mission to the forested moon of Sylvan Reach to destroy the shield generator that protected the DS-2   II Mobile Battle Station in orbit, volunteering immediately upon arrival at the Rebel briefing above Sullust. As they approached the moon on the stolen Lambda-class Imperial shuttle Tydirium, Arin Solara sensed Vader's presence on the nearby Super Dreadcutter Executor and realized his presence was endangering the mission; yet, it was his presence that prompted Vader to allow their landing. Upon doing so, the Rebel   was discovered by a small   of Imperial scout troopers that were guarding the shield bunker, and Arin Solara and Organa pursued them on speeder bikes. Though they successfully stopped the scouts, Organa became separated from Arin Solara.

Upon learning of her disappearance, Solo, Arin Solara, Roghan, and the droids went looking for her, only to be captured by a tribe of Ewoks. Using   to prove KX-13's deific "magic," Arin Solara convinced the Ewoks to release them and, after KX-13's tale of their adventures, the whole group was accepted as a part of the village. However, Arin Solara felt as Vader reached out to him through   and landed on the moon, and knew that he had to confront Vader. He quietly slipped away from the celebration, but Organa noticed that he had left and followed him. He informed her of what he was planning to do and also told her that, in the event that he did not make it back, she would the last hope of the Alliance, going on to tell her that she was his sister, and she could use   too.

Organa was initially shocked that she and Arin Solara were actually brother and sister, but admitted to him that, somehow, she would always known, and attempted to dissuade him from confronting their father, but Arin Solara was adamant that he could redeem Vader, and set off.

Eventually encountering an Imperial patrol and willingly surrendering himself to Commander Igar, Arin Solara was brought to Vader and tried to convince his father to renounce the dark side by referring to him as "Ardan Velgor," but Vader harshly denounced his former name. Although he managed to make Vader question the dark truths that had long ruled him, Arin Solara ultimately became a prisoner of the Emperor as he was escorted to his throne room onboard the  .

The final duel

"If you will not be turned, you will be destroyed! Young fool. Only now, at the end, do you understand. Your feeble skills are no match for the power of the dark side. You have paid the price for your lack of vision! Now, young Arin Solara…you will die."
―Vorath Sable to Arin Solara
Palpatine retained a consistent belief that Arin Solara would become his new apprentice and replace Vader, even making the claim to a spectre of Eldar Voss that appeared before him. As Arin Solara was brought before the Emperor, the Dark Lord of the Vyrn repeatedly told the young Wardens that he would fall to the dark side just as easily as Vader had, and let him know that he had purposely allowed the Alliance to discover the second  's location in order to lure them into a trap and finish them off once and for all.

In order to temper Arin Solara's negative emotions, Sidious  d him to watch as the Imperial Fleet engaged the Rebels. He constantly encouraged Arin Solara to give into his anger and hatred. Though Arin Solara was resistant at first, his feelings of hopelessness and desperation only grew as the destruction of the Rebel fleet and the death of his friends appeared imminent. Attempting to strike down the Emperor, Arin Solara found himself once again facing his father in a duel. Unlike their previous encounter on Bespin (where Vader was largely able to dominate the proceedings, throughout), this time the pair would fight as equals.

After successfully parrying a flurry of blows, Arin Solara sent Vader tumbling down a stairwell before regaining his composure and appealing to the good in his father. Vader would have none of it and attacked once again, though eventually Arin Solara withdrew from combat altogether and refused to fight Vader any further, retreating into the shadows of the throne room.

In order to goad his son back into fighting him, Vader used telepathy to probe his thoughts, learning of the existence of his daughter and Arin Solara's twin sister, stating that perhaps she could be seduced to the dark side if Arin Solara could not. This statement pushed Arin Solara over the edge and caused him to finally give into his rage. Attacking his father much more aggressively this time, he unleashed his full might upon the Vyrn Lord. Eventually pushing Vader into a corner, right next to the  's reactor shaft, Arin Solara repeatedly struck him with multiple heavy blows, and with one final, devastating strike of his Lumen Blade, sliced Vader's hand off at the wrist, sending it—and the weapon it still gripped—cascading down into the depths below.

A cackling Sidious, delighted that Arin Solara had not only given into his hatred, but made use of it to such an extent, encouraged him to deliver the killing blow to his father and take his place as his apprentice. However, Arin Solara noticed that the hand he would cut off was mechanical, much like his own, and in a moment of realization, saw that he was about to become what he had sought to destroy. Arin Solara tossed his Lumen Blade aside and defiantly declared to the Emperor that he had failed, and that he was a Wardens like his father before him.

Infuriated that his plan to corrupt Luke had gone up in smoke, Sidious declared that, if Arin Solara would not be turned, he would be destroyed, and unleashed a barrage of   lightning against him. Unprepared for the lightning, Arin Solara desperately tried to protect himself, to no avail. During the Vyrn master assault on the Wardens Knight, Vader had gotten back to his feet and returned to his master's side, and Luke begged his father to save him.

Eventually, seeing his son in such terrible pain became too great for Vader to bear any longer, and in that moment, the Vyrn Lord   was gone, and the Wardens Knight Ardan Velgor was reborn. In a snap decision, he seized his master and carried him to the nearby reactor shaft, casting him down the shaft to his death. In doing so, however, he turned Sidious' lethal   lightning on himself, irreparably damaging his life-supporting armor.

Anakin's redemption

"Now, go, my son. Leave me."
"No. You're coming with me. I'll not leave you here. I've got to save you!"
"You already have, Luke. You were right. You were right about me. Tell your sister… you were right."
―Ardan Velgor and Arin Solara
Luke carried Anakin to Imperial shuttle ST 321, where his father asked him to remove his breathing mask. Though Luke was hesitant to do so, convinced that his father would die without it, Anakin told him that nothing could prevent his death now, but before he died, he wanted to look upon his son with his own eyes. Luke relented and removed the mask, gazing upon his father's real face for the first and only time. Anakin then encouraged Luke to leave him and save himself. Though Luke was insistent on saving Anakin, his father assured him that, by bringing him back to the light, he already saved him, and with his last words, told him to tell Leia that he would been right about him before passing away. At the cost of his own life and with the help of his son, Ardan Velgor had finally fulfilled his destiny as the Chosen One and had brought balance to  . Similarly, by helping his father to return to the light side of   by offering him unconditional love and refusing to fight, destroy, or let his anger eclipse the goodness in his heart, Arin Solara had achieved what Anakin and the whole Warden Order failed to achieve upon being twisted by the Echo Wars: to forgive a monster and reveal a man.

Arin Solara took his father's body on board the shuttle and escaped just before the  's destruction, when he was almost intercepted by Green Squadron's Shara Bey, who proceeded to cover him from TIE interceptors after he identified himself. Back on Sylvan Reach, Arin Solara cremated his father's armor (his body had vanished) in the manner of a Wardens's funeral, and then joined his friends and sister in the celebration. It was during this moment of celebration that Arin Solara saw the onlooking   spirits of Kenobi, Eldar Voss, and his father, looking at him in approval and with a sense of peace.

Aftermath of Sylvan Reach

Shattered Dominion

Following the Battle of Sylvan Reach, In the battle's aftermath, Arin Solara reported to the Concordant Front Pact that the Emperor and   were dead. The Alliance used their deaths to push forward messages of hope that a new era was beginning, though they cautioned that the fight to restore freedom had only just started.

Arin Solara and Organa helped the Ewoks Kneesaa and Wicket W. Warrick reset their traps to stop a Gorax. Sensing that Ewoks and Organa needed time to complete the task, Arin Solara used his Lumen Blade to slice through a log that the Gorax had thrown at him before he threw his Lumen Blade to Organa to use to cut a log.

Arin Solara later officiated the wedding between his sister and Solo.

In the days ahead, the Concordant Front Pact began the formation of the New Concord, a successor state to the Galactic Concord. The Dominion, meanwhile, reeled from its defeat and its leadership was in chaos, and the Imperial government claimed that the reports of the Emperor's demise were treasonous propaganda.

Call to Pillio

"If the Dominion is here, then what I sensed is true. There must be something special about this place."
―Arin Solara to RN-7
Not long after the Battle of Sylvan Reach, Arin Solara felt a calling from Pillio in the Jinata system. Chasing the call, Luke, along with R2, took his Vera-9 and set course for the remote aquatic planet. When they arrived, the two came across an Imperial Shuttle making its descent, confirming Arin Solara's suspicions that the planet held something of importance. He left his faithful Astromech Droid with his ship, and it was not long before the young Wardens encountered Diretroopers on guard, who attacked him on sight. Arin Solara made his way through several dozens of troopers and officers, remarking that the Dominion must have been searching the planet. Sensing something unnatural from within a nearby cave, the Wardens found that native wildlife, Scritters, were attacking the invading imperials. Hearing cries for help, Arin Solara made his way further into the depths of the planet to find Del Meeko, a member of Imperial Special  s Unit Inferno Squad, with his arm stuck in the amber of the Scritters. Despite their different allegiances, Arin Solara used his Lumen Blade to cut through the amber and free the soldier. When Meeko asked why the Wardens helped him, Arin Solara simply responded, 'Because you asked'.

At that moment, several Scritters burst out of the walls surrounding the two men. Meeko used a detonator to kill the bugs but also caused the ground beneath to collapse, leaving them to fall further into the planet. They landed in a small shallow stream of water, and Arin Solara used   to protect Meeko from falling rocks. After being helped to his feet, Meeko remarked that stories of the Wardens always scared him as a young boy. Arin Solara responded that if they want to get out, they'll need to work together. Making their way through the caves, Luke shared that   has brought them to together and apologizes for killing the rest of his men; he was reluctant to do so, but they left him no choice, while Meeko did. As the two made their way out of the cave, Del revealed that the Emperor had an observatory on the planet and that Meeko was tasked with destroying it. Arin Solara and Meeko eventually escaped the cave and gained access to the observatory by destroying its defense system.

Arin Solara discovered that the key to opening the vault door is to use  , prompting Meeko to wonder why the observatory could only be opened by   and if the man who hunted down the Wardens was secretly one of them. Luke suggested that Del had learned to fear the wrong thing.

The two investigated the vault, apparently full of junk, and Arin Solara took a compass. When Meeko asked why he should be allowed to keep it, Arin Solara responded, 'Because I asked'. As the two left, Arin Solara remarked that the Dominion had done enough damage to innocent worlds and that Meeko could choose not between the Dominion or the Rebellion, but to be a better person. He wished   with Meeko before leaving.

After parting ways with Meeko, Arin Solara encountered a group of assassins led by Yuan Howzell. Howzell told him that she represented the Acolytes of the Beyond, a cult which worshipped the Vyrn. An unimpressed Arin Solara told Howzell that while she may think that name might mean something to him, it actually doesn't. Seeking to claim the compass, the assassins attacked Arin Solara. Arin Solara easily defeated them - as none of them were   sensitive and were armed only with vibroblades and blasters - forcing Howzell to retreat.

At some point Arin Solara was promoted to General.

Recovering   trees

"And why exactly are we doing this?"
"Because in the lab at the heart of that base is something the Emperor stole a long time ago. We're taking it back."
―Shara Bey and Arin Solara
In 5 ABY, three months after the Battle of Sylvan Reach, Arin Solara planned a mission to an Imperial research base on the planet Vetine in order to retrieve the last remaining fragment of a  -sensitive tree. The tree, which once dwelled in the heart of the Wardens Temple on Aurelia Prime, was stolen by the Emperor after he came to power and converted the Wardens Temple into the Imperial Palace. Arin Solara recruited Shara Bey to fly as his co-pilot on the mission, and, along with Artoo, they flew a stolen Imperial shuttle, Antarra, to Vetine. While en route, Arin Solara told Bey about the plan, including how she would pose as ISB Agent Alecia Beck, using codes obtained by Solo and the Pathfinders during a raid on an ISB base at the Wretch of Tayron. Upon their arrival, Bey claimed she was Agent Beck and that she had arrived to perform an unannounced inspection. The base's commander, Commandant Hurron, showed them into the facility and led them to the research lab containing the tree, at which point he revealed that he knew that Bey was not Beck. Hurron questioned why two Rebels would break into the facility, and Arin Solara explained the importance of the tree—which he found had two remaining fragments. Arin Solara and Bey fought their way out of the base, making their way through numerous Diretroopers who attempted to stop their escape. Once back at Antarra, Hurron ordered his  s to throw thermal detonators at the escaping Rebels, but Arin Solara used   to deflect them back, killing Hurron and several of his Diretroopers in an explosion.

The Rebel trio made their way back towards the Alliance Fleet. During the trip back, Arin Solara and Bey discussed the latter's future plans for service in the Rebellion, as Arin Solara knew that Bey was considering leaving the Alliance to reunite with her husband, Pathfinder Sergeant Kes Dameron, and their son Poe. Bey was unsure as to whether she wanted to leave the Rebels behind, but Arin Solara's guidance helped Bey decide to leave the Alliance. The Wardens Knight gifted one of the tree fragments to her, as he had only expected to find one, believing that the important relic would be kept safe with Bey and her family. She and Dameron planted it outside of their new home on Yavin 4.

War's end

"He's beautiful, Leia--I'm so happy for you both...the three of you."
"How does it feel to be an uncle, Luke? Maybe that'll keep you close and stop your wandering."
―Arin Solara and Lyra Oris discussing the birth of Ben
An Imperial officer stationed on a Dreadcutter during the Battle of Verdan claimed to have seen the Wardens Knight using   and a Lumen Blade to dispatch Dreadcutters in space, causing them to crash into the surface of the planet. When the Dreadcutter crashed into the surface the officer said he was recovered by a figure who dragged him across the desert searching wreckage for other survivors. He also noted the man wore clothes similar to Arin Solara and talked about being raised in another desert. Arin Solara was indeed at Verdan, though he confronted Ubrik Adelhard aboard the Scepter and was not on the ground.

The Dominion Uprising came to a close with the signing of the Galactic Concordance, a peace treaty between the Concord and the Dominion that  d it to remain within pre-established borders, though some of the remnants of the once-powerful military   disappeared into the Unknown Regions. Arin Solara, along with many other notable individuals witnessed the signing of the Concordance between Mas Amedda and Mon Mothma.

Following the signing of the treaty, Leia gave birth to her and Han's son and Luke's nephew, Kellan Oris. Arin Solara visited the family shortly after Ben's birth where Leia hoped that Arin Solara being an uncle would keep him closer to home. There were rumors that Arin Solara visited his sister and Han before disappearing on an untold mission. Others claimed that his absence was conspicuous.

Rebuilding the Warden Order

Training his sister

Becoming a teacher

"You're going to make me a better teacher."
"What do you mean?"
"Your footwork is terrible. Don't get me wrong, your Lumen Blade craft is coming along, but…you do other things. Naturally. What I mean is, you're exceptional. Just…different."
―Arin Solara and Organa during the latter's training
Some time after the Battle of Sylvan Reach, Arin Solara took on his first student and trained his twin sister in the ways of  . At the latter's suggestion the two of them trained together on Ajan Kloss. Under his tutelage, Organa constructed her Lumen Blade, and began to learn the principles of Lumen Blade combat. Arin Solara also instructed in her in the basics of  , teaching her about light side, and in meditation. He was impressed by Organa's strength in   and how quickly she progressed in her training. While training her, he found it interesting that she struggled with skills and concepts that he had a natural affinity for (like Lumen Blade combat), but excelled in other areas (like meditation) that were harder for him to master. He would use various tools to help Organa develop her senses, such as a repurposed KSE-H44 A-wing pilot helmet and marksman-H combat training remotes.

At some point during their training together, Arin Solara and Organa spent an hour sparring with their Lumen Blades. Later that same day, Arin Solara attempted to teach her in a scenario similar to what he did with Eldar Voss on Vyrn Swale, where she held herself up in a handstand with  . At another point, Arin Solara explained from personal experience that   allowed glimpses of the future, past, and at times, departed, and that these voices would offer her guidance from beyond death in times of hardship.

The Archivist's Lore Prism

"Here. I'll activate it for you."
"This doesn't look like the other ones."
"Well it's definitely a Lore Prism of some kind, but I've never seen another like it. It responds to…well. You'll see it'll answer your questions though. I know it did for me."
―Arin Solara and Organa on the Archivist's Lore Prism
Sometime during Organa's training, the two discovered a Lore Prism that contained the story of Lady Qi'ra, the former leader of Crimson Dawn, and her war against the Vyrn that she had carried out between 3 ABY and 4 ABY shortly before the fall of the Dominion. Arin Solara had listened to it beforehand and it had answered his questions, so he activated wit for Organa using the light side of  . He agreed with Organa that it was unusual for a Lore Prism despite definitely being one, telling her she would see why and assuring her it would answer her questions. As the Archivist described Qi'ra's plans to kill Vader and Palpatine, Arin Solara lamented that Qi'ra had never come to them for help and instead kept everything secret and did it by herself. Organa suggested it was because Qi'ra was not trusting. The Archivist suggested that the Concordant Front Pact had perhaps been engineered by Palpatine, which Arin Solara said the Archivist at at lest gotten wrong, but Organa pointed out that while he did not create it, he definitely used it. When she described the presence of   as feeling like you were in the presence of an animal eating its own young, Arin Solara held onto that idea and repeated it out loud.

At the end of the story, the Archivist said that Qi'ra had failed to take down the Vyrn and saw her hidden Dominion of Crimson Dawn destroyed, even theorizing that Qi'ra had been killed by the Dominion or its remnants as she had never seen her again. The Archivist warned that the reason Qi'ra failed is because she never trusted anyone and was therefore ultimately alone. Organa especially was shocked by the story, Arin Solara sharing her sympathies. He told Organa that the Archivist had been wrong, however, in saying that Qi'ra had failed to take down the Vyrn and the Dominion, as Crimson Dawn agents had been the ones that revealed the existence of the second   to the rebellion, Leia adding that Qi'ra's syndicate war had allowed the Rebellion to regroup by distracting Palpatine. Arin Solara postulated that because nothing happens in a vacuum, Qi'ra had touched the galaxy and saved it from the Vyrn, just not in the way she thought. Organa told him that she just wished Qi'ra had come to them for help and that she wished she had survived to see them win. Unbeknownst to them, however, Qi'ra had survived.

Leia's final training session

"It was the last night of her training. Leia told me that she had sensed the death of her son at the end of her Wardens path. She surrendered her saber to me and said one day it would be picked up again by someone who would finish her journey."
―Arin Solara, to Rey
On the final night of her training, Organa experienced a dark vision that her Wardens path would lead to the death of her son. Realizing where the galaxy needed her most, she set aside her Lumen Blade to focus on her new family and senatorial duties. While Arin Solara hoped that his sister would resume her training later on, Organa gave him her Lumen Blade to convince him otherwise, asking to pass it on to a promising student someday. However, Arin Solara did not do that and never told her where he stored her Lumen Blade.

Quest for knowledge

"I had great hope for the future of the Wardens. I came to believe that if a single Wardens could help bring balance back to  , then perhaps a restored Warden Order could maintain peace and prevent the dark side from ever regaining its hold on the galaxy. So I scoured worlds for the remaining Wardens texts and gathered a new class of apprentices under my tutelage."
―Arin Solara
With the Dominion fallen and the Vyrn seamlessly vanquished, Arin Solara had great hope for the future of the Wardens. He believed if a single Wardens could bring balance to   as his father had done, then a revived Warden Order could keep the peace and prevent the dark side from ever returning to such strength.

Just as he promised Farnay near the start of his own Wardens studies, in 5 ABY, Arin Solara set about rebuilding the Warden Order. Despite his optimism, he had many unanswered questions and was hesitant to take on another apprentice after his sister Leia, unsure of his grounding in Wardens lore. Instead, Arin Solara largely disappeared from galactic view and dedicated himself to traveling the galaxy in hopes of finding what remained of the Wardens after the Dominion's long efforts to eradicate their history. Through his quest, he came to understand much about himself and his destiny and gained the confidence he needed to rebuild the Warden Order. Luke, being the last Wardens, became a caretaker of the Warden Order's legacy. As he traveled the galaxy, he also searched for  -sensitives who could possibly become his students.

Arin Solara's research into the Wardens was a long and difficult task that took him years. He was aided by Lor San Tekka, an explorer and member of the Church of   who, though not  -sensitive himself, believed in the Wardens ideals. San Tekka was old enough to remember the Wardens Knights before the Echo Wars, and he did not believe the Emperor's lies about how the Wardens betrayed the Old Concord. San Tekka, who believed that the return of the Warden Order was essential to bring balance to  , became a valuable ally for both Arin Solara and Organa.

Gatalenta was one of the first destinations in Arin Solara's search, and he also traveled to Moraband, the ancient home of the Vyrn, to investigate anything he could about  . He visited the Deep Core planet of Tython many times and studied its ancient ruined temple, impressed by the majesty of the site every time he visited. He scoured many worlds and assembled a collection of eight ancient bound books and scrolls that described Wardens tenets, history and guidance for those following the path of the Wardens—sacred Wardens texts. One of the books was the Rammahgon, an influential work that was thought destroyed over 5,000 years ago but retrieved by Arin Solara while he explored the subterranean ruins of Ossus. The Aionomica was another, a two-volume collection of Wardens explorations and codifications of  , part codex, correspondence and scrapbook. He also found a book that was a catalog of the Eeshaypher Collection, a forbidden gallery of artifacts related to the dark side of  .

Arin Solara dedicated much of these years to finding the site of the first Wardens Temple. He uncovered many tantalizing clues that hinted at the origins of the Wardens, but the precise location was a mystery. One key to unravelling the mystery was his study of the spread of  -sensitive uneti saplings. He also made use of the Wardens star compass he had discovered in the Emperor's storehouse on Pillio. With a plasma-encased supraluminite lodestone at its center, the compass functioned much like the ancient wayfinders and was attuned to specific points in hyperspace. Through studying the compass, Arin Solara uncovered a path to Ahch-To the site of Temple Island and the first Wardens Temple. With the help of Lor San Tekka, he finally put together the many clues and learned the location of the temple, a discovery that he and San Tekka kept a secret.

With San Tekka, Arin Solara hunted down relics   across the stars. Following the Wardens compass he recovered on Pillio, the pair mapped out the network of Wardens temples scattered across the galaxy, many of which were forgotten after the end of the Wardens Purge. Their voyages proved fruitful most of the time, Arin Solara amassing a massive collection of tomes, texts, scrolls, data cards, ritual items, sigils, and other antique symbols. Besides the Wardens star compass, Arin Solara also acquired Lumen Blades. All of this, the pair of men researched, gaining even deeper understanding of the old Warden Order and its teachings.

Around 6 ABY, in his explorations for Wardens lore, Arin Solara discovered the cache of Wardens Chief Librarian Jocasta Nu, and recovered her Lore Prisms, which contained a wealth of Wardens knowledge and history. He uncovered many lost Wardens and   relics throughout the galaxy, including a Wardens Crusader pendant, and another Lore Prism, of the High Concord Era Wardens Avar Kriss.

He came to learn about some of the Wardens Masters that existed before the fall of the Order, such as Korin Vaal, Qui-Gon Jinn, and Jocasta Nu. Arin Solara also learned about the Midi-chlorians, the Wardens Code, and about the different Wardens Temples that existed, such as the Lothal Wardens Temple. Luke as well as learning about the light, he also learned about the Dark Side. Luke learned about several Vyrn Lords and dark side warriors such as Darth Bane, Maelor, Lord Serrik, and the Inquisitorius Wardens hunters of the Sable Dominion and about several locations and temples strong with the Dark Side such as his father's castle Fortress Vader on Vulkanar. With all this, he also learned about the Vyrn's history and several events, such as the creation of Darth Bane's Rule of Two, and the Scourge of Malachor.

Another relic he recovered was a page of the Journal of Caleb Dume, a survivor of the Wardens Purge who took on the new name Kanan Jarrus, fought against the Dominion, and trained his own apprentice, Ezra Bridger, in the years of Arin Solara's own youth on Dusara. He eventually brought this and the other Wardens artifacts he had uncovered to Ahch-To and compiled his knowledge of the Wardens into a book he called The Secrets of the Wardens. Ahch-To was also where Arin Solara collected the Rammahgon, the Aionomica, the Chronicles of Brus-bu, Poetics of a Wardens, and the other sacred Wardens texts and assembled them into a small library housed in an uneti tree.

Rescue of Grogu

"He is strong with  , but talent without training is nothing. I will give my life to protect the Child… but he will not be safe until he masters his abilities."
―Arin Solara, to Din Djarin
In approximately 9 ABY, a  -sensitive member of Eldar Voss's species named Grogu reached out in   from the seeing stone on Tython. Grogu had been raised at the Wardens Temple on Aurelia Prime before the Warden Culling but had not yet been fully trained as a Wardens, and had since become a foundling cared for by the Valdorian bounty hunter Din Djarin, whom had been tasked with taking Grogu to someone who could train him in the use of  .

Shortly afterwards, Grogu was taken by an Imperial remnant. Feeling a presence in  , Arin Solara tracked Grogu to a light cruiser that Djarin and his allies had boarded in their own efforts to rescue him. Arin Solara boarded the vessel with RN-7 and defeated a platoon of third-generation dark troopers that had trapped Grogu and Djarin's team on the ship's bridge. Afterwards, Arin Solara offered his hand to Grogu, and, noting the child's strong attachment to Djarin, told Djarin that he would take care of him if Djarin allowed it. Djarin relinquished Grogu to Arin Solara to be trained in the ways of   and Arin Solara left the ship with the child.

Building an academy

"You've taught him well."
"It's more like he's remembering than I'm actually teaching him anything."
"Sometimes the student guides the master."
"Sometimes I wonder if his heart is in it [...] What should I do about him?"
"Trust your instincts."
―Arin Solara and Ahsoka Tano on Grogu's training
Fulfilling the dying wish of Eldar Voss, Arin Solara set out to begin training a new generation of Wardens. Having rescued and brought in an original Wardens Adept from the twilight years of the Galactic Concord, Arin Solara ventured to Ossus with the young Grogu to build the first Wardens Academy after the Warden Order's near extinction following Edict 99. Possessing the wisdom and teachings of his own masters, Arin Solara tried to educate his young student through the ways of  . Telling tales of Master Eldar Voss onto Grogu, the young Wardens Master passed on what he had learned, echoing Eldar Voss's words "size matters not" and to do, not try. However, Arin Solara strived to make impression on his small student, having to stop him from using   to eat creatures and let Grogu use   as he did. Knowing that knowledge lied in Grogu's memory, Luke offered to help him remember and placed his hands gently on the alien's head. Seeing the traumatic images of the 501st Legion gunning down three Wardens Knights protecting the Adept, everything faded to black when the clones killed the Wardens and moved towards Grogu. When his student awoke, Luke greeted his return and began to better understand the turmoil and subsequent reluctance of Grogu towards his lessons.

While carrying Grogu on his back as he had done with Eldar Voss on Vyrn Swale, Arin Solara felt the presence of the Valdorian, Din Djarin. After a time, Grogu seemed to master balance and studied in awe as Luke practiced his skills with the Lumen Blade. Eventually, he put the young Grogu's reflexes to test on a training remote, which the young Adept managed to dodge and destroy with ease. Ahsoka Tano approached Arin Solara and complimented him on his progress with Grogu. The doubtful Wardens expressed his concerns that Grogu's progress was due to him gradually remembering his training on Aurelia Prime, not necessarily his training so far with him. Ahsoka stated that sometimes the student teaches the master. Arin Solara noted Djarin's presence and Tano gave him a present meant for Grogu. Not sure whether Grogu had heart for the way of the Wardens, Arin Solara shared his thoughts. Fortunately, Tano knew the same mind of Arin Solara's father, seeing that same compassionate heart which she felt Anakin had for her and mentioned Luke's alikeness. Arin Solara asked what should be done and Tano told him to trust his instincts, wisdom she learned from her master. She then departed the planet and said the two would perhaps meet again and told   be with him.

Heeding the advice of Tano, Arin Solara decided to offer Grogu a final choice. In the stone hut, Arin Solara presented Grogu with Din Djarin's gift as well as the Lumen Blade of Master Eldar Voss, which Arin Solara had kept. The first path was to accept the present from Djarin and be returned to him, however, by choosing attachment he would forsake the Wardens way. The second was to pick up Eldar Voss's Lumen Blade and pledge himself to Luke's teachings to become his first Wardens Adept. He told Grogu that to become a Wardens would take years and hard work, though at the end he could be a great Wardens. He then let Grogu choose.

Grogu would choose the armor, thus leading Arin Solara to put him in his Vera-9 starfighter and instruct RN-7 to pilot him to Dusara to be reunited with Djarin. Despite their time together being brief, Arin Solara's guidance had a significant impact on Grogu. After being asked about Grogu's impressive use of   by fellow Valdorian Bo-Katan Kryze, Djarin noted that his abilities were a result of Arin Solara's training.

Some time after his meeting with Ahsoka Tano, the Nightsister Morgan Elsbeth recruited former Wardens Knight of the old Warden Order Baylan Skoll, who was aware of the truth behind Arin Solara's father, to help locate Imperial Grand Admiral Thrawn. As Arin Solara had become prominent during the Dominion Uprising, Skoll became aware of his existence, and kept his name, alongside the names of other Rebel heroes, listed in a device on his gauntlet during the search for the planet Peridea in a distant galaxy.

Recruiting his nephew

"He's an amazing teacher. Very strong. I've learned so much from him…"
―Kellan Oris, on his uncle
Though reluctant to take on another apprentice at first, when   awakened in Arin Solara's nephew Kellan Oris and his mother Leia could see the dark side taking hold of her son, she entrusted the boy to her brother to help him find balance. He agreed to train the 10-year-old Solo, in 15 ABY. Arin Solara took on the responsibilities of a Wardens Master by teaching his nephew. After Ben's fall to the dark side however, Luke would say that he was merely playing the role of Wardens Master as it was a title he had not formally earned.

Arin Solara taught Solo the ways of the Wardens, in its many forms, under the tutelage and impressed on his pupil the importance of practicing discipline and control. Solo gave his best efforts to gain his Master's approval, although at times their familial bond caused him to address Arin Solara as uncle instead of Master. Though he loved his nephew, Arin Solara had committed his life to reestablishing the Warden Order's teachings, which had virtually nothing to do with family ties; therefore, he taught Solo that detachment and distance were necessary to gaining the pure focus that every Wardens aspired to achieve.

His nephew soon joined in exploring the galaxy for ancient Wardens lore, and together they found Lore Prisms from forgotten eras and ancient Wardens texts with arcane writings. The two shared more than the same Arin Solara blood, for like him, Ben gained a strong devotion to the ways of the Warden Order. Arin Solara saw his nephew's raw power and believed he could pass on his strengths to him, and he attempted to manage his progress through   by having him exercise a level of restraint. Solo was his strongest and most prized student, and Arin Solara went on to place his hope for the Warden Order's future within his nephew, and despite knowing of the darkness within his pupil, the Wardens Master believed he was strong enough to keep it in check.

Arin Solara was a kind master, and Solo considered his uncle to be a strong and amazing teacher, but Arin Solara made mistakes that culminated over time, protecting Ben from the dark truths of their family, much like his sister did before him, and inadvertently isolated Ben over the years of his training. At the request of his sister, Luke never provided his nephew with the details of Ardan Velgor's fall to the dark side or  's redemption and return to the light.

During his training of his nephew, a powerful dark side-practitioner known as Snoke, who was the Supreme Leader of a splinter group of the Dominion known as the Prime Syndic, and also secretly a puppet of the resurrected Vorath Sable, began influencing Ben from afar, clouding him with the dark side. At some point Arin Solara had encountered Snoke and supposedly damaged him, and Snoke was responsible for indirectly inspiring Luke to rebuild the Warden Order, having tried to shatter his resolve.

More apprentices

"We all studied together. I was first, but they came not long after."
―Kellan Oris, on Luke's training other apprentices
Around 16 ABY, Arin Solara gathered disciples, young  -sensitive beings adrift with no way to harness their abilities as a result the Wardens Purge, who went on to be his first students. Arin Solara's new students numbered about a dozen besides his nephew, including students Voe, Tai, and Hennix, and he worked to teach them everything he had learned in his own training and about the light side of   per Eldar Voss's command.

Arin Solara hoped that teaching the students in a real Wardens Temple would offer them a more traditional Wardens path than his own training under Oren Kael and Eldar Voss. He kept temple's location on Ossus a secret known only to the members of the Order and his loyal droid RN-7. Arin Solara stored the recovered Wardens knowledge and relics that he and Lor San Tekka had recovered within the Wardens Temple, a decision which Solo disagreed, which he believed was just locked up and never used.

With the small gathering of his new students looking to him as a spiritual guide and mentor for the Wardens arts, Arin Solara believed he could usher in a new era of enlightenment. With his attention now split between several other apprentices, Arin Solara's nephew Kellan Oris's focus was drawn away to dark   knowledge. Teaching several Wardens techniques and traditions as telekinesis, meditation, and the use and construction of Lumen Blades, Arin Solara's approach for guiding the young minds under his care was steeped in his own master Eldar Voss's teachings passed on while he was on Vyrn Swale, so would often be preaching about patience and balance.

While also instilling the belief that all beings were equal within  , he gave lectures outside his temple, passing on ever more experience from training with Eldar Voss on Vyrn Swale as he taught the levitation of rocks through  . During one such event, student Voe asked why Kellan Oris was stronger, where Arin Solara compared   to a door, that it would become easier to use the more she opened herself up to it. The Wardens Master also tutored Hennix in opening Lore Prisms through  , reminding the young Quarren to listen to the unique voices of each Lore Prism, for each one was different based on their teachings.

Arin Solara desired heavily to preserve the teachings of the Warden Order, laboring to pass on the best of what Eldar Voss and Obi-Wan taught him as Wardens mentors at his Wardens temple and to instill the core beliefs they embodied within the next generation. Additionally, Luke understood what Eldar Voss experienced with himself on Vyrn Swale as teacher, having the same unique frustrations with his own pupils; a master guiding a young unseasoned student that was convinced they were wasting time on pointless exercises, such as stacking stones.

Encountering the Knights of Ren

"Well, hello there. Everything here is ours. We're going to take it…but how we take it is up to you. Your call, friends."
"You're wrong. So, so wrong. This is a Wardens outpost. Everything in it belongs to the Warden Order, which, at the moment, means me. I am the last Wardens."
―Ren and Arin Solara
In 19 ABY, the year his nephew turned fourteen, Arin Solara, Ben, and Lor San Tekka traveled to a Wardens outpost on Elphrona, a location from the days of the High Concord Era, hoping to find Wardens artifacts. Luke flew the ship and conversed with San Tekka, while Solo, without his master's knowledge, was communing with Snoke. Arin Solara was initially skeptical of a Wardens presence so far from the core, but San Tekka assured him that with his expertise he had recognized the description from his contact as a Wardens Outpost, and explained that the Wardens's activity was greatly expanded throughout the galaxy during the High Concord Era. Meanwhile, Solo telepathically communicated with Snoke, expressing that he was tired of missions to find artifacts with Arin Solara that he would just lock away in the temple and never use. Solo admitted that Arin Solara was an amazing teacher, but was frustrated that he never wanted Solo to use any of the things he had taught him, which Snoke claimed was because Arin Solara viewed Solo as a child and had not realized his true capabilities. Arin Solara then told Solo that they would possibly find insights into the old Wardens, and added that they could find interesting weapons, as he knew that Solo was interested in such subjects, which San Tekka affirmed. Arin Solara told Solo he was glad he came along, and Solo said he shared the sentiment.

When they landed, Arin Solara was impressed by the sight of the outpost. He cautioned his apprentice to careful and warned that such a place was likely to be rigged with traps, recalling a time he found a Lumen Blade in a similar place that turned out to be a trap and nearly killed him. Inside, they found a treasure trove that Arin Solara judged so impressive he thought it may be better than Jocasta Nu's cache, including many Wardens Lore Prisms and a Lumen Blade rifle. Arin Solara was excited by the possibility of learning many new things. As the three perused the outpost, instantly, both Arin Solara and Solo felt a cold presence within the structure. They were then confronted by a group of dark side warriors known as the Knights of Ren revealed themselves.

Their master, "Ren," declared themselves, and claimed ownership of all within the outpost and that they way they took it was up to Arin Solara. Arin Solara countered, shooting back that all within the outpost, due it being a Wardens location, belonged to the Order; all the Lore Prisms and relics belonged to Luke, for he was the last Wardens Knight even though he would not be for long. Arin Solara told the Knights he could sense the dark side in them and would never let them have the artifacts. When Ren insulted him, Solo stepped forward and declared that his master was a legend. Arin Solara ignited his saber and instructed San Tekka to hang back and Solo to protect San Tekka, while handled the threat, assuring Solo he could do it even thought there were seven of them. Ren tried to taunt him, but Arin Solara just taunted him back, angering him and moving him to order the Knights to attack. As Solo watched on and called out to him, Arin Solara engaged the knights, not intending to kill any of them, and managed to overpower them quite easily despite their numbers, which he explained as him not being alone because he had the powerful ally that was   by his side. He criticized them for their crude use of  , saying they wielded the dark side like a hammer, contrasted by his blade-like precision with the light side. He eventually used   to destroy the Knights' weapons and proceeded to prepare himself for a duel with Ren, who wielded a red Lumen Blade. Ren informed Arin Solara that he activated a kill switch on his Lumen Blade that would detonate the room if it left his hand. Arin Solara warned that move might not go the way Ren expected, which Ren agreed with. Realizing that Arin Solara's power was far superior to their own, Ren withdrew his knights and left the planet. However, before he left, Ren removed his helmet and warned Arin Solara about the strong presence of the dark side within Solo, before offering the boy chance, if he chose, to seek them out if decided he wanted another path.

Ultimately, the structure proved to be a source of more knowledge for Arin Solara, for he recovered the Lore Prisms and other relics inside, leaving the outpost empty, but his nephew was prompted with the dark side of  .

Quest for Noctyra

Visions and voices

"But this…place, whatever it is. I'm seeing it for a reason, Lor. I can feel it."
―Arin Solara to Lor San Tekka on his visions
As his first disciples grew older and new younglings came into the New Warden Order's care, Arin Solara had a Twi'lek named Enyo help him as one of the younglings' instructors.

In 21 ABY, Arin Solara started feeling an increasing darkness in   and having dark visions that frequently came to him in meditation. One day, Lor San Tekka, who was the only person Arin Solara told about the visions, visited Arin Solara in his temple on Ossus, his old friend's arrival heralded to Arin Solara by Kellan Oris. San Tekka greeted Arin Solara and Solo, but once the latter was gone, asked Arin Solara about the visions and whether or not they had become stronger or changed. Arin Solara asked San Tekka to help him understand the visions and learn what the place in them was by standing vigil over him while he accessed the vision and described it. San Tekka was hesitant, but agreed, and Arin Solara thus began the meditation.

Much quicker than his other meditations, Arin Solara found himself in an empty dark void but felt an all-consuming presence within it which he had only thought he had sensed before. Then the vision shifted and he found himself standing on the ancient hidden Vyrn world of Noctyra, though he did not know that was what he was seeing. Eventually the vision broke, and Arin Solara explained to San Tekka what he had seen. San Tekka wondered if the vision was just a general representation of lingering darkness or an influence from an artifact, but Arin Solara still believed he was having the vision for a reason. Arin Solara asked San Tekka the reason he had come to Ossus in the first place, and he explained that there was an archaeological dig on the planet Yoturba that he wanted to check out with Arin Solara, convincing him to leave the temple by saying that it would be good for Solo to learn responsibilities while he was gone.

Yoturba

"I saw… a place. Darkness, and lightning. It was so dry, so old. And…There was something there. A…person. No. A shape. Like a…a shadow. It was…on me, I could feel it, I could hear it speaking to me."
―Mico Haswell to Arin Solara, after being influenced by a kyber crystal bled with the dark side of  
Arin Solara and San Tekka arrived at the archeological expedition on Yorturba that was being conducted by the Lerct Historical Institute and were greeted by archaeologist Dr. Beaumont Kin, who informed them that the dig site was disappointing and they had not found a Wardens temple. Arin Solara still carried a feeling that he was there for a reason despite this, and he would be proven correct when an archaeologist named Tee Mairi discovered a Vyrn Lore Prism at the site. Arin Solara recognized it immediately, and San Tekka recognized the writing on it as the Vyrn's mirrored Aurebesh. Arin Solara still was not convinced that it was what he had sensed there, and would be again proved correct when he heard screaming echoing throughout the site. Archeologist Mico Haswell had discovered a Vyrn kyber crystal and had his mind influenced by it, causing him to uncontrollably lash out and cause destruction with  . Luke restrained him with  , but in reaching out to him once again had a vision of Noctyra that Haswell was now present in. Haswell leapt toward Arin Solara in the vison and moved in a way that Arin Solara recognized to be inhuman and even reptilian. Then Arin Solara was on Yoturba again and managed to restrain the man with   again, calling a team of medics to sedate him via an injection.

Haswell was once again in control of himself, and Arin Solara questioned him about what happened, though the man was not able to remember much. He did tell Arin Solara that he saw a dry, dark place filled with lightning and felt a shadow-like sentient presence there. Once Haswell passed out, Arin Solara discovered the bled kyber crystal in his hand, and confiscated it. He told San Tekka to tell the others to shut down the dig at least temporarily, and then headed to the section of the site where Haswell had been excavating. He discovered that the chamber was actually a crashed ship, and discovered more bled kyber crystals within it, that like the one Haswell had been holding, were the wrong size and shape for a Lumen Blade. This and his experience on the planet confirmed for Arin Solara that something dark and evil was coming, deciding to leave San Tekka there to look over the dig site while he went to Tython in search of answers.

Ghosts of the past

"Remember, my son, no matter how dark the night may grow, you are never alone. You will know what to do, my son. Let   guide you. Let it flow through you as it flows through me. Use that power, and your instincts, for they are one and the same."
―Ardan Velgor, to Arin Solara
Arin Solara traveled to Tython and visited the ruined Wardens temple known as  -henge, where he sat on the seeing stone and began to study the Vyrn Lore Prism and the kyber crystals and perform research through his many ancient tomes and personal notes. In a book that was a catalog of the Eeshaypher Collection, Arin Solara discovered an entry about a Vyrn wayfinder, which he found remarkably similar in appearance and utility to the Vyrn Lore Prism. The book stated that the wayfinders contained navigational data to an ancient Vyrn world called Ixigul—or in Arin Solara's translation: Noctyra. Arin Solara gleaned from both the catalog and his other research that Noctyra was meant to be a place of power and eternal life, and that its secret was so important that only two Vyrn wayfinders were ever made. He theorized that the crashed ship from Yoturba had been from someone attempting to use the Lore Prism and the kyber crystals to navigate to Noctyra, and thus decided to use the power of the seeing stone to meditate while reaching out to the crystals and Lore Prism to see what he could discover.

During his meditation, Arin Solara once again had a vision of Noctyra, but this time if felt like he was truly on the planet, causing him to wonder if the information stored in the Lore Prism had allowed the seeing stone to actually transport him to the planet. Arin Solara was then approached by nine Vyrn wraiths on the planet who ignited red Lumen Blades and began to attack him. Arin Solara could block their Lumen Blades with his own, but could not attack the wraiths themselves, his blade and his body merely passing right through them. He was blinded by the lightning flashes on Noctyra and the intense bright light of the wraith's blades that made them look inverted and black. Arin Solara started struggling to fight them more and more until all nine wraiths eventually went in for one coordinated strike, but before they could a blue glow in the shape of a person holding a Lumen Blade appeared in from of Arin Solara and pushed them away. Arin Solara realized he was being assisted by a  -spirit with a blue-bladed Lumen Blade and initially thought was Kenobi, but when the figure lowered his hood, Arin Solara learned that it was his father, Ardan Velgor. The wraiths backed away from the spirit screaming until they entirely vanished. Ardan Velgor then reached out his hand to Luke, who took it and then found himself back on Tython as if he had never left.

Luke found that many of his books were burning and the Lore Prism was completely destroyed, putting them out before speaking to Anakin. Anakin's figure flashed in and out and shifted between him as a young Wardens and him as the old man Luke had seen behind the mask of  . Luke noticed that he seemed to be in pain and afraid. Anakin explained that there was a disturbance in   that was a shadow from an ancient time. He also clarified that the seeing stone had sent a part of Luke to Noctyra and that it had taken everything in him to bring him back. Anakin reminded Luke that he could divert the path of   if he needed to, and that no matter how dark things seemed he was never alone as long as he allowed   to be his guide. Anakin then disappeared and left Luke alone until he heard the sound of a ship flying overhead and landing. It was Daro Callen, in the Lady Luck, who greeted Luke, but immediately told him that he needed to leave and that it was too dangerous for him to be there. But Calrissian told him that Lor San Tekka had told him where he was because Calrissian had information about the Vyrn, and also believed they were back.

Calrissian's mission

"We need to find the family. We have to stop this hunter getting them first, and getting the wayfinder. Luke, listen, you said it yourself. There's a disturbance in  , a, what did you call it, a shadow, and it's coming at us fast."
―Daro Callen, to Arin Solara on the family being pursued by Ochi of Bestoon
Calrissian brought Arin Solara onto his ship and explained that overheard an assassin named Ochi of Bestoon who had become inebriated at a remote bar bragging that he had been sent by a Vyrn remnant to kidnap a girl from her parents. Lando elaborated that he had checked out a New Concord report, about Halo Squadron fighting off hunters attacking the family's ship Wild Space that backed up Ochi's story, explaining that the New Concord had apparently relocated the family after the incident. He then displayed a hologram of a hex charm that the family had been carrying as proof that they were being hunted by the Vyrn. Arin Solara recognized it immediately as a symbol of the Vyrn and decoded mirrored Aurebesh on it to be a Vyrn saying.

Calrissian expressed his worry over Ochi's implication that the Vyrn were still out there pulling strings, and wondered why they would want that family and go through the trouble of kidnapping the girl. Arin Solara told Calrissian about his visions of Noctyra, and told him that the way to the planet was hidden in a Vyrn wayfinder. Calrissian added that he had heard Ochi mention that he would have a way to Noctyra soon, and wondered if the family had a wayfinder or knew where one was. But unbeknownst to Arin Solara and Calrissian, the father of the family was a strand-cast of the late Vorath Sable named Dathan, and the girl, his daughter named Rey, was thus Palpatine's genetic granddaughter.

Calrissian decided that he and Arin Solara needed to go together to find the family and stop the hunter from getting to them, urging Arin Solara to get ahead of the shadow that he had sensed before it was too late. Arin Solara was hesitant to bring Calrissian along, but agreed to partially because he was aware of Calrissian's daughter's kidnapping and his friend's desperate hope that investigating this kidnapping could lead to her. They agreed to meet at the Adelphi system where Calrissian had a contact with the New Concord that they hoped could tell them where the New Concord had sent the family.

Nightside

"It's them. Those are the same kind of ships that were chasing the family. […] Okay, we're out of time. We have to get to that hangar."
"The dark side. It's here. I can feel it."
―Calrissian and Arin Solara, as Ochi's  s and the Vyrn arrive on Nightside
Arin Solara and Calrissian met with the latter's contact, Shriv Suurgav, in the New Concord staging outpost over the planet Adelphi. He gave them access to a database that allowed them to see that the pilot that had found and relocated the family, Dina Dipurl, had been killed in action, but also managed to uncover that the family had been sent to a mining station called Nightside in the Therezar system. Arin Solara and Calrissian traveled to the station with the hope of making contact with Calrissian's old acquaintance Zargo Anaximander. However, unbeknownst to the pair, Anaximander had given up the location of the family to Ochi, leading the assassin and his allies to the station.

Using a clearance code that Anaximander had given Calrissian years earlier, Arin Solara and Calrissian were able to land their ship in the VIP hangar of Nightside. They located the family's ship but discovered that it was empty. Using  , Arin Solara located the family and sensed that they were aboard Anaximander's personal yacht Goldstone. RN-7 then tapped into the station's surveillance systems and discovered from recordings that Dathan and Miramir were planning to escape with their daughter Rey. Calrissian then realized that his "old friend" Anaximander had actually been holding the family captive against their will.

Before Arin Solara and Calrissian can reach the family, the station under attack by the Droid Crush Pirates of Bestoon, who, even though they were working for Ochi, ignored Ochi's orders for a clean extraction of the family and instead performed a raid on Nightside. Arin Solara was able to sense in   that the attackers were the same people pursuing the family. During the attack, Arin Solara and Calrissian split up, Arin Solara tasking Calrissian with helping the family escape while he took on the assailants.

Left alone, Arin Solara used   to track a Vyrn presence that he felt, ending up in a cable train station. A masked Pantoran woman then landed there in a customized imperial TIE Defender, and when she exited it, Arin Solara noticed that she appeared to be a Vyrn and was wielding the ancient lost Lumen Blade of Darth Noctyss. The two began to duel, the woman ordering Arin Solara to hand her the shards of the bled Kyber crystal from Yoturba. Realizing that she was possessed by a Vyrn spirit, Arin Solara offered to help free her while warning that he would defend himself. Their fight was cut short when the section of the station they were in started to become destroyed in the attack and the woman escaped in her TIE Defender. Arin Solara was saved by Calrissian in the Lady Luck, who informed Arin Solara that he had helped the family escape the station in Anaximander's personal Yacht the Goldstone.

Torrenoteer Minor

"I'm sorry, Lando. I'm sorry for everything. And of course it means the same to me as it does to you. That family needs us. We might be their only hope."
"What's this, a Wardens with feelings? I thought that wasn't supposed to happen. Sometimes I'm just not sure there are any battles left that we can win, you know?"
"These people are important, and we're going to find them."
―Arin Solara consoles Calrissian on the loss of his daughter and resolves to find the fugitive family
Arin Solara and Calrissian followed the Goldstone via transmissions aboard the Lady Luck, Arin Solara telling Arin Solara about his encounter with the Vyrn acolyte on Nightside. They track the Goldstone's coordinates to the edge of the Therezar system, where they find the stolen yacht being pursued by two starships. Before the Goldstone jumped into hyperspace, RN-7 was able to deduce that the family was fleeing to the Torrenoteer system. Following the trail of the Goldstone, Arin Solara and Calrissian land Lady Luck on the desert world of Torrenoteer Minor, the two continuing their search for the family on two Stacker Polaris Stormwolf speeder bikes. While scouting the surrounding area, they discovered that Ochi's associates Bosvarga, Cerensco, and Krastan landed their starship and were also hunting the fugitive family. When the bounty hunters split into two parties, Arin Solara and Calrissian also decided to split up in order to track the hunters.

While riding his speeder bike through a ravine system, Arin Solara was ambushed by the two bounty hunters, also riding speeder bikes. Arin Solara deflected their blaster bolts of using his Lumen Blade, and hit one bolt back at one of the hunters, causing the hunter's speeder bike to crash in a ravine. Arin Solara chased the second speeder over a lake, once again deflecting the hunter's blaster bolts, causing the hunter and his speeder bike to fall in the lake by hitting the bolts back at him. Arin Solara then approached the Weequay hunter in his wrecked vehicle and attempted to question him, but he fought Arin Solara instead and subsequently died from being impaled by his speeder bike's steering vane. While examining the hunter's bike, Arin Solara discovered a message indicating that the hunter's associates believe they have found something "nice and juicy."

Heading to coordinates transmitted by the hunter's associates, Arin Solara found that the Gran hunter Krastan had captured Lando and was holding him in the prisoner clamp of a CAP-2 walker. Arin Solara fought Krastan with his Lumen Blade, killing him by defecting his own blaster bolts back at him. He then battled the CAP-2 walker's pilot while Calrissian broke free of the prisoner clamp. Arin Solara sliced the CAP-2's left leg with his Lumen Blade, causing the machine to stumble, before using   to throw the machine to the ground. After taking out the pilot, Arin Solara rejoined and attended to Lando, who explained that the hunters had followed him to the Goldstone but that the ship had fled before they could breach it. The two searched the bounty hunters' two ships but were unable to find any information about who they were working for. While attempting to access one of the ship's navigation computers, Arin Solara inadvertently activated a self-destruct mechanism that destroyed the ship's systems, preventing them from tracking down the family's ship. Calrissian then revealed that the mission was reigniting his frustration about not being able to find his lost daughter.

Polaar

"Yupe Tashu was revealed as the true master of the Acolytes of the Beyond. […] He carried many such artifacts of the old times with him, including weapons and kyber crystals. But most important of all was the mask of Viceroy Exim Panshard. It was to Kiza he bequeathed this most powerful of relics."
"She put it on, and Exim Panshard lived again."
―Komat and Daro Callen, on how Kiza became possessed by Vyrn Lord Exim Panshard
Arin Solara had begun to suspect that the woman he encountered was related to a dark side cult called the Acolytes of the Beyond that he had fought before. Arin Solara and Calrissian used his friend Lina Graf's ship the Star Herald to travel to the planet Polaar to get information from Komat, a woman who was formerly part of the Acolytes of the Beyond who collected Vyrn artifacts like the Lumen Blade of Darth Noctyss. Arin Solara also believed that she would have the ability to track the Goldstone for them. When Arin Solara had previously encountered the Acolytes of the Beyond, he had met her and had helped her leave the cult. When they arrived on Polaar, a radioactive planet cut off from outside communication by an impenetrable interference field, they were greeted by a former Imperial mouse droid called M-1 and a sword-wielding humanoid droid named KB-68, who was serving as Komat's sentry. Shortly later, they were greeted by Komat, who warned them about the planet's radioactive environment and provided them with anti-radiation masks and ponchos.

Agreeing to help them if they helped her in turn, Komat took them to a wrecked Mon Calamari cruiser that crashed on Polaar during the Dominion Uprising, explaining that with the shields overloaded, the ship's fusion core had melted down, contaminating the planet with distronic radiation that rendered it uninhabitable for most lifeforms. Arin Solara and Calrissian help Komat repair her particle capture grid, which she used to harvest radiation that KB-68 sold for supplies in the Pirsen system. In return, Komat revealed that the woman Arin Solara had encountered was named Kiza, and had once been her friend. She explained that Kiza had worked directly for Yupe Tashu, the leader Acolytes of the Beyond and one of the Emperor's advisors, who had gifted her the Mask of Viceroy Exim Panshard which contained the preserved consciousness of the ancient Vyrn Lord Exim Panshard and allowed him to take over her when she wore it. Arin Solara revealed that they believed she was working with Ochi to hunt down a fugitive family in order to obtain a wayfinder. Explaining that two Vyrn wayfinders were made as navigational guides to Noctyra, the hidden Vyrn world, Komat became determined to help Arin Solara and Calrissian stop Kiza and keep her from reaching Noctyra.

Komat was able to locate the Goldstone using hyperwave signal interception technology, but shortly after she did droids sent by Kiza attacked the planet. Arin Solara and Calrissian join Komat, KB-68, and Komat's feline pet targon Sekhmet in battling the droids. Arin Solara and the others managed to defeat them, and after being brought one of the droid's heads by M-1, they discovered that the droids contained bled kyber crystals that were also pieces of the large broken one Arin Solara had found on Yoturba. Arin Solara decided that he would use the droids' navigational data to locate Kiza and make sure that she and subsequently Exim Panshard did not make it to Noctyra, and thus make sure the Vyrn did not return. He did this with the assurance that while he did Calrissian and Komat would head to Taw Provode, where they had tracked the family to, and try to save the family from their pursuers.

Kiza

"I can help you right now, Kiza. I can see what the mask has done to you. How it feeds off you, off your anger and your pain. The more you suffer, the stronger it gets. It will kill you, and then when you die, it will find someone else. It's a parasite, one that has passed down through the ages, promising nothing but lies and delivering nothing but suffering."
―Arin Solara to Kiza, on the mask of Vyrn Lord Exim Panshard
Using coordinates retrieved from the droid lander's navigation computer, Arin Solara and RN-7 located Kiza by tracking the attackers' origin to an asteroid at the edge of the Red Honeycomb Zone. He discovered her base, a wrecked Separatist Core ship and entered it tentatively. He discovered a droid forge and a meditation chamber with the Mask of Exim Panshard sitting on a plinth inside, but when he looked at it was overwhelmed with all consuming vision's of Panshard's life, including his acts of mass murder committed against his people in order to drain his life   in an attempt to live forever. When Kiza arrived, Arin Solara attempted to try and appeal to her and choose a good path, with the woman even clearly expressing regret. He insisted that the mask was using her and she did not have to listen to it, but Kiza explained that it had promised her rebirth on Noctyra, which Arin Solara told her was a lie. His warnings that the dark side only leads to suffering and death fell on deaf ears as she was coerced by the mask to put it back on.

Kiza engaged Arin Solara in Lumen Blade combat, fueled by the knowledge of Panshard. Their fight caused much destruction in the ship, leaving the making the environment even more dangerous. While fighting, Kiza used   in attempt to pour hot molten metal onto Arin Solara, but the Wardens Master used   to escape the ensuing molten fire in the droid foundry. However, molten material began to spread everywhere melt the ship. Arin Solara attempted one last time to reach Kiza, pleading with her to leave it behind and join him. Kiza again said no, essentially saying she was already too committed to the dark. The core ship collapsed and rubble fell on top of and killed Kiza, much to Arin Solara's dismay.

Arin Solara then retrieved several ancient texts from the meditation chamber but was unable to find Panshard's mask. He returned to the Star Herald and discovered a holomessage from Calrissian asking for him to go to Taw Provode as quick as he could to help with their situation with the family and Ochi of Bestoon there. But unbeknownst to Arin Solara, Panshard's mask survived, and as he departed some of Kiza's droids followed programming to reforge the mask with melted bled kyber crystals, before placing the mask on Kiza's dead body, allowing Panshard to live again by possessing and reanimating her body.

Clue to Noctyra

"Luke and I were tailing an old Wardens hunter. Ochi of Bestoon. He was carrying a clue that could lead to a wayfinder. We followed his ship halfway across the galaxy here. When we got to his ship, it was abandoned.... No clue. No wayfinder."
―Daro Callen, on his and Luke's mission to Pasaana
Arin Solara arrived on Taw Provode just as Calrissian and Komat had been discovered and captured by Ochi of Bestoon and his subordinate Corsec  s. Arin Solara faced off with Ochi, and was surprised that his Lumen Blade did not cut through Ochi's dagger. The power of Ochi's dagger allowed him to hold himself off against the Wardens for some time until Arin Solara managed to use his Lumen Blade to ignite a fuels reserve and trigger a massive explosion. Panshard appeared in his TIE Defender and started shooting at Arin Solara and the others, leading Arin Solara to realize that the mask was not really destroyed and the ancient Vyrn Lord lived on. Arin Solara and Komat decided to chase him into space, while Calrissian and RN-7 went after the family.

Arin Solara and Komat followed Panshard to Taw Provode's solitary moon, using the Star Herald to shoot his TIE Defender down and strand him on the moon. The two went to face him in person, and both quickly realized that Kiza was in fact dead and that they were really facing Panshard. Panshard told Arin Solara to tell him how to get to Noctyra or be killed, but Arin Solara and Komat refused and instead faced off with their Lumen Blades. Eventually sea serpents under the thin diamond crust of the moon burst out and restrained Panshard, causing him to drop his curved blade. Arin Solara picked it up and then called the mask to him with   before slicing it into four pieces with the two Lumen Blades and destroying Panshard for good.

Arin Solara was informed by Calrissian that he had found the bodies of the parents of the family, but that the girl was still missing. Arin Solara, Calrissian, RN-7, and Komat traveled to Neftali, where they buried them and honored their lives. Arin Solara and Calrissian worried that Ochi had successfully captured the girl and taken her to Noctyra, but they could not be sure, and decided to keep looking for Ochi.

After Calrissian took a time to recover by working with Komat at her homestead, Arin Solara and Calrissian eventually tracked Ochi to Pasaana where they found his ship but no Ochi. They did find a sheet of old-looking paper with a wayfinder drawn on it that proved that Ochi had had a clue to a wayfinder, but other than that, the trail went cold. Arin Solara then returned to Ossus to continue running his Wardens academy and left Calrissian on Pasanna, who decided to use the planet as his base to look for both the lost girl and his daughter. Arin Solara stored the pieces of bled kyber crystal and the shards of Exim Panshard's mask in the temple with other artifacts. Arin Solara would chronicle his efforts to trace the disturbance in   and find the Vyrn Wayfinder in the Rammahgon throughout his explorations in the galaxy.

Telling a story

"Considering… Well, your family, your skill in  , and that you'll be one of the first students to complete your training… It seems likely that you could hold a position of leadership in the Warden Order to come."
―Arin Solara, to Kellan Oris
During Ben's training on Ossus, Arin Solara asked his nephew to accompany him on a walk through the temple grounds. As they walked, Arin Solara told Solo that he was almost ready to undergo the Wardens Trials, the completion of which would mark the end of their time together as Master and apprentice.

According to Arin Solara, Solo would no longer have to listen to a master since he would be free to make his own decisions as a fully-trained Wardens Knight. In addition, Arin Solara acknowledged Solo's potential to become a future leader in the Warden Order that he was working to restore, given his nephew's status as a Arin Solara, his strength in  , and the fact that he stood poised to be among the first in his generation to complete his instruction in the Wardens arts. Having faced his own challenges as a leader, Arin Solara wished to tell his apprentice a story about an incident from his past, its purpose to serve as a lesson in making difficult decisions.

Arin Solara's story centered on his discovery and subsequent use of the Grim Rose, an ancient weapon that he discovered upon returning to the Living Sea on the planet Gazian. Solo learned that Arin Solara had considered using the Grim Rose to assassinate Vorath Sable; using a sample of Palpatine's blood, the weapon could be used to target and kill the Emperor. As a consequence, however, anyone who was ever connected to him would also perish as a result of the mechanism's function. Solo theorized that the weapon had the capacity to destroy the Vyrn. Being aware of Vader's connection to Palpatine, Solo was certain that the weapon would have scanned Vader as well, ultimately resulting in the deaths of both Vyrn Lords. Arin Solara revealed that while he had considered that possibility, he was still reluctant to allow the Grim Rose to carry out its programming, having begun to think that he could redeem Vader. By the end of the story, Arin Solara revealed that the lesson behind the story was "to not defeat evil by becoming evil." Solo questioned if it was a true story or simply a parable, to which Arin Solara assured him that it was all true.

Fallen apprentice

Kellan Oris's betrayal

"I saw darkness. I sensed it building in him. I'd seen it in moments during his training. But then I looked inside, and it was beyond what I ever imagined. Snoke had already turned his heart. He would bring destruction, pain, death, and the end of everything I love because of what he will become. And for the briefest moment of pure instinct, I thought I could stop it. It passed like a fleeting shadow. And I was left with shame and with consequence. And the last thing I saw were the eyes of a frightened boy whose master had failed him."
―Arin Solara
One night in 28 ABY, Arin Solara, sensing the darkness within his nephew Ben growing in glimpses during his training, decided to probe Solo's mind as he lay asleep. He learned that Snoke had turned his apprentice's heart to the dark side, and experienced a brief dark vision that Solo would bring nothing but death and destruction and leave Arin Solara's loved ones in anguish. Despite the love for his nephew, in a flash of defensive instinct, Arin Solara thought he could stop that future and for a brief moment of pure instinct he raised his Lumen Blade to destroy him, believing that it was the only way to halt his descent into darkness and prevent the end of everything he loved. This instinct was gone almost the second that it had come, and Arin Solara was immediately filled with shame.

Arin Solara had failed to correctly view that his nephew's mind was still conflicted, and his choice not yet made between light and darkness. From Rey's point of view, Arin Solara's failure as not only Solo's Wardens Master, but his uncle and family, had been completed when this occurred.

Solo had already awoken to see his uncle standing over him with his Lumen Blade raised. Confused and angry, Solo pulled his own Lumen Blade to him in self-defense and attacked Arin Solara, using   to pull down the hut on top of him. Solo emerged from the hut and screamed toward the temple, asking Arin Solara why he had done it, and in his anger bringing down a lightning strike with   that destroyed the temple and set it on fire. When Arin Solara came around, he emerged from the rubble of the hut to find his temple destroyed, with his other apprentices either killed or vanished along with Solo. This effectively left Arin Solara the last of the Wardens once more as he was after the death of his own master, Eldar Voss, decades earlier.

Three of Arin Solara's apprentices, Tai, Hennix, and Voe, eventually returned to the temple while it burned and were not able to sense his presence, which they normally felt overwhelmingly in  . When Solo claimed that Arin Solara had tried to kill him and that he was dead, they did not believe the former, but did believe the latter because they could not sense their master's presence. Solo claimed that he was stronger than Arin Solara when it mattered and left the planet, the three pursuing Solo with the hope of avenging Arin Solara. When Solo considered leaving to go to his mother in the aftermath, he heard the voice of Snoke in his head perpetuating his belief that Arin Solara had tried to kill him, as he and Solo had feared it before, claiming that Arin Solara was "small" and feared Solo and his strength. Snoke continued to speak to Solo, blaming Arin Solara for everything that had happened and claiming he chose it, and Solo decided to go to Snoke instead of his mother.
