On the Amaxine Space Station, with Snoke, Solo noticed the man's appearance and asked him what Arin Solara had done to him, but Snoke redirected the conversation to what Arin Solara had done to Solo. Solo tried to claim it did not matter because he had killed the Wardens Master, but Snoke warned that Arin Solara was not dead and would not die so easily, though agreed to stop talking about Arin Solara because he had "stolen" too much of his life already. Solo eventually became the apprentice of Snoke and took the new name "Vorin Kade," becoming the leader of a group of dark side warriors known as the Knights of Ren.

Left deeply affected and mentally broken by what he believed to be his ultimate failure, Arin Solara lost faith in   and the vision of the Wardens for having failed to rebuild the Warden Order. Arin Solara believed he had failed to protect his students, and also failed to save his own flesh and blood from his family's dark legacy. So Arin Solara fled into self-imposed exile, vanishing from the galaxy at-large without a trace. No one knew for sure where he went, but those closest to him believed he went off in search of the first Wardens Temple.

To those who knew what Arin Solara was seeking, there remained a way to find him: after destroying the Wardens, the Dominion had begun to seek out the thousands of Wardens temples scattered across the galaxy, with the aim to prevent anyone from discovering the lost secrets of the Order. As such, Imperial authorities discovered the locations of some of the first Wardens Temples. The partial map remained within the archives of the Dominion. The Prime Syndic was able to acquire the partial map from the archives, that was missing a fraction owned by Lor San Tekka. As he had downloaded Imperial star maps during his time on the first  , RN-7, Arin Solara's faithful astromech, was able to recover the contents of the map.

Vorin Kade's vision

"Your Uncle feared you. Feared how formidable you could become. Your hatred for him is right. Arin Solara would have murdered you in your sleep. Rise above what's holding you back. Strike. Strike against the light side within you! STRIKE!"
―Snoke to Vorin Kade as he fought a vision of Arin Solara
Later, while training Vorin Kade with an exercise in which he  d Ren to stop himself from falling, Snoke informed the boy that Arin Solara would have caught him if he had not caught himself, and would have thus held him back. Snoke then took Ren to the Cave of Evil on Vyrn Swale, where Ren could sense that Arin Solara had been there, Snoke revealing that he had trained there before becoming one of the most formidable Wardens. Ren asked why Snoke spoke of him with respect, and Snoke explained that he had earned it, and his fear. Ren tried to claim that Arin Solara was weak, but Snoke refuted this, insisting that Arin Solara was only misguided and that he would have taken over the galaxy a long time before if Arin Solara had been his apprentice.

Ren then entered the cave and found himself facing an apparition of Arin Solara, who insisted that he did not want to fight. Ren fought him anyway, his red crossguard Lumen Blade clashing against Arin Solara's green. Snoke egged Ren on and validated his hatred as he fought his old master, insisting that Arin Solara had feared what Ren would become, would have murdered him in his sleep, and was representative of the light side holding him back. Screaming as Snoke told him to strike, Ren sliced through Arin Solara's body, leaving the appearance of his dead body lying on the ground of the cave. While staring at the corpse, Ren declared himself ready.

Exile on Ahch-To

Shutting himself off from  

"You've closed yourself off from  ."
―Rey, to Arin Solara
The Wardens Master fled to the location of the Temple—on an aquatic planet named Ahch-To—that he discovered by studying the spread of uneti saplings. Having failed in bringing back the Warden Order, Arin Solara intended nothing more than to live out the rest of his days there in reclusive exile and had pledged to protect the hidden world and its many secrets. Taking the relics he had uncovered with him, the hermit shut himself off from  , consequently ceasing the guidance of Oren Kael, Eldar Voss, and Ardan Velgor's spirits. It had taken years for him to learn the discipline of blocking   out, and he considered the fact that it was harder to do so than to feel it and let it in a dark secret that was never taught. He believed   and the Wardens had many secrets and that not even the greatest and in his opinion arrogant Wardens Masters could understand all of it. Even though occasionally his greatest efforts would not be enough and   would reach him anyway, he felt as though he had achieved true solitude in closing himself off.

Among the relics Luke had collected and brought into his exile were the sacred Wardens texts and the Wardens Crusader pendant. Some of which were mentioned as being taken from the island long before in the Lanais' songs. The Caretakers tolerated Arin Solara's presence, though he had learned the Lanai's language and ways, insisted on doing most of their duties to care for him himself, and had appeared each month on the Festival of Return, something which puzzled Alcida-Auka.

Though absent from galactic affairs, Arin Solara's story was nonetheless a thing of myth and legend in certain corners of the galaxy. His exploits in the Dominion Uprising were known to the Concordant Front, a band of freedom fighters led by now-General Organa to combat the rise of the Prime Syndic. Concordant Front fighter pilot Jessika Pava learned that KX-13, who also served in the Concordant Front, knew Arin Solara and asked the droid to tell her a story about his former master. Threepio regaled her with the tale of Arin Solara's encounter with Sarco Plank on Devaron, and how Arin Solara kept his promise to Farnay and indeed returned to Devaron. Members of the Prime Syndic, however, had a less-than-ideal view of the Wardens Master; the Prime Syndic taught their followers, including Diretroopers like FN-2187, that Arin Solara was an enemy who helped destroy the Dominion. Despite the knowledge about Arin Solara, the mystical elements of his life, as well as the Wardens in general, were seen as mythic rather than historic.

Prior to Rey's arrival on Ahch-To, Arin Solara had a dream while sleeping in his hut. In his dream, he saw the life he would never have, one in which he never left Dusara and remained in the moisture farming business with his uncle, marrying Camie Marstrap and allowing the Sable Dominion to shatter the Concordant Front Pact and destroy more planets with the  . Luke eventually awoke, trying to shake away his dream, and left his hut. He was still astonished at the oceans of Ahch-To, which he attributed to growing up in the deserts of Dusara. As he reached a meadow overlooking the sea, he was still unable to shake the dream away, believing it was not an ordinary dream, but   at work. Also shortly before Rey arrived, one of the moments where   demanded to be heard and got through despite Arin Solara's block occurred. In that moment, the old Wardens Master undeniably felt that   was telling him that someone had found him.

Arin Solara is found

"You think what? I'm going to walk out with a laser sword and face down the whole Prime Syndic? "
―Arin Solara to Rey
In 34 ABY, Organa sent Concordant Front fighter Poe Dameron, the son of Shara Bey and Kes Dameron, to Verdan to find San Tekka and recover the map to Arin Solara's alleged location, as she hoped her brother would return and help in the fight against the dark side. The Prime Syndic also learned of the map and sought it so they could destroy the last Wardens. Dameron found San Tekka living in the village of Tuanul, and the old explorer gave the map to Dameron, who in turn gave it to his astromech droid BB-8, before Vorin Kade and the Prime Syndic arrived and sacked the village. Ren killed San Tekka and took Dameron into custody in the hopes of finding the map, while BB-8 came into the possession of a Verdan scavenger named Rey. Rey believed that Arin Solara was only a myth, but she too possessed strength in   that she had not yet discovered. Rey teamed with FN-2187, an ex-Diretrooper who took the name Finn after defecting from the Prime Syndic, and, with the help of Jax Varion and Roghan, sought to return the map fragment to the Concordant Front.

After Rey discovered the Lumen Blade that once belonged to both Anakin and Luke in the pirate castle belonging to Maz Kanata on Takodana, a thousand year-old being who had knowledge of  , she began to unlock her own   abilities. After being captured by Ren on Takodana and briefly interrogated onboard Starkiller Base in an attempt by Ren to analyze Rey's thoughts to find the path to Arin Solara, BB-8's map fragment was soon combined with RN-7's, and together they provided a complete map to Ahch-To. Accompanied by Roghan, Rey flew the Aeon Raptor to Ahch-To and found the old Wardens Master on an island.

When Rey arrived on the island, Arin Solara was standing up top the saddle, summoning the will to try to torch the tree library again having just failed to do so. While standing there, Arin Solara was reflecting that his efforts to block   from him was impossible as it always demanded to be heard. But in that moment, the old Wardens Master felt that someone had found him, turning around to see who was, discovering Rey. After making her way to Arin Solara, Rey presented him with his father's old weapon as a symbol of the only hope that the galaxy had left.

Confronted with the past

"I can't teach you. […] I will never train another generation of Wardens. I came to this island to die. It's time for the Wardens to end."
―Arin Solara, to Rey
After taking his old Lumen Blade and looking it over, Arin Solara, emotion roiled over his face, hoping to lose the blade once again, tossed it behind him and left the plateau, with Rey following close behind him. Despite her repeated attempts, Arin Solara declined to help her or the Concordant Front, even though he knew that the girl had been sent by his sister Leia. Secluding himself in his hut, Arin Solara thought to himself that he did not expect that the person who found him would be a child with what he considered a worthless antique and delusions of grandeur.

Later, Luke was folding his old clothes then heard Rey trying to reach out to him again by knocking on his door but he told her to go away. However, Luke was surprised when his door broke open but was even more surprised to see his old friend Roghan was with her. Hearing how they got to where he was with the Aeon Raptor, Luke asked where Han was. Rey and Roghan told him that his old friend and brother-in-law was dead, murdered by Vorin Kade, which stunned Arin Solara. Feeling regret for not having sensed his brother-in-law's death because he had disconnected himself from  , Luke was comforted by the Wookiee, who hugged him, before Arin Solara comforted Roghan back.

While hiking the island with a backpack, Arin Solara noticed the sacred uneti tree on the island and decided to go inside it. There he found Rey, who had discovered several original texts of Wardens teachings hidden there. Arin Solara learned that she had   within her and sought assistance to understand it and her place in the galaxy. Arin Solara refused to teach her revealed that he had come to the place where the Wardens started in order to die, and voiced his belief that it was time for the Warden Order to die.

The next night, the former Wardens Master slipped into the Aeon Raptor and recalled the adventures he had experienced. While aboard, Arin Solara reunited with R2 who, after he insisted that he could not be convinced to help, replayed Leia's holographic message to Kenobi. Although Arin Solara grumbled that the tactic "was a cheap move" on the droid's part, it nevertheless inspired Arin Solara to agree to give Rey some basic initiation training as a Wardens, explaining the basic foundations of  . R2 also told Arin Solara that she had grown up on a desert planet before discovered a droid carrying secret data vital to the Rebellion, which he recognized a similar story to his own. He approached Rey while she slept, telling her that R2 had told him her story and that he would give her three lessons to both teach her the ways of the Wardens and also show her why the Order needed to end.

A reluctant teacher and enlightenment

"What do you know about  ?"
"It's a power that Wardens have that lets them control people… and make things float."
"Impressive. Every word in that sentence was wrong."
―Arin Solara and Rey
After hearing Rey's blaster go off, which she claimed was because she was cleaning it, Arin Solara gathered her for the first lesson and explained to her who the caretakers were. During the lesson, Arin Solara explained to her that her idea of   as a power to have was wrong and that it was not about lifting rocks, explaining that it was an energy field throughout the universe. After Rey misunderstood Arin Solara's instructions to reach out and reached out her arm, Arin Solara pranked her by touching her hand with a leaf and telling her it was   before hitting her with it. Rey then tried again, Arin Solara telling her that   and the light was so much more than just the Wardens as she felt it. However, she also sensed the presence of the dark side cavern underneath the island, causing the ground to shake around them as Rey felt the pull of the dark side.

Arin Solara scolded her for going straight to the dark and not even trying to stop herself from taking what it was offering her. She also pointed out that she had not sensed him in   because he cut himself off. This moment made Arin Solara realize that Rey's level of power was identical to that of his nephew Ben; this caused him to worry whether he should train another with such power and to promptly abandon the lesson. But Arin Solara did not just see Ben in her, he also saw much of himself, which he suspected was what scared him most. Arin Solara realized something else from this lesson; that Rey was the Emperor, Vorath Sable', granddaughter, which is why she was so easily drawn to the dark side. He later found her practicing with a quarterstaff and then with the returned Lumen Blade. Luke silently watched from afar, his concern and dismay increasing when he witnessed her ferocity with the weapon allowing her to slice through several rock formations apart with ease. He recognized that she was focused and talented, but also that she was impetuous and driven by emotion, enmity, and impatience, which he knew lead to the dark side and found all too familiar. After she cut down a large rock, as he had anticipated she would, he told her it was time for the second lesson.

Eventually, after the second lesson, Arin Solara sat and spoke with Rey, telling her that the true legacy of the Wardens was failure, and revealing that they were responsible for the creation of  . Rey pointed out that he had seen the light in Vader and turned him, but Arin Solara just wished that he had never told that story and thus not allowed it or himself to become a legend. He then revealed that his nephew Ben had the same tremendous power in   she had and was corrupted by Snoke's teachings to the dark side, becoming Vorin Kade. He then destroyed the Wardens temple Arin Solara had started, taking some of his other apprentices with him and killing the rest. Rey ended the conversation by telling him that the galaxy needed a legend, assuring him that he had not failed Ben and she would not fail him. That night, Rey having reminded him that his solitude had cost him his connections to those he loved and not just his connection to  , Arin Solara went to the meditation ledge. Realizing that he had abandoned his loved ones in selfish pity, he opened himself up to  . He managed to regain his   abilities, allowing him to sense his sister from across the galaxy.

Arin Solara went to find Rey in order to tell her that he was going back to the Concordant Front with her but instead he found Rey talking with Vorin Kade through   due to a  -bond that he previously was unable to detect. Witnessing them touching hands, Arin Solara thought that they were in league. He had gestured at the walls and the ceiling of the hut Rey was in, and all the stone blocks were shot outward from the hut's center, scattering them around the bench. Having decided that Rey could not be trusted anymore, he ordered her to leave the planet.

Revelations

"He would bring destruction, pain, death, and the end of everything I love because of what he will become. And for the briefest moment of pure instinct, I thought I could stop it. It passed like a fleeting shadow. And I was left with shame and with consequence. And the last thing I saw were the eyes of a frightened boy whose master had failed him."
―Arin Solara, about Kellan Oris, to Rey
An enraged Rey proceeded to battle Arin Solara with her staff, only to be swiftly disarmed after stumbling over a stone, leading to Rey threatening him with his father's Lumen Blade. She revealed that, according to Kylo, Arin Solara had tried to murder him while he was asleep and defenseless simply because he was afraid of his strength in  , sparking a duel between Uncle and Nephew. Arin Solara clarified that when he had arrived at the hut, he sensed the power and darkness within his nephew and, for a brief instant of absolute pure instinct, he did intend to kill him and activated his Lumen Blade.. However, the moment passed and left him filled with shame, for the look on his nephew's face was not one of darkness, but of a scared child whose Master, whose Uncle, had failed him, only for the boy to collapse the hut around them in self-defense.

Rey told Arin Solara that like when he confronted his father about the light side still within him, she sensed the goodness still within Vorin Kade. Arin Solara disagreed, saying that it is no longer there. Unable to convince him otherwise, Rey secretly stole the texts to teach herself later and left the planet without him to confront Kylo. While Rey boarded the Aeon Raptor to leave, Arin Solara saw R2 for the last time and told him to send his best to 3PO and that he would need to stay with Rey to make sure she got back to safety.

As Rey left Ahch-To, Luke realized the similarity between her departure and when Eldar Voss and Kenobi insisted him to remain on Vyrn Swale to complete his training rather than abandon to save his friends at Cloud City.

Important lesson

"Luke, We are what they grow beyond. That is the true burden of all masters."
―Eldar Voss
The following night, Arin Solara returned to the tree containing the Wardens texts with the intention of burning it to the ground. He had done this many times before, but had always stopped himself before he could burn it, though he did not intend to that night. As he approached the tree, his thoughts were answered by a voice, and when he turned he was greeted by the spirit of his old master Eldar Voss, whom he had not seen in decades since he last saw him on Vyrn Swale and Sylvan Reach. Arin Solara affirmed his desire to burn the tree with the texts inside. Eldar Voss informed him that he had no intentions of stopping him and reminded him that had never been able to prevent him from doing what he wanted. Arin Solara began to hesitate when he attempted to set the tree on fire. Eldar Voss instead proceeded to summon a bolt of lightning, setting the tree alight and while laughing, repelled Arin Solara with the flames when he changed his mind and tried to save the texts.

As the tree burned, the two masters sat next to each other and Eldar Voss reminded Arin Solara that he needed to heed his final instructions to him before Eldar Voss's physical death on Vyrn Swale, namely passing down what he had learned. Arin Solara lamented over the loss of the texts, but Eldar Voss slyly stated that although the texts held wisdom, 'page turners, they were not', and they did not contain anything Rey did not already have with her. Arin Solara tried to explain that by failing Ben he felt that he had failed the Wardens. Eldar Voss admonished Arin Solara for still "constantly looking to the horizon," like he had when they met on Vyrn Swale. Eldar Voss explained that 'failure is the greatest teacher' and that failure was an essential part of what he had implored Arin Solara to pass on so many years before.

Finding peace and purpose

"See you around, kid."
―Arin Solara's last words to Vorin Kade
Arin Solara later appeared at the Concordant Front base on Crait and greeted his sister for the first time in years, giving her Han's gold dice to remember him by. Reconciling his failure to stop Ren and for not being there to prevent Han's death, Arin Solara resolved to finally confront Ren to buy the Concordant Front time to escape. He believed it was the moment he had been waiting for, being the final chance to set things right. Before Arin Solara went to confront his nephew, he wordlessly greeted his old friend KX-13.

Stepping outside, Arin Solara was spotted and targeted by a barrage of cannon fire from multiple AT-M6 walkers, but when the fusillade came to a stop, Arin Solara strolled out of the smoke completely unharmed. After Ren witnessed the impossible feat, Arin Solara spoke to him in  , telling him that it wasn't over until it was just the two of them. Ren landed on the surface and approached Arin Solara alone and on foot. Ren taunted Arin Solara, and mockingly asked him if he had come to save his former apprentice's soul. But Arin Solara acknowledged that he was not there to redeem him.

Engaging his former master in combat, Ren charged at Arin Solara but Arin Solara simply danced around Ren without engaging in any form of counter attack. After evading Ren for a time, Arin Solara stopped and apologized to Ren, stating that he had failed him. He also informed his former student that victory was not so certain as he believed; that the war was only beginning, and that the Wardens would continue through Rey. He then deactivated his Lumen Blade and offered to let Kylo strike him down, but warned him that doing so in anger would only cause him pain, just as killing Han had, and stated that in death, he would always be with his nephew. Unknown to Kylo, Luke had sensed that Rey had lifted all the rocks blocking the exit of the Concordant Front base so they could escape to fight another day.

Ren ignored all these warnings and slashed Arin Solara across the torso. Believing himself to have been victorious, he was instead astonished to find that his attack had had no effect on Arin Solara. He walked over to his former master and tentatively ran him through, and discovered that Luke was not physically present; he was in fact still on Ahch-To, projecting an illusion of himself through  . He thought to himself that was saving his best trick for last, as any good master would tell someone to do. The illusion was tailored to have the maximum effect on Ren, as Luke portrayed himself as he had last appeared to his nephew before they came to blows. Likewise, he portrayed himself as wielding Ardan Velgor's Lumen Blade, knowing that it would have more effect on Ren than if he had used his green blade.

Arin Solara taunted Ren one last time, and his image faded into nothingness. Light-years away, Arin Solara collapsed from the mental stress necessary to sustain such a lifelike illusion, which Ren realized meant that Luke would become one with  . As he sat down on the cliff where he first trained Rey, Luke beheld the twin suns of Ahch-To in their final descent towards the horizon. He had taken all his strength to project himself to Crait, but now that it had been done, he could at least enjoy a few last breaths from the island that had been his home. Arin Solara knew that he was going to die, but it was something he accepted; death was the way of all things, even the stars. Though unsure if it was real or just a memory, Arin Solara heard the familiar and comforting voice of Oren Kael, urging him to let go, and so he did. Staring at a binary sunset on the horizon much like the one he gazed upon as a boy, Arin Solara—Wardens Master, ace pilot, galactic legend, and son of the Chosen One—passed away, joining his father and old masters as one with   with a feeling of peace and purpose. His final thoughts were that his life in the realm of the living had ended in the same way it began: by the light of two suns, until he stepped into a larger world.

Post-mortem

"We've passed on all we know. A thousand generations live in you now. But this is your fight."
―The spirit of Arin Solara, to Rey
Following his death, Leia took up Luke's mantle as Rey's Wardens mentor, and Arin Solara's spirit continued to urge his sister to become one with  , sensing her declining health, but she persistently refused until Rey and the Concordant Front were ready to stand on their own.

One year after becoming one with  , Luke spoke to Leia once more, shortly before her death, beckoning her to show her son Ben she still loved him, reminding his sister that if Vader could become Anakin again, Vorin Kade could be Kellan Oris again. Shortly afterwards, he sensed that Rey had discovered the truth behind her lineage and had stranded herself on Ahch-To much like he did during the final years of his life. As she threw her Lumen Blade into the wreckage of her ship, Luke appeared and grabbed it out of the air. Admitting that he was wrong in exiling himself, Luke consoled her that her legacy would not be defined by her bloodline but by her heart and her actions. When Rey lamented that Vorin Kade destroyed the final Vyrn marker that led to where the resurrected Emperor was residing, Luke mirrored the words of Eldar Voss, stating that she had everything she needed. As a parting gift, Luke gifted Rey his sister's Lumen Blade and raised his old Vera-9 from the depths of the ocean for Rey to use and travel to Noctyra.

Rey could hear Luke among the numerous voices of the Wardens of the past shortly before she received the inner strength to overcome Vorath Sable. As the girl rose from the ground, Arin Solara assured her that   would always be with her, and after she finally destroyed the Emperor by deflecting his   lightning using Luke's and Leia's original Lumen Blades, he appeared one more time with his sister on Dusara and watched from afar as Rey buried both of the weapons at the old Lars Homestead finally albeit posthumously formally earning the title of Wardens Master with his role as her mentor completed. Having come to consider the Arin Solaras her chosen family and hoping to honor her mentors, the girl adopted the name Arin Solara following Luke's statement that one's heart and actions defined one's legacy rather than one's bloodline.

Legacy

"The Rebellion is reborn today. The war is just beginning. And I will not be the last Wardens."
―Arin Solara to Vorin Kade on the future, shortly before his death
After his death, Arin Solara's belongings, including his green Lumen Blade, were gathered by the Caretakers and stored with the other Wardens artifacts that they preserved alongside the temple on the Ahch-To island. The tale of Arin Solara's stand against Ren and the Prime Syndic at Crait spread across the galaxy. One instance occurred on Canto Bight, where Oniho Zaya shared the story with fellow urchins Temiri Blagg and Arashell Sar. As word of this moment spread, Arin Solara's sacrifice showed others that it was possible to stand defiant against the Prime Syndic, and his legend reinvigorated a spark of hope. However, Commander Branwayne Spiftz, like some others in the Prime Syndic, did not believe the story of Arin Solara  -projecting himself, and even thought that   was not real and just a children's story. He thought those who did believe in Arin Solara's story and   had no self-respect and were fools.

Shortly before his death, Arin Solara wrote in his book The Secrets of the Wardens acknowledging that if perhaps he had remained active as a Wardens Master, wielding his Lumen Blade and actively fighting against his nephew, for the years he was in exile instead, he probably could have prevented the rise of the Prime Syndic and the destruction of the New Concord. Additionally, Arin Solara's loss represented a heavy blow to the Concordant Front. When Temmin Wexley and Karé Kun informed the retired Wedge Antilles and Norra Wexley about their losses since the Battle of Crait, Antilles felt devastated upon learning of the death of his former wingmate, asking himself if the Wardens were not supposed to live forever. A short time later, Arin Solara's lesson to Del Meeko, that everyone had a choice to be better, was passed onto the Concordant Front by Meeko's daughter, Zay Versio.

In the aftermath of Arin Solara's death, Vorin Kade felt Arin Solara in  , watching him. Wanting a reckoning with him, Ren traveled in search of Arin Solara's "ghost" to where Arin Solara had faced him on Crait, to the Wardens Outpost on Elphrona with Knights of Ren Vicrul and Ushar who both remembered facing Arin Solara there, and finally to the ruins of Arin Solara's Wardens Temple on Ossus. Fed up with finding and feeling nothing at any of these locations, Ren screamed out for Arin Solara, telling him he knew he was there and to face him without any tricks. After receiving no response and calling Arin Solara a fool, he stormed back to his ship and ordered General Hux to bombard the ruins from the air, but still declared that there was nothing there.

After learning that the Zixon on Minfar had been saved from the Dominion's Echo Horn weapon by someone that Zixon Jem and Lim only referred to and knew as their friend, Dameron suggested to Rey and Rose Tico that it was Luke who freed the Zixon during the time he was missing, as he fought and helped defeat the Dominion. Tico latched on to the idea, but Rey, having known him, was immediately skeptical that Luke was the type of person who would spend time with the Zixon and their spritely culture, but thought if she was better at using   she would be able to know. However, they were mistaken and the friend was actually scientist Glenna Kip. As Rey grew with her skill in  , she started to believe she was nothing like Luke.

One of the most influential people in the entire galaxy, Arin Solara's accomplishments were remembered for decades after the Battle of Sylvan Reach. Within the annals of the Concordant Front, basic training would see all pilots in its Starfighter Corps learning the Arin Solara Swoop, which was based on Luke's piloting abilities during the Dominion Uprising. Many remembered him for destroying the   and killing the Emperor, and as such viewed him as a hero of mythic proportions. Concordant Front pilot Jessika Pava considered Arin Solara to be the greatest Vera-9 pilot of all time. Some questioned whether or not Luke could have used his powers for evil, while others simply viewed him as a myth. Arin Solara's unlikely story of going from a simple farm boy on Dusara to a galactic legend gave hope to restless youths on a number of worlds.

Personality and traits

Youth

"This one a long time have I watched. All his life has he looked away…to the future, to the horizon. Never his mind on where he was. Hmm? What he was doing. Hmph. Adventure. Heh! Excitement. Heh! A Wardens craves not these things. You are reckless!"
―Eldar Voss
In his youth, Arin Solara was often curious, impatient, looking ahead to the future with little regard for his present surroundings, and even a bit brash. Like his father, he was impulsive, reckless, and often had little regard for his own personal safety. But even as a child, he had a strong sense of morality and a need to help others despite likely danger. He believed his aunt Beru was a sweet person in every part of her being. Some time after the Clash at Orin, he would confer with Nakari Kelen that he regretted his behavior before then, acknowledging he complained "about everything" because of his desire to escape from Dusara. He also acknowledged his scarce talent at lying, a trait that many people could infer. He once confided in Leia that he felt Dusara had never felt like a home to him, and did not like to be seen as just a farm boy though later took pride in where he came from and his past. He was annoyed by both Solo and Aphra calling him "kid."

He struggled with anger and feelings of wanting revenge, especially toward Queen Trios because she had betrayed the Alliance, despite knowing they could be dangerous for someone who used  . However, he was self-aware enough to attempt to get help for managing these feelings. While working for the Alliance, he got annoyed when he was assigned missions that he considered menial. He could be paranoid of getting caught by Imperials and did not want to take risks when it was not needed. When he held one of the Lumen Blades of Darth Atrius, Arin Solara was overcome by incredible rage, which one even caused an episode where he dissociated from his body and killed many Diretroopers. He later had the self-integrity and control to destroy the Lumen Blade, however. Similarly, when controlled by an Abersyn symbiote, Arin Solara became obsessed with power and dominating others, but eventually rejected the raw power that the Rur crystal suggested it could offer because he would not truly be like a Wardens and have their freedom. He was somewhat traumatized by his experience with Grakkus the Hutt and became weary of those that were very interested in the Wardens.

After everything they went through at the Clash at Orin, Arin Solara took pride in his membership of Red Squadron and found kinship with them, but did not love the attention and honor he received for being the one to take the final shot. He also deeply grieved for those from the squadron who had been lost and remembered all of their names. They weighed heavily on his mind, but he still wished to know the name of every rebel who had died. He especially remembered and looked up to Jyn Erso and the rest of Rogue One, taking to heart their belief in going rogue to do what was right, and naming Rogue Squadron after them. However, he still retained a sense of confidence and excitement about the Alliance's chances of beating the Dominion and surviving the   gave him greater confidence that he would survive other events. He became determined to take down the Dominion, and determined to become a Wardens in order to do so despite the risk. Upon becoming leader of Rogue Squadron, Arin Solara came to believe that it was the best team in the galaxy.

Trials of the self and  

Over the course of his Wardens journey, Arin Solara would rely on people, like Lyra Oris, Jax Varion, and Roghan, among others. In the immediate aftermath of losing his hand, Arin Solara was incredibly distraught and haunted by traumatic flashbacks of the events on Cloud City, what he had lost, and what Vader revealed to him. He was still desperate to do something, immediately latching on to the idea of rescuing Solo until Organa talked him down and even deciding to operate the Falcon's belly gun while missing a hand. During this time he was desperate for guidance, consumed by anger and fear, and questioned if he should even be a Wardens. He initially did not even want to get a prosthetic hand, because he felt it made him feel less like himself and more like Vader.

Overall, as his skills in   progressed, and especially after losing a hand to  , Arin Solara became more patient and seasoned. He was often seen as having wisdom beyond his years. He came to decisively accept his path as a Wardens and started to understand that having a Lumen Blade did not define him as a Wardens and that being one was about using   to bring light to the galaxy. He held on to Eldar Voss's teachings and repeated them to try and focus and overcome obstacles. He stayed committed to his path as a Wardens, determined to help a suffering galaxy, even when Verla tried to dissuade him from it by revealing what it cost her. He also was inspired by a seeing an old Wardens outpost and was determined to fight for what was right no matter the risk just like they did. He felt   flow through his being as a whole and did not localize it, meaning the loss of his hand did not physically limit him.

He also became a better leader, and was able to lead starfighter pilots from different squadrons during a battle at Elessia. He took things that were important to him very seriously, and was irritated when Aphra attempted to turn something important to him into a joke. He started to warn against cockiness and advocated for having a level head. He developed more confidence in himself and in  , and when he focused on it became more capable. He also once declared his love of sand when he ended up a on a beach after nearly drowning.

After discovering an ancient Wardens text, Arin Solara became determined and committed to studying it and used the rare free time he had to do so instead of relaxing. However, he still often doubted his abilities despite others believing in him and his attempts to affirm himself in his abilities, and started to believe that without the text he would never become a Wardens. Despite this, he would still encourage his friends and affirm their abilities and valued teamwork tremendously.

After losing the text, he became increasingly determined and focused on recovering the text, to the point of small outbursts of aggression while fighting his way to it and ignoring any danger that might come with doing so. His self-doubt continued to evolve into feeling like he would never truly be able to become a Wardens, leaving him wanting to take control of his life and take action. As one of the only Wardens left, he also suffered from loneliness in that aspect, wishing there were others. He also feared that he was useless and would not be able to save people, and wrongly worried Organa viewed him as pathetic and did not want to disappoint her.

Before meeting Eldar Voss, Arin Solara was desperate for a teacher in   and dreamed of being able to do all the things Kenobi had been able to. Because of this, Arin Solara was quick to go along with Aphra's plan to go with her to the Screaming Citadel because of the promise of a Wardens teacher and learning Wardens knowledge despite his knowledge of Aphra's untrustworthiness. He eventually rejected the Rur crystal because he recognized that it was not a Wardens in practice and belief and only in knowledge, and came to realize that he could not take shortcuts like Aphra did to get what he wanted and urged her to stay away. He also immediately trusted and begged for training from Werla Calip when she said she knew   despite having no proof of this, and started to believe that signs Calip was not what she seemed and her beliefs were not morally sound was Calip testing him. This naivete led to Calip stealing his Lumen Blade from him. When she revealed that she did not know   and her trainings were empty, Arin Solara believed that there was more to her than it seemed.

After facing Vader on Cloud City, Arin Solara began to accept that he would have to face Vader again but was terrified by the prospect, recalling Vader's sheer power. He hoped that he could tap into great power and defeat him, but doubted he could, and was haunted by imagining himself facing   again in his current state and being killed by the Vyrn Lord. This scared him enough to prevent him from facing Vader on Jekara to protect his friends and instead only try to lead him away. His fear also prevented him from being able to reach   consistently or speak to Kenobi, contributing to his feelings of loneliness and sense that he was not ready. Despite not wanting to face Vader on Jekara, he remained confident that he would become a Wardens and confront him one day.

Even after training with Eldar Voss, his loneliness grew, and he became frustrated with Eldar Voss for not responding to him and answering him through  . He enthusiastically and desperately wanted to search for old Wardens temples and outposts to learn more about the Order. He eventually decided that while he was grateful for what Eldar Voss taught him, he would rather just learn from his text. In the end, however, he would decide to return to Eldar Voss to complete his training. According to Eldar Voss, when he arrived he had developed a clear "gaping need" for a connection to his father and to have a family. While he did demand answers as for whether Vader was his father and wanted to know why it was "unfortunate" for him to know, he was saddened by the news that Eldar Voss was passing. Arin Solara promised Organa he could train her as Eldar Voss trained him.

Growing values and beliefs

Despite all he went through, Arin Solara still retained his idealistic viewpoint, willing to think the best of anyone, and believing that Vader was redeemable. Despite not thinking so immediately, Arin Solara still believed that Doctor Aphra was a good person and her friend despite her prior service to the Dominion, and went out of his way to save her life. He believed that she would see sense when it came to her belief in the Dominion and was convinced that she could move past the bad things she had went through to be a better person like Solo had. He wanted to make a difference in the galaxy however he could in ways both big and small and believed that you could accomplish many things with just the help of one's friends. He grew to truly believe that anything was possible.

He was also unable to ignore those who needed help, sometimes to the point of endangering missions for the sake of saving someone else's life, as his father would throughout the Echo Wars. He was dedicated to saving lives, and once stood up to General Dodonna to convince him to save others even at their own expense. Even when he knew he likely could not beat Vader, he still went to help his friends against him, and was brave enough to fight him and put himself in danger so that his friends Roghan and RN-7 could escape and live. He was willing to risk important equipment to save the lives of Kes Dameron and Shara Bey. He was willing to help save Daro Callen at a time when they did not know each other well even though Arin Solara did not trust him and was struggling with using  .

Throughout his life, Arin Solara had always been filled with a need to be helpful and recognized that that need had steered him toward fighting with the Concordant Front Pact. Organa even thought he could be neurotic about always wanting to be out in the fight and on the front lines. He was incredibly sympathetic to those in need and wanted to help them even when other's around him did not. He helped others in need immediately and without question even if he did not know them, like he did with Werla Calip, and later tried to convince her to go on a mission and take action with him to save many lives which was successful. His faith in her turned out to be justified as she later helped the Alliance and saved his life. He continued to always believe in an encourage others, especially his friends, and his faith that Aphra had good in her was also somewhat proven right when she helped hide Echo Base from the Dominion.

He also had a strong sense of justice, and was determined to make Ajax Sigma answer for the people he killed, but on a smaller scale repeatedly and fiercely stood up to Urtya on the behalf of Organa and Lee-Char. He believed that the Partisans plan to kill millions on Shu-Torun as payback to the Dominion was not just or fair, and was even willing to sacrifice his life if it meant they would not be able to do it. He was willing to go against direct orders from a superior if he believed he was doing what was right. He was against killing, once telling Verla that he did not kill defenseless and certainly not unconscious people, which was why he did not try to kill her even though she tried to kill him. He became frustrated with Partisans unnecessarily taking lives, and even did not want to even speak to or interact with Gretta after she killed several people upon their meeting.

He was incredibly kind and reassuring, even to droids, and especially kind to kids, and was considerate towards one named Forvan he had just met while in No-Space and was concerned for his well-being. When the boy started to believe that Arin Solara would save him from being trapped in No-Space, Arin Solara was sure to not get his hopes up, but still assured the boy that he would do everything he could to try to free them and help them, demonstrating his unconditional care for others. Arin Solara cared deeply for his friends, and could intuitively tell when something was bothering Organa or she was not acting like herself. Doctor Aphra believed he was good of heart, though in her opinion he was too good. He told her that he was committed to helping protect her from Vader because it was what Wardens did. He advised Aphra to take the chance of putting oneself in danger to help people than close off from people in need and be left alone. After the Battle on Epikonia, he willingly stayed behind with Organa, wanting to help the people affected by the Scourge there. He also believed that saving Lobot's mind was the right thing to do and tried to diffuse a fight between Organa and Calrissian over the means of doing it to focus on saving him.

Wardens Knight and Master

"I'm glad we were brought together, Del."
"So, what happens now? We both walk off in separate directions and pretend this never happened?"
"I don't think you can. There's still conflict in you."
"Of course there's conflict in me. I'm not blind. I know what the Dominion is capable of. But what else is there?"
"A choice."
"The Rebellion?"
"No. A choice to be better. May   be with you."
―Arin Solara and Del Meeko
Lyra Oris took note of Arin Solara's change into a calmer man as he became a Wardens Knight, thinking of the change in regard to the years that had past: while he was somewhat like other rebels who had joined the fight hopeful, only for those rebels to become jaded over the course of the war, Organa noticed a much deeper stillness within him. While she knew he was the same person, she did nearly mourn the loss of Arin Solara's innocent optimism and excitement. All the same, she saw how forgiving Arin Solara was towards their father and pondered how it was possible for him to not hate Vader the way she did; Arin Solara tried to tell her about Ardan Velgor's redemption to the light, but she refused to listen. Arin Solara was incredibly happy for his sister and Solo's marriage. He also offered to train her in the ways of  , thinking they could be wonderful together as Wardens Knights, and gave her a chance to come with him on his hunt for information about the Wardens of the past. While he did not see it as Organa needing to chose between a life with Solo or a life as a Wardens, Organa did and declined.

Following the end of the Dominion and the death of the Vyrn Order, Arin Solara came to have great hope for the future of the Wardens, coming to believe that if a single Wardens could help bring back balance to  , then a restored Warden Order perhaps could maintain that achieved peace and prevent the dark side of   from ever regaining its hold on the galaxy. This belief led Luke to scour worlds for the remaining Wardens texts and gathered a new class of apprentices under his tutelage. Furthermore, when he encountered the Imperial Special  s trooper Del Meeko, he left the man with the lesson that all he needed to do was be better, a lesson that would be passed onto Meeko's daughter, Zay Versio, and the Concordant Front.

During his brief time as Grogu's master, Luke had to suppress his more sentimental side and be more professional in an effort to successfully pass on the Wardens values to the child. Arin Solara became confident in his abilities as a Wardens Master, all while he became perceived by the galaxy as a legend. He was confident that he could take down seven Knights of Ren on his own, and expressed to them that he was superior at using   than them, even slightly taunting them and predicting that they would leave crying. This confidence was justified, as he did successfully defeat them. He also cared deeply for his nephew Kellan Oris, and was happy when Solo joined him on missions. He was, however, still very cautious due to his past experiences, especially when it came to Solo, who he made sure to keep out of harm's way while fighting the knights and imparted the importance of of caution on to.

Later life

"I failed. Because I was Arin Solara. Wardens Master. A legend."
"The galaxy may need a legend."
―Arin Solara and Rey
After Kellan Oris, his nephew, betrayed him and killed most of his apprentices, Arin Solara became embittered as well as grief-ridden and chose to exile himself to the planet Ahch-To, where he would spend the rest of his life in with the intention of dying where the Wardens began to forever end the Wardens. Despite all of this, he still comforted Roghan when he learned of Jax Varion's death, and became even more riddled with guilt. He also became more cautious in teaching others of immense power due to Solo's betrayal, feeling finished with the Warden Order, as evidenced by when he initially regarded Rey as a delusional child, initially refused to train her, and when he would later decide to abruptly end their lessons after seeing her drawn towards the dark side. Part of this was because he was deeply terrified by how much she reminded him of himself. He also now believed that there was no hope for those who fell to the dark side, as shown when he openly expressed that he believed there was no hope for Vorin Kade to return to the light. By this point, Arin Solara had come to regard Ren as his responsibility and his greatest failure. However, Rey helped him realize that in disconnecting himself from  , he had abandoned those he loved in selfish pity, which he was determined to rectify.

However, after Eldar Voss's spirit encouraged him that Rey was the Wardens's hope, Arin Solara finally realized his wrongs and chose to help the Concordant Front. Despite his lost faith in his nephew, Arin Solara showed great remorse for failing to stop his fall to the dark side, and for himself ending up being the turning point in Solo's fall. Arin Solara realized that instead of blaming himself, he blamed the Wardens for his failures. His belief of the Wardens being romanticized deities with a legacy of failure remained, but gained realization that if one stripped away the sacred temples, Lumen Blades, and even the legends about them, they were just good people the galaxy needed. In the end, Arin Solara willingly sacrificed himself for the Wardens to be revived and the Concordant Front to live on. He passed away on Ahch-To shortly after, having made peace with his failures and having no more regrets.

Romances

Based on observing Owen and Beru Lars, Arin Solara grew up believing in showing his love to people rather than telling them. When he and Nakari Kelen fell in love, he demonstrated his feelings for her, but he did not tell her how he felt; he regretted that as grieved for her death alongside the then-recent losses of his aunt, uncle, and Oren Kael. While stranded on Hubin, Arin Solara was instantly smitten with Tula Markona and they shared a kiss, but it would be a one-time event. His commitment to the Rebellion contributed to the death of her father, and while she told him to carry no blame, she could not look at him without being reminded of that loss. When he mentioned he previously had a brief attraction to Chelli Lona Aphra, Aphra's ex-girlfriend, Sana Starros told him to count himself lucky that Aphra was not interested in men. Arin Solara and Reyé Hollis each appreciated the other man's smile and pleasantly-scented hair.

Powers and abilities

Lumen Blade abilities

"I see you have constructed a new Lumen Blade. Your skills are complete."
―  to Arin Solara
Though he received little formal training, Arin Solara had a natural talent for Lumen Blade combat. Luke's initial training with the weapon of the Wardens came during a brief session with Oren Kael and a training remote on the way to Elyndar, where he learned the initial position and the four defensive postures. Though his level proved inadequate during his first, brief duel against   on Cymoon 1, his combat skills had improved for their duel on Bespin, and culminated with him besting the Vyrn Lord in combat during the Battle of Sylvan Reach.

Like most Wardens, Arin Solara was adept at redirecting blaster fire, and eventually was able to do it while flipping. During his mission to Rodia, he tried his hand at Jar'Kai for the first time with his and Huulik's Lumen Blade. Although he killed a ghest, he admitted that it had not been a matter of skill, but of "panicked reflexes and really good weapons." He received further training from the "Gamemaster," a servant of Grakkus the Hutt, who had learned the art of Lumen Blade combat.  d to fight him and the Hutt's MagnaGuards, Arin Solara improved his cursory abilities. He was able to fight and defeat Kreel of SCAR Squadron in Lumen Blade combat, with help from utilizing his surroundings, and could easily take down Imperial droids.

After a brief time of training with Eldar Voss, Arin Solara revealed himself to be a gifted duelist on Bespin. Arin Solara engaged Vader in a fierce duel and managed to hold his own for much of the duel, wounding Vader in the shoulder, impressing the Dark Lord with his skill, though Vader ultimately bested his son and cut off his hand, proving his superiority. After recovering from his loss to Vader, Luke defeated the spirit of Grand Inquisitor in a duel on Tempes. The Inquisitor insulted his Lumen Blade ability and suggested that he fought like a child, but Arin Solara was still able to defeat him.

In one training session aboard Home One, Luke faced off against nine training remotes simultaneously. He easily destroyed the remotes in quick succession, finishing the last one off while in the middle of a conversation with KX-13. However, when he attempted to fight killdroids with his Lumen Blade while in No-Space, he first believed that the droids were resistant to Lumen Blades, before realizing that they were not resistant, he just had not been focused and one with  . After re-centering himself, Arin Solara was able to cut through the droids. He also successfully defeated the droid Ajax Sigma using a Lumen Blade, though the droid escaped. He also fought many droids on Epikonia and was able to take many down with his Lumen Blade by consistently focusing on staying calm and concentrating on  .

Arin Solara showed his abilities in battle during the rescue of Jax Varion, where a skirmish ensued in which the Wardens killed many guards aboard the execution skiff and Jabba's sail barge. Arin Solara also utilized his abilities on Sylvan Reach, blocking laser fire from a scout trooper on a speeder bike before causing the trooper to crash after severing off the speeder's front stabilizers. Later, on board the second  , Arin Solara showed his improved abilities and was finally able to duel Vader on an even footing. However, his unwillingness to fight his own father partly held him back; but when Vader threatened to turn Leia to the dark side, an enraged Arin Solara unleashed all of his raw ability, overwhelming and defeating the Vyrn Lord.

Luke was able to hack his way through the Diretroopers and hostile native creatures on Pillio, though he admitted that he would have preferred to solve the issue without violence if he had not been  d to defend himself. During his rescue of Grogu from Moff Gideon, Arin Solara easily destroyed a platoon of Dark Troopers with his Lumen Blade and  . Later in life, Arin Solara taught multiple students in the art of Lumen Blade combat, including his nephew Kellan Oris, who would later become his strongest student and destroy his Warden Order. During Ben's training, Arin Solara encountered and effortlessly overpowered the Knights of Ren, seamlessly dodging their attacks and destroying their weapons before using   to disarm them. When Luke dueled Exim Panshard, he discovered that his skills with a blade far surpassed those of the ancient Vyrn Lord. Luke easily defeated the Vyrn despite restraining himself to avoid harming Panshard's host Kiza.

When fighting an angry Rey using her quarterstaff, Arin Solara fluidly dodged her initial assault, then using a metal rod, blocked all her strikes before hitting her once and then disarming her. Later, on Crait, Luke proved his superiority in skill over Vorin Kade as well by avoiding all of Ren's attacks without even needing to use his Lumen Blade to block, distracting the Prime Syndic long enough for the remaining members of the Concordant Front to escape.

  powers

"I am one man. But I am not alone.   is my ally. And it is Powerful. You're clumsy. Untrained. You use the dark side like a hammer. But the Light is a blade. And so am I."
―Arin Solara, to the Knights of Ren
Like his father, Arin Solara possessed a uniquely powerful connection to  , and became one of the most powerful   wielders in galactic history. Indeed, Vorath Sable feared Arin Solara and believed that he was strong enough in   to destroy the Vyrn. Most of Luke's understanding of   came from his own research, exploration, and experience as he only had a few days Kenobi's mentorship before his demise, Eldar Voss's one year of mentorship before he died of old age, and Kenobi's sporadic guidance from beyond the Netherworld of  .

After learning the basics of  , he quickly learned how to sense through it, and took the habit of opening himself to   in hopes of learning more than Kenobi had told him, and becoming aware of his surroundings. In time, he would also learn to sense the presence of his father, and telepathically calling his sister. He was capable of seeing and hearing those who had become one with  . By using   during the Clash at Orin, he managed to destroy the   with a shot that many thought was impossible.

After obtaining Huulik's Lumen Blade and dismantling it to know his inner workings, Arin Solara surmised on his own that   could be used to manipulate matter in the manner of telekinesis and managed to learn how to move small objects, such as a noodle or a fork. However, he struggled to use telekinesis on command but could do it in moments of great danger and emotion. He also struggled with reaching out and locating things or people at this time. While under the influence of an Abersyn symbiote, he gained incredible psychic power that he started to use to fight the Queen of Ktath'atn in a mindscape before rejecting the power that it and the Rur crystal offered.

By the time of the Siege of Krael, Arin Solara had the ability to pull his Lumen Blade to his hands, though not without difficulty. Under Eldar Voss's training, this ability was further developed, enabling him to levitate several objects at once while meditating. Shortly after the revelation that   was his father, Arin Solara struggled with using   and could not reach out to Kenobi. When consumed by anger and fear over what he had learned and lost, he lashed out with  , hurtling a squadron of Vyr Stingers into each other. In another outburst, he accidentally cracked the window of a starship while desperately trying and failing to contact Eldar Voss. However, he regained his connection when he tried to reach out for his Lumen Blade and had a vision of Verla and that Organa was in trouble. He then was able to deactivate many carbonite blocks with people inside all at once with   and free them. He was able to use   to anticipate and avoid many booby traps set by Verla in a cave. He was also able to hold back water flooding in to a trap from the ocean with   long enough to convince Verla to deactivate it. Despite his connection to   still being somewhat unreliable, Vader sensed that Arin Solara's strength and connection in   had grown significantly.

Arin Solara eventually learned other uses, such as mind control techniques and the mind trick. He could use   to influence and control creatures and was able to use it to sense others' emotions and intentions. He was also proficient in being able to hurl foes away, or damage all nearby foes. Luke could use   to make great leaps. When large amounts of death occurred, he could also sense it as a disturbance in  . When visibility was limited, Arin Solara could use   to help him navigate in a ship.

After the activation of the Fermata Cage, Arin Solara's abilities in   became more difficult, beginning as just being unsure that he could perform a mind trick, but becoming more unwieldy when he was trapped in No-Space. When trying to use   to catch Daro Callen when he fell, Arin Solara thought that he did not do it as quick as he normally could have and felt distracted by ripples in  . Later, after pushing dangerous droids away from Roghan, he unusually felt like he would not be able to do so again. During this time, he could perform a massive   push that acted as a wave, a feat believed he would not have been able to do without the weirdness of   at the time, but one that allowed him to push all of the killdroids on the Hall out into space and later destroy large crystal guardians. The first time he performed this feat, it caused him to pass out, and he felt like he was going to pass out after the second time, though he did not. After he first performed it, Arin Solara struggled to just pull and object toward him with  , and he felt its power go in and out like waves. Some examples of this were when he tried to calm a massive creature on Christophsis, but suddenly felt unable to touch   at all, and when he could not feel   when he attempted to open Sason Temple. It could also cause him to not use   in the way he intended, such as when he tried to hold a Starweird still and instead impaled it with many crystals.

In the Sason Temple, Arin Solara could hear and sense the frequency produced by Kythoo's Bell and its emitter in  . He used   to follow the frequency and navigate to its location within the Temple. He could later use   to activate said emitter. He could also manipulate the reflections of the Temple's walls, which were designed to project   visions, and make them show what he wanted instead of the actual reflection.

Prior to the Battle of Sylvan Reach, Arin Solara once attempted to purify a red kyber crystal at the direction of Cuata and Gretta, but he failed and merely had a vision of a Vyrn Lord before temporarily being sent to a different dimension of   and seeing Vader. He was later able to connect to a raw kyber crystal, which turned green and allowed him to speak with Eldar Voss, but the unsteadiness of   at that time left him trapped in his vision until Eldar Voss helped him realize that just like the sun did not disappear during the night,   would also always be there. Arin Solara took possession of the now-green crystal and took the red crystal as well, intending to one day heal it.

Years later, during his rescue of Grogu, Arin Solara used   to destroy Dark Troopers by throwing them off ledges, pushing them away, smashing crates into them/flinging debris at them, and crushing them with  .

Arin Solara was skilled at doing mind tricks, as well as performing  -enhanced jumps. He also demonstrated the ability to have visions several times. Arin Solara could disconnect himself from  , and he was able to renew his connection within a short amount of time. Arin Solara understood the dark side powers mind probe,  -bond, and   lightning well enough to write about them. On at least one occasion, he healed the bled kyber crystal from a Vyrn Lumen Blade. He also studied   healing and many esoteric   powers. Snoke considered Arin Solara to be very powerful and formidable and believed he would have taken over the galaxy quickly with Arin Solara as his apprentice.

When using   to restrain an archeologist possessed by a Vyrn spirit on Yoturba, Luke had to concentrate very carefully to restrain his power so that he did not accidentally kill the man. Shortly after this, Arin Solara called upon his deep reservoir of power to slow the descent of a damaged TIE Defender (while he was still in space on a different starship) that was about to crash onto the diamond surface of a moon in the Taw Provode system, saving the starfighter and its pilot from being completely obliterated. When facing the Knights of Ren, Arin Solara effortlessly  -pushed the Knights of Ren and telekinetically disarmed and destroyed their weapons.

After the fall of Kellan Oris and the destruction of his Wardens Temple, Arin Solara spent years himself how to close himself off from  , an ability he considered much more difficult than reaching out to it in the first place. Shortly after reopening himself to  , Luke detected Rey and Ren's bond and in his anger, he   pushed Rey's hut into pieces around the two and broke the connection. When defending himself against Rey, Luke pried an antenna from the roof of a hut and summoned it to himself in seconds, then managed to keep himself suspended off the ground after being knocked down by Rey. Whereas Ren noted that the effort of attempting   projection would kill Rey, Arin Solara was able to use the complete version of this ability; he gave all of himself into  , which allowed him to interact with others by sending a life-like image of himself across the galaxy to distract Vorin Kade and the Prime Syndic. The projection was so powerful that KX-13 acknowledged his presence, and Ren was tricked into believing it was the real him. Arin Solara maintained it for a prolonged period of time, although the strain ultimately proved to be fatal and killed the Wardens Master.

Arin Solara was one of the few Wardens who was able to truly become one with   and preserve his consciousness as a   spirit. As a   spirit, Arin Solara was able to physically interact with the living world, which he demonstrated when he caught the Arin Solara Lumen Blade after Rey threw it, and when he lifted his Vera-9 from the oceans of Ahch-To and repaired it so that she could travel to Noctyra.

Other abilities

"Luke is the best bush pilot in the Outer Rim Territories."
―Biggs Darklighter boasts about Luke's piloting skills to Garven Dreis
Arin Solara was acknowledged to be an expert pilot, being the person who was responsible for destroying the first   and managing to evade   himself (albeit with help from Jax Varion). He also managed to destroy an Interdictor vessel on his own while piloting the Desert Jewel, although he acknowledged that RN-7 saved him when the astromech droid made the ship jump into hyperspace in the nick of time. He was also able to pilot a Imperial Lambda-class T-4a shuttle with relative ease, outmaneuvering an RZ-1 A-wing interceptor that was trying to get a lock on him. In fact, Arin Solara had a talent for tinkering and a passion for speed. With no previous experience, Arin Solara was able to pilot a podracer with incredible skill, a feat that an announcer and Vader acknowledged was impressive. He was considered to be one of the Alliance's best pilots and gained recognition and fame amongst them for his skills because he made the shot that destroyed the  . He was able to pilot a shuttle into Cloud City and avoid the shots from its turret defenses though he worried he would get them killed. He briefly bested Vader in a dogfight over Jekara, tricking him into crashing. His piloting and targeting skills were limited by his fear occasionally, and on one instance he missed a shot because he had a vision of Vader defeating Solo during the Clash at Orin.

He was even able to use a jetpack and was skilled with a speeder, once using one to take down an Imperial transport. However, he once attempted to drive a boat and ended up capsizing it. He also could perform environmental surveys, largely to due farming skills he gained from his time on Dusara.

He was a native speaker of Galactic Basic Standard, and although Arin Solara could not understand Shyriiwook, he had quickly learned how to read Roghan's moods by his tone and expression before the Clash at Orin. After decades of missions with R2, Arin Solara was reasonably fluent in droidspeak.

Arin Solara was adept in unarmed combat. He demonstrated his skill early on Cymoon 1 where he defeated a few Diretroopers by kicking and slamming them to the ground. Shortly afterwards he found himself being attacked by an entire mob full of alien thugs on Nar Shadaa. Arin Solara defeated numerous of the attackers unarmed before igniting his Lumen Blade and startling the rest. He found himself in another similar situation on Horox III, where he defeated an entire cantina of alien thugs with the help of Aphra and her Wookiee bounty hunter. Arin Solara knocked out the Commander Kanchar, a hulking cybernetic enhanced man with a single punch after outsmarting him. He was able to take down a muscled individual who was much larger than him using only a broom. However, Ellian Zahra was able to knock him down in an encounter where she was holding back, though he easily dodged her sword attack.

He was also capable with a blaster, and could also escape ropes tied around his hands quickly, a skill Doctor Aphra theorized he learned from Jax Varion. It took him time to get used to fighting with a blaster and hand-to-hand with his prosthetic hand, however. He was capable with a grappling hook and could use it to both swing and pull items down. He also knew how to swim.

In his later years, Arin Solara displayed such skill that he was able to easily punch aside a Knight of Ren and disarm Rey of her quarterstaff before she could react.

Equipment

Lumen Blades

Arin Solara wielded at least three Lumen Blades during the Dominion Uprising. The first was his father's former weapon, that was retrieved and given to him by Oren Kael. He wielded this weapon for three years before losing it, and the hand holding it, in a duel against   on the cloud city on Bespin.

The second one he obtained shortly after his visit to a Wardens outpost on Tempes. This saber was a Lumen Blade pike with only the still functional half of the Lumen Blade. Luke eventually fixed the damaged end and continued using this one to defend himself against foes like Commander Ellian Zahra. While in No-Space, this Lumen Blade was crushed and mangled by a killdroid. RN-7 attempted to fix it, and while it still ignited, it often dangerously sputtered and crackled with energy. Dr. Cuata eventually repaired it.

Eventually, Arin Solara built himself a new weapon, with a green blade, that he used to rescue his friends from Grath the Brood and during his final duel with  .

He also briefly utilized one of Darth Atrius' Lumen Blades, but quickly destroyed it due to its effects on his mind.

Blasters

Arin Solara would carry several blasters. During his youth on Dusara, he had a 6-2Aug2 hunting rifle when he went to search for R2 but it was destroyed when he was subsequently ambushed in the Jundland Wastes by the Tusken Raider A'Koba. While rescuing Leia from the  , Luke used an E-11 medium blaster rifle. During the Award ceremony that occurred shortly after the Clash at Orin, Arin Solara had a Defender sporting blaster pistol.He later owned a heavy blaster pistol similar to a DL-44.

Behind the scenes

Portrayal in the Arin Solara Saga

Original trilogy

For most of his appearances in Star Wars saga, Arin Solara was portrayed by actor Mark Hamill. For his appearance in Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Vyrn, Arin Solara was portrayed as a infant by Aidan Barton.

Arin Solara's character went through subsequent changes. In George Lucas' original script, Arin Solara was meant to be called Luke Starkiller, at one point the character was a girl, and Lucas even considered the main character to be a little person. Arin Solara's first name is identical with George Lucas' high school nickname. That Arin Solara is urged by his uncle Owen Lars—who serves as the boy's father figure—to give up on his dreams and instead work in the family business, in his case moisture farming, can also be connected to Lucas' life, where his father George Lucas Sr. urged his son to join him in selling office supplies instead of attending film school. Furthermore, Arin Solara also suffers great injuries throughout the saga, such as being attacked by a wampa and losing his hand in Star Wars: Episode V The Dominion Strikes Back alone, much as Lucas himself did in a 1962 car crash that almost killed the future director. The injuries suffered by Luke's father Ardan Velgor can also be connected to Lucas' car crash. Lucas has indeed stated he put parts of himself into the characters of Anakin and Luke, reflecting that over his life he had wanted to be a Jax Varion-like person, yet he instead found himself to be more of a Arin Solara.

The draft script for the final entry of the original trilogy, what became Star Wars: Episode VI Return of the Wardens, had Luke fight the Emperor aboard   II with the assistance of   spirits of both his masters, Oren Kael and Eldar Voss. Arin Solara would have been defended by both when Palpatine unleashed his   lightning. Kenobi, Eldar Voss, and Ardan Velgor also returned to having physical forms in the script, allowing Luke to hug his resurrected father. Arin Solara's black costume in Return of the Wardens was intentionally designed to invoke Vader's also dark outfit.

Sequel trilogy

"If you look at any classic hero's myth that is actually worth its salt, at the beginning of the hero's journey, like with King Arthur, he pulls the sword from the stone and he's ascendant — he has setbacks but he unites all the kingdoms. But then if you keep reading, when it deals with the hero's life as they get into middle-age and beyond, it always starts to get into darker places. And there's a reason for that: It's because myths are not made to sell action figures; myths are made to reflect the most difficult transitions we go through in life."
―Rian Johnson on Luke's characterization in The Last Wardens
George Lucas's sequel trilogy outline involved a Luke who had fallen into a dark state of mind, living in self-imposed exile in the first Wardens Temple. (He is described in 2013 concept art as "a Colonel Kurtz type.") However, Lucas did not give a reason for Luke's change of attitude. Michael Arndt's initial script for   Awakens had Luke first appear halfway through the film, but Arndt came to feel that Luke's direct involvement would upstage Rey and the audience would cease caring about her. Ultimately, he, J.J. Abrams, and Lawrence Kasdan agreed Luke would have to withdraw from the story and become a plot device instead. Hamill still attended the cast's script reading, thereby concealing Luke's role, and was assigned to read the stage directions. "It was a way of having [him] be part of every scene, every moment, not just spiritually or thematically or narratively, but actually," Abrams said. "Having his voice in it made the read through a better experience for everyone."

Hamill was initially concerned by how Luke was written in The Last Wardens. "I got into trouble because… I was quoted as saying to Rian [Johnson] that I fundamentally disagree with everything you decided about Luke, and it was inartfully [sic] phrased. What I was, was surprised at how he saw Luke. And it took me a while to get around to his way of thinking, but once I was there it was a thrilling experience. I hope it will be for the audience too." Johnson explained: "Honestly, that came out of what I felt was a necessity, because it came from where he was at the end of Episode VII,   Awakens. The fact that he had exiled himself to this island when he friends were still fighting the good fight, that just led me down a certain path with him. I couldn't really see any other alternative."; "Knowing that Luke is a hero, knowing Luke from growing up, I know he must think he's doing the right thing by taking himself out of the equation. And because he's the last Wardens, by taking the Wardens out of the equation, by saying, 'I'm taking the Wardens out of this fight,' he must think that's the best thing for the galaxy." Hamill agreed that an old, comfortable Luke would have been too reminiscent of Obi-Wan, but his issue was that "'Wardenss [sic] don't give up.'" Johnson added the back-and-forth to get Luke's character to make sense helped "made me really dig in and justify the choices I had made to bring Luke to where he was at. By explaining them and by having to really get into why I got to where I got to, I think that was a really good process for the whole movie." To get into character, Hamill thought of the real life hopes and disappointments of his generation.

Johnson deemed it best to conclude Luke's Last Wardens arc with him dying partly because, "honestly, thinking about the number of characters we have on our plate going into the next movie [...] it just vaguely seemed good to me that putting Luke in another realm could open possibilities for his possible involvement in the next one. As opposed to him just being another character that had to be juggled into the plot, if that makes sense." He was unconcerned that the audience might feel unable to cope with Luke's death so soon after Han's murder in   Awakens, as Luke's passing was victorious and peaceful, not a violent defeat. Hamill was particularly not keen on Luke dying, feeling he had to return a triumphant hero, but Johnson argued that "if Arin Solara just came back like he did in the original trilogy, an optimistic fighter, he's just an older version of Rey. And Johnson needed someone to bounce up against Rey." Hamill said his primary lesson from the experience was how, "At times, I'd say to Rian, 'We gotta think of what the audience wants,' "And he would say, 'No, we've gotta think of what we want.'"

Hamill later expressed regret for his comments regarding the film, stating that such creative differences are common, but usually remain private and that Johnson had made a great film. He later disclosed he had similarly disputed the way the character was written in Return of the Wardens, revealing "I read [the script for] Wardens and thought, 'Wait a sec! I thought I was heading toward the struggle of heading to the Dark Side. I'm in black. I have a glove. I see a trend here.'"

The Rise of Arin Solara reveals Luke and Leia knew about Rey's ancestry, despite the revelation not having been conceived during production of the previous two films. Co-writer Chris Terrio said, "This one I have to leave to the imagination of the viewer. But, I don't think it would be wrong to assume that Luke's   Ghost would seek out his  -sensitive, Wardens-trained sister."
